### 4.2 前端加载速度提升

#### 4.2.1 资源压缩与优化

##### Vite构建优化配置

```javascript
// vite.config.js - Tailor IS前端构建优化配置
import { defineConfig } from 'vite'
import vue from '@vitejs/plugin-vue'
import legacy from '@vitejs/plugin-legacy'  // 浏览器兼容性
import compression from 'vite-plugin-compression'  // Gzip压缩
import imagemin from 'vite-plugin-imagemin'  // 图片压缩
import { visualizer } from 'rollup-plugin-visualizer'  // 包体积分析

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [
    vue(),
    
    // 浏览器兼容性处理(支持旧浏览器)
    legacy({
      targets: ['Chrome >= 64', 'Firefox >= 67', 'Safari >= 12'],
      additionalLegacyPolyfills: ['regenerator-runtime/runtime']
    }),
    
    // Gzip/Brotli压缩静态资源
    compression({
      algorithm: 'gzip',
      ext: '.gz',
      threshold: 10240,  // 大于10KB才压缩
      deleteOriginFile: false
    }),
    
    // 图片自动压缩(PNG/JPEG/WebP)
    imagemin({
      gifsicle: { optimizationLevel: 7 },
      optipng: { optimizationLevel: 7 },
      mozjpeg: { quality: 80 },
      svgo: { plugins: [{ removeViewBox: false }] },
      webp: { quality: 80 }
    }),
    
    // 包体积可视化分析
    visualizer({
      filename: 'dist/stats.html',
      open: false,
      gzipSize: true
    })
  ],

  build: {
    // 生产环境构建优化
    minify: 'terser',  // 使用terser压缩JS(比esbuild更彻底)
    terserOptions: {
      compress: {
        drop_console: true,  // 移除console.log
        drop_debugger: true, // 移除debugger
        pure_funcs: ['console.log', 'console.info']  // 移除指定函数调用
      },
      format: {
        comments: false  // 移除注释
      }
    },
    
    // CSS代码拆分与压缩
    cssCodeSplit: true,
    cssMinify: true,
    
    // chunk分包策略(关键优化!)
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        // 手动分包配置
        manualChunks: {
          // Vue核心框架(稳定不变,长期缓存)
          'vue-vendor': ['vue', 'vue-router', 'pinia'],
          
          // UI组件库(Element Plus)
          'element-plus-vendor': ['element-plus', '@element-plus/icons-vue'],
          
          // 工具库(lodash/moment等)
          'utils-vendor': ['axios', 'dayjs', 'lodash-es'],
          
          // 业务公共模块
          'common': [
            './src/components/common/',
            './src/utils/',
            './src/api/'
          ]
        },
        
        // 文件名哈希(内容变化才更新缓存)
        chunkFileNames: 'static/js/[name]-[hash].js',
        entryFileNames: 'static/js/[name]-[hash].js',
        assetFileNames: 'static/[ext]/[name]-[hash].[ext]'
      }
    },
    
    // 构建性能
    chunkSizeWarningLimit: 1000  // chunk大小警告阈值(KB)
  },

  // 开发服务器配置
  server: {
    port: 3000,
    open: true,
    cors: true,
    
    // 代理API请求(解决开发环境跨域)
    proxy: {
      '/api': {
        target: 'http://localhost:8080',
        changeOrigin: true,
        rewrite: (path) => path.replace(/^\/api/, '')
      }
    }
  }
})
```

##### 图片资源优化策略

```vue
<!-- ImageOptimizer.vue - 智能图片优化组件 -->
<template>
  <picture>
    <!-- WebP格式优先(现代浏览器) -->
    <source 
      v-if="supportsWebP"
      :srcset="webpSrcSet"
      :sizes="responsiveSizes"
      type="image/webp"
    />
    
    <!-- 降级到原始格式 -->
    <img
      ref="imgRef"
      :src="optimizedSrc"
      :alt="alt"
      :loading="lazyLoading ? 'lazy' : 'eager'"
      :width="width"
      :height="height"
      :class="['optimized-image', { 'image-loaded': isLoaded }]"
      @load="onImageLoad"
      @error="onImageError"
    />
  </picture>
</template>

<script setup>
import { ref, onMounted, computed } from 'vue'

const props = defineProps({
  src: { type: String, required: true },
  alt: { type: String, default: '' },
  width: { type: [Number, String], default: 'auto' },
  height: { type: [Number, String], default: 'auto' },
  quality: { type: Number, default: 80 },  // 压缩质量
  lazyLoading: { type: Boolean, default: true },  // 默认懒加载
  breakpoints: {  // 响应式断点
    type: Array,
    default: () => [320, 640, 960, 1280, 1920]
  }
})

const supportsWebP = ref(false)
const isLoaded = ref(false)

onMounted(() => {
  // 检测浏览器WebP支持
  const canvas = document.createElement('canvas')
  supportsWebP.value = canvas.toDataURL('image/webp').indexOf('data:image/webp') === 0
})

const optimizedSrc = computed(() => {
  // 通过CDN URL参数动态调整尺寸和质量
  const baseUrl = props.src.replace(/^https?:\/\/[^\/]+/, CDN_BASE_URL)
  return `${baseUrl}?w=${props.width}&q=${props.quality}&format=auto`
})

const webpSrcSet = computed(() => {
  // 生成响应式srcset
  return props.breakpoints
    .map(bp => `${props.src}?w=${bp}&q=${props.quality}&format=webp ${bp}w`)
    .join(', ')
})

const responsiveSizes = computed(() => {
  // 响应式sizes属性
  return '(max-width: 600px) 100vw, (max-width: 1200px) 50vw, 33vw'
})

function onImageLoad() {
  isLoaded.value = true
}

function onImageError() {
  console.error('图片加载失败:', props.src)
  // 可选: 显示占位图或重试
}
</script>

<style scoped>
.optimized-image {
  opacity: 0;
  transition: opacity 0.3s ease-in-out;
  background-color: #f5f5f5;  /* 加载前背景色 */
}

.image-loaded {
  opacity: 1;
}
</style>
```

#### 4.2.2 懒加载实现方案

##### 路由懒加载配置

```javascript
// router/index.js - Tailor IS路由懒加载配置
import { createRouter, createWebHistory } from 'vue-router'

/**
 * 路由懒加载策略说明:
 * 
 * 1. 首屏必需路由(立即加载):
 *    - Home(首页)、Login(登录)、ProductList(商品列表)
 * 
 * 2. 二级路由(按需加载):
 *    - UserCenter(个人中心)、Cart(购物车)、Order(订单)
 * 
 * 3. 三级路由(访问时加载):
 *    - MerchantCenter(商家中心)、AdminPanel(管理后台)
 */

const routes = [
  {
    path: '/',
    name: 'Home',
    component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "home" */ '@/views/home/HomeIndex.vue'),
    meta: { title: 'Tailor IS - 首页', keepAlive: true }
  },
  
  // ==================== 用户端路由(按需加载) ====================
  {
    path: '/product',
    component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "product" */ '@/views/product/ProductLayout.vue'),
    children: [
      {
        path: 'list',
        name: 'ProductList',
        component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "product-list" */ '@/views/product/ProductList.vue'),
        meta: { title: '商品列表' }
      },
      {
        path: ':id/detail',
        name: 'ProductDetail',
        component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "product-detail" */ '@/views/product/ProductDetail.vue'),
        meta: { title: '商品详情' }
      }
    ]
  },
  
  {
    path: '/cart',
    name: 'Cart',
    component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "cart" */ '@/views/order/Cart.vue'),
    meta: { title: '购物车' }
  },
  
  {
    path: '/order',
    component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "order" */ '@/views/order/OrderLayout.vue'),
    children: [
      {
        path: 'confirm',
        name: 'OrderConfirm',
        component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "order-confirm" */ '@/views/order/OrderConfirm.vue'),
        meta: { title: '确认订单' }
      },
      {
        path: 'list',
        name: 'OrderList',
        component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "order-list" */ '@/views/order/OrderList.vue'),
        meta: { title: '我的订单' }
      },
      {
        path: ':id/detail',
        name: 'OrderDetail',
        component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "order-detail" */ '@/views/order/OrderDetail.vue'),
        meta: { title: '订单详情' }
      }
    ]
  },
  
  // ==================== 商家端路由(访问时加载) ====================
  {
    path: '/merchant',
    component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "merchant" */ '@/views/merchant/MerchantLayout.vue'),
    meta: { requiresAuth: true, role: 'MERCHANT' },
    children: [
      {
        path: 'dashboard',
        name: 'MerchantDashboard',
        component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "merchant-dashboard" */ '@/views/merchant/Dashboard.vue'),
        meta: { title: '商家工作台' }
      },
      {
        path: 'product/manage',
        name: 'ProductManage',
        component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "product-manage" */ '@/views/merchant/product/ProductManage.vue'),
        meta: { title: '商品管理' }
      },
      {
        path: 'order/manage',
        name: 'OrderManage',
        component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "order-manage" */ '@/views/merchant/order/OrderManage.vue'),
        meta: { title: '订单管理' }
      }
    ]
  },
  
  // ==================== 管理后台路由(权限控制) ====================
  {
    path: '/admin',
    component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "admin" */ '@/views/admin/AdminLayout.vue'),
    meta: { requiresAuth: true, role: 'ADMIN' },
    children: [
      {
        path: 'dashboard',
        name: 'AdminDashboard',
        component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "admin-dashboard" */ '@/views/admin/Dashboard.vue'),
        meta: { title: '管理面板' }
      },
      {
        path: 'users',
        name: 'UserManage',
        component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "user-manage" */ '@/views/admin/user/UserManage.vue'),
        meta: { title: '用户管理' }
      },
      {
        path: 'merchants',
        name: 'MerchantManage',
        component: () => import(/* webpackChunkName: "merchant-manage" */ '@/views/admin/merchant/MerchantManage.vue'),
        meta: { title: '商家管理' }
      }
    ]
  }
]

const router = createRouter({
  history: createWebHistory(),
  routes,
  
  scrollBehavior(to, from, savedPosition) {
    // 路由切换时滚动行为
    if (savedPosition) {
      return savedPosition
    } else {
      return { top: 0 }
    }
  }
})

export default router
```

##### 组件级懒加载指令

```javascript
// directives/lazyLoad.js - Vue3自定义懒加载指令
import { useIntersectionObserver } from '@vueuse/core'

/**
 * v-lazy 懒加载指令用法:
 * <img v-lazy="imageUrl" />
 * <div v-lazy:background="bgImageUrl"></div>
 */

export const lazyLoadDirective = {
  mounted(el, binding) {
    const imageUrl = binding.value
    const modifier = binding.arg || 'src'  // src 或 background
    
    // 设置初始占位图
    const placeholder = 'data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB3aWR0aD0iMjAwIiBoZWlnaHQ9IjIwMCIgeG1sbnM9Imh0dHA6Ly93d3cudzMub3JnLzIwMDAvc3ZnIj48cmVjdCB3aWR0aD0iMTAwJSIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxMDAlIiBmaWxsPSIjZjVmNWY1Ii8+PC9zdmc+'
    
    if (modifier === 'background') {
      el.style.backgroundImage = `url(${placeholder})`
      el.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'
      el.style.backgroundPosition = 'center'
    } else {
      el.src = placeholder
    }
    
    // 使用IntersectionObserver监听可视区域
    const { stop } = useIntersectionObserver(
      el,
      ([{ isIntersecting }]) => {
        if (isIntersecting) {
          // 进入视口,开始加载真实图片
          const img = new Image()
          img.onload = () => {
            if (modifier === 'background') {
              el.style.backgroundImage = `url(${imageUrl})`
              el.classList.add('lazy-loaded')
            } else {
              el.src = imageUrl
              el.classList.add('lazy-loaded')
            }
          }
          img.onerror = () => {
            console.warn('Lazy load failed:', imageUrl)
          }
          img.src = imageUrl
          
          stop()  // 停止观察(只触发一次)
        }
      },
      {
        rootMargin: '200px'  // 提前200px开始加载
      }
    )
  }
}

// main.js 注册全局指令
app.directive('lazy', lazyLoadDirective)
```

#### 4.2.3 CDN加速部署策略

##### Nginx CDN配置

```nginx
# /etc/nginx/conf.d/tailor-is-cdn.conf
# Tailor IS CDN加速配置

# ==================== 静态资源CDN ====================
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name cdn.tailoris.com;

    # Gzip压缩配置
    gzip on;
    gzip_vary on;
    gzip_proxied any;
    gzip_comp_level 6;
    gzip_types
        text/plain
        text/css
        text/xml
        text/javascript
        application/json
        application/javascript
        application/x-javascript
        application/xml
        application/xml+rss
        image/svg+xml;

    # 静态资源根目录
    root /usr/share/nginx/html/dist;

    # ==================== 缓存策略配置 ====================
    
    # HTML文件 - 不缓存(始终获取最新)
    location ~* \.html$ {
        add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        add_header Pragma "no-cache";
        expires -1;
    }

    # JS/CSS带哈希值 - 长期缓存(1年)
    location ~* \.(js|css)$ {
        # 文件名包含哈希,内容变化URL也变,安全长期缓存
        add_header Cache-Control "public, max-age=31536000, immutable";
        expires 365d;
        
        # 启用Gzip
        gzip_static on;
    }

    # 图片资源 - 中期缓存(30天)
    location ~* \.(jpg|jpeg|png|gif|webp|svg|ico)$ {
        add_header Cache-Control "public, max-age=2592000";
        expires 30d;
        
        # 防盗链(仅允许本站引用)
        valid_referers none blocked *.tailoris.com tailoris.com;
        if ($invalid_referer) {
            return 403;
        }
    }

    # 字体文件 - 长期缓存(1年)
    location ~* \.(woff|woff2|ttf|eot|otf)$ {
        add_header Cache-Control "public, max-age=31536000";
        expires 365d;
        
        # CORS允许跨域访问字体
        add_header Access-Control-Allow-Origin *;
    }

    # API接口 - 不缓存
    location /api/ {
        proxy_pass http://backend_servers;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_cache_bypass 1;  # 禁用缓存
    }

    # 错误页面定制
    error_page 404 /404.html;
    error_page 500 502 503 504 /50x.html;
}
```

##### CDN域名规划

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                   Tailor IS CDN架构                              │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  用户请求                                                       │
│     ↓                                                          │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │             CDN边缘节点(全球分布)                         │   │
│  │  北京 ←→ 上海 ←→ 广州 ←→ 成都                          │   │
│  │    ↓        ↓        ↓        ↓                         │   │
│  │  东京   新加坡   法兰克福  纽约                          │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│                                                                 │
│  域名分配策略:                                                   │
│  ┌────────────────┬──────────────────┬──────────────────────┐  │
│  │ 域名           │ 用途             │ 缓存策略             │  │
│  ├────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────────────┤  │
│  │ cdn.tailoris.  │ 静态资源(JS/CSS) │ 1年(哈希文件名)      │  │
│  │ com            │                  │                      │  │
│  ├────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────────────┤  │
│  │ img.tailoris.  │ 图片资源         │ 30天                 │  │
│  │ com            │                  │                      │  │
│  ├────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────────────┤  │
│  │ api.tailoris.  │ API接口          │ 不缓存               │  │
│  │ com            │                  │                      │  │
│  └────────────────┴──────────────────┴──────────────────────┘  │
│                                                                 │
│  回源策略:                                                       │
│  - 静态资源 → OSS对象存储                                        │
│  - 动态API → Nginx负载均衡 → 后端服务集群                       │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### 4.2.4 Web Vitals核心指标优化

##### 核心指标定义与目标值

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│              Core Web Vitals 优化目标(Tailor IS)                │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │  🔵 FCP (First Contentful Paint)                       │   │
│  │  首次内容绘制                                            │   │
│  │  定义: 页面首次绘制文本/图像的时间                        │   │
│  │  目标: ≤ 1.8 秒 (优秀: < 1.0s)                          │   │
│  │  优化: 减少阻塞资源/启用CDN/代码分割                      │   │
│  ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤   │
│  │  🟢 LCP (Largest Contentful Paint)                      │   │
│  │  最大内容绘制                                            │   │
│  │  定义: 视口内最大图像/文本渲染时间                       │   │
│  │  目标: ≤ 2.5 秒 (优秀: < 2.5s)                          │   │
│  │  优化: 优化首屏图片/WebP格式/预加载关键资源              │   │
│  ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤   │
│  │  🟡 CLS (Cumulative Layout Shift)                       │   │
│  │  累积布局偏移                                            │   │
│  │  定义: 页面生命周期内意外布局移动的总和                   │   │
│  │  目标: ≤ 0.1 (优秀: < 0.1)                              │   │
│  │  优化: 尺寸预留/字体显示策略/动态注入控制               │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│                                                                 │
│  辅助指标:                                                      │
│  • TTFB (Time to First Byte): ≤ 800ms                          │
│  • FID (First Input Delay): ≤ 100ms                             │
│  • TBT (Total Blocking Time): ≤ 200ms                           │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

##### Web Vitals监控SDK

```typescript
// utils/webVitals.ts - Core Web Vitals采集与上报
import { onFCP, onLCP, onCLS, onFID, onTTFB, Metric } from 'web-vitals'

interface VitalsReport {
  url: string
  timestamp: number
  metrics: {
    fcp?: Metric
    lcp?: Metric
    cls?: Metric
    fid?: Metric
    ttfb?: Metric
  }
  userAgent: string
  connectionType: string  // 4g/3g/wifi
}

/**
 * 初始化Web Vitals监控
 */
export function initWebVitalsMonitoring() {
  const report: Partial<VitalsReport> = {
    url: window.location.href,
    timestamp: Date.now(),
    userAgent: navigator.userAgent,
    connectionType: (navigator as any)?.connection?.effectiveType || 'unknown'
  }

  // 采集各项指标
  onFCP((metric) => { report.metrics!.fcp = metric })
  onLCP((metric) => { report.metrics!.lcp = metric })
  onCLS((metric) => { report.metrics!.cls = metric })
  onFID((metric) => { report.metrics!.fid = metric })
  onTTFB((metric) => { report.metrics!.ttfb = metric })

  // 页面隐藏时上报(不影响用户体验)
  document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', () => {
    if (document.visibilityState === 'hidden') {
      sendReport(report as VitalsReport)
    }
  })

  // 备用: 30秒后强制上报
  setTimeout(() => {
    sendReport(report as VitalsReport)
  }, 30000)
}

async function sendReport(report: VitalsReport) {
  try {
    await fetch('/api/v1/monitor/web-vitals', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify(report),
      keepalive: true  // 页面关闭也能发送
    })
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Web Vitals上报失败:', error)
  }
}

// CLS优化辅助函数
export function reserveSpace(element: HTMLElement, minHeight: number) {
  element.style.minHeight = `${minHeight}px`  // 预留空间防布局偏移
}

// LCP优化: 预加载关键资源
export function preloadCriticalResources() {
  // 预加载首屏大图
  const heroImage = document.querySelector('[data-hero-image]')
  if (heroImage) {
    const link = document.createElement('link')
    link.rel = 'preload'
    link.as = 'image'
    link.href = (heroImage as HTMLImageElement).dataset.heroImage!
    document.head.appendChild(link)
  }
}
```

---

### 4.3 服务器响应时间改进

#### 4.3.1 接口性能优化策略

##### 接口优化Checklist

```yaml
# api-performance-checklist.yml
api_optimization_checklist:

  # 1. 减少数据库操作
  reduce_db_operations:
    items:
      - name: "批量查询替代循环查询"
        priority: "P0"
        check: "是否存在N+1查询问题?"
        solution: "使用MyBatis的<collection>一次性关联查询"
        example: |
          # ❌ N+1问题
          for product in products:
              skus = db.query("SELECT * FROM sku WHERE product_id=?", product.id)
              
          # ✅ 批量查询
          product_ids = [p.id for p in products]
          all_skus = db.query("SELECT * FROM sku WHERE product_id IN (?)", product_ids)
      
      - name: "减少不必要字段查询"
        priority: "P1"
        check: "是否使用了SELECT *?"
        solution: "明确列出所需字段,使用ResultMap映射"
      
      - name: "合理使用缓存"
        priority: "P0"
        check: "热点数据是否已加入缓存?"
        solution: "配置Redis缓存+本地Caffeine缓存"

  # 2. 异步处理非核心流程
  async_processing:
    items:
      - name: "发送消息通知(短信/邮件/站内信)"
        priority: "P1"
        pattern: "@Async + ThreadPoolTaskExecutor"
        code: |
          @Async("notificationExecutor")
          public void sendOrderNotification(OrderDTO order) {
              smsService.send(order.getUserPhone(), "下单成功通知");
              emailService.send(order.getUserEmail(), "订单确认邮件");
              pushService.send(order.getUserId(), "新订单提醒");
          }
      
      - name: "操作日志记录"
        priority: "P2"
        pattern: "异步写入日志表/ELK"
      
      - name: "统计数据计算"
        priority: "P1"
        pattern: "定时任务聚合 + Redis计数器"

  # 3. 批量接口设计
  batch_api_design:
    items:
      - name: "商品批量上下架"
        endpoint: "POST /api/v1/products/batch-status"
        payload: |
          {
            "productIds": [1001, 1002, 1003],
            "status": 1,
            "reason": "换季促销"
          }
      
      - name: "订单批量发货"
        endpoint: "POST /api/v1/orders/batch-ship"
      
      - name: "SKU批量导入"
        endpoint: "POST /api/v1/skus/batch-import"
        max_batch_size: 500  // 单批次上限
```

##### 异步线程池配置

```java
// AsyncConfig.java - 异步任务线程池配置
@Configuration
@EnableAsync
public class AsyncConfig {

    /**
     * 通知类任务线程池(短信/邮件/推送)
     * 特点: IO密集型,可适当增加线程数
     */
    @Bean("notificationExecutor")
    public Executor notificationExecutor() {
        ThreadPoolTaskExecutor executor = new ThreadPoolTaskExecutor();
        executor.setCorePoolSize(5);        // 核心线程数
        executor.setMaxPoolSize(20);         // 最大线程数
        executor.setQueueCapacity(500);      // 任务队列容量
        executor.setKeepAliveSeconds(60);    // 空闲线程存活时间
        executor.setThreadNamePrefix("notify-");  // 线程名前缀
        
        // 拒绝策略: 由调用线程执行(保证不丢失任务)
        executor.setRejectedExecutionHandler(new ThreadPoolExecutor.CallerRunsPolicy());
        
        // 允许核心线程超时关闭
        executor.allowCoreThreadTimeOut(true);
        
        executor.initialize();
        return executor;
    }

    /**
     * 日志记录线程池
     */
    @Bean("logExecutor")
    public Executor logExecutor() {
        ThreadPoolTaskExecutor executor = new ThreadPoolTaskExecutor();
        executor.setCorePoolSize(2);
        executor.setMaxPoolSize(5);
        executor.setQueueCapacity(1000);
        executor.setThreadNamePrefix("log-");
        executor.setRejectedExecutionHandler(new ThreadPoolExecutor.DiscardOldestPolicy());
        executor.initialize();
        return executor;
    }

    /**
     * 统计计算线程池(CPU密集型)
     * 特点: CPU密集型,线程数≈CPU核心数
     */
    @Bean("statisticsExecutor")
    public Executor statisticsExecutor() {
        int cpuCount = Runtime.getRuntime().availableProcessors();
        ThreadPoolTaskExecutor executor = new ThreadPoolTaskExecutor();
        executor.setCorePoolSize(cpuCount);
        executor.setMaxPoolSize(cpuCount * 2);
        executor.setQueueCapacity(100);
        executor.setThreadNamePrefix("stats-");
        executor.initialize();
        return executor;
    }
}
```

#### 4.3.2 多级缓存架构设计

##### 三级缓存架构实现

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│              Tailor IS 多级缓存架构(L1/L2/L3)                   │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  Client(用户端)                                                 │
│     │                                                           │
│     ▼                                                           │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │  L3: CDN/浏览器缓存(离用户最近)                          │   │
│  │  ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐               │   │
│  │  │ 静态资源  │ │ 图片CDN  │ │ API响应  │ TTL: 可配置  │   │
│  │  └──────────┘ └──────────┘ └──────────┘               │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│     │ MISS                                                      │
│     ▼                                                           │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │  L2: Redis分布式缓存(集群共享)                            │   │
│  │  ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐               │   │
│  │  │ 热点数据  │ │ 会话数据  │ │ 分布式锁  │ TTL: 分钟级  │   │
│  │  └──────────┘ └──────────┘ └──────────┘               │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│     │ MISS                                                      │
│     ▼                                                           │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │  L1: 本地缓存(Caffeine/JVM内存)                          │   │
│  │  ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐               │   │
│  │  │ 元数据    │ │ 配置数据  │ │ 权限数据  │ TTL: 秒级   │   │
│  │  └──────────┘ └──────────┘ └──────────┘               │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│     │ MISS                                                      │
│     ▼                                                           │
│  Database(MySQL)                                                │
│                                                                 │
│  数据流转:  DB → L1 → L2 → L3 → Client                         │
│  失效策略:  写入时反向清除(L1→L2→L3)                            │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

```java
// MultiLevelCacheService.java - 多级缓存服务
@Service
@Slf4j
public class MultiLevelCacheService {

    @Autowired
    private CaffeineCacheManager localCache;  // L1: Caffeine本地缓存

    @Autowired
    private RedisTemplate<String, Object> redisTemplate;  // L2: Redis

    /**
     * 多级缓存读取(读路径: L1 → L2 → DB)
     * 
     * @param cacheKey 缓存Key
     * @param clazz 返回类型
     * @param dbLoader DB加载函数(当缓存全部未命中时调用)
     * @return 缓存数据
     */
    public <T> T getFromMultiCache(String cacheKey, Class<T> clazz, Supplier<T> dbLoader) {
        
        // 1️⃣ L1: 查询本地缓存(纳秒级)
        T data = getFromLocalCache(cacheKey, clazz);
        if (data != null) {
            log.debug("L1命中: {}", cacheKey);
            return data;
        }
        
        // 2️⃣ L2: 查询Redis缓存(毫秒级)
        data = getFromRedis(cacheKey, clazz);
        if (data != null) {
            log.debug("L2命中: {}", cacheKey);
            // 回填L1缓存
            setLocalCache(cacheKey, data, Duration.ofMinutes(5));
            return data;
        }
        
        // 3️⃣ DB: 查询数据库(最慢)
        log.debug("缓存未命中,查询DB: {}", cacheKey);
        data = dbLoader.get();
        
        if (data != null) {
            // 4️⃣ 回填L1和L2缓存
            setLocalCache(cacheKey, data, Duration.ofMinutes(5));
            setRedis(cacheKey, data, Duration.ofMinutes(30));
        }
        
        return data;
    }

    /**
     * 多级缓存失效(写路径: L1 → L2 → L3)
     */
    public void evictMultiCache(String cacheKeyPattern) {
        // 清除L1本地缓存
        localCache.getCacheNames().forEach(name -> {
            Cache cache = localCache.getCache(name);
            if (cache != null) {
                cache.evict(cacheKeyPattern);
            }
        });
        
        // 清除L2 Redis缓存(支持模糊匹配)
        Set<String> keys = redisTemplate.keys(cacheKeyPattern + "*");
        if (!CollectionUtils.isEmpty(keys)) {
            redisTemplate.delete(keys);
        }
        
        log.info("多级缓存已清除: {}", cacheKeyPattern);
    }
    
    // ... 其他辅助方法
}
```

#### 4.3.3 负载均衡配置

##### Nginx七层负载均衡配置

```nginx
# /etc/nginx/nginx.conf
# Tailor IS 负载均衡主配置

# ==================== 上游服务定义 ====================
upstream backend_servers {
    # 轮询策略(默认)
    server 192.168.1.101:8080 weight=5;  # weight权重
    server 192.168.1.102:8080 weight=3;
    server 192.168.1.103:8080 weight=2;
    
    # 备用节点(其他节点全部宕机时启用)
    server 192.168.1.104:8080 backup;
    
    # 连接参数
    keepalive 32;  # 保持32个长连接
    
    # 健康检查(需要ngx_http_upstream_health_check_module)
    # interval=3000 rise=2 fall=3 timeout=3000 type=http;
}

upstream frontend_servers {
    # IP Hash会话保持(WebSocket场景)
    ip_hash;
    server 192.168.1.201:3000;
    server 192.168.1.202:3000;
}

# ==================== 主Server配置 ====================
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name www.tailoris.com api.tailoris.com;

    # ==================== 反向代理配置 ====================
    location /api/ {
        proxy_pass http://backend_servers;
        
        # 请求头传递
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
        
        # 连接超时设置
        proxy_connect_timeout 10s;
        proxy_send_timeout 30s;
        proxy_read_timeout 60s;  # 长轮询/流式接口需加大
        
        # Buffer配置
        proxy_buffer_size 16k;
        proxy_buffers 4 32k;
        proxy_busy_buffers_size 64k;
        
        # 支持WebSocket
        proxy_http_version 1.1;
        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
        
        # 跨域配置
        add_header Access-Control-Allow-Origin * always;
        add_header Access-Control-Allow-Methods 'GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, OPTIONS' always;
        if ($request_method = 'OPTIONS') {
            return 204;
        }
    }

    # ==================== 静态资源 ====================
    location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|gif|ico|woff2?)$ {
        proxy_pass http://frontend_servers;
        expires 30d;
        add_header Cache-Control "public, immutable";
    }

    # ==================== 限流配置 ====================
    # 使用令牌桶算法限制请求频率
    limit_req_zone $binary_remote_addr zone=api_limit:10m rate=100r/s;
    limit_req zone=api_limit burst=200 nodelay;  // 突发200请求
    
    # ==================== SSL/TLS(HTTPS) - 符合Spec需求6.2 ====================
    # listen 443 ssl http2;
    # ssl_certificate /etc/nginx/ssl/tailoris.com.crt;
    # ssl_certificate_key /etc/nginx/ssl/tailoris.com.key;
    # ssl_protocols TLSv1.3;  # 强制TLS 1.3(禁用TLS 1.0/1.1/1.2)
    # ssl_ciphers TLS_AES_256_GCM_SHA384:TLS_CHACHA20_POLY1305_SHA256;  # TLS 1.3专用套件
}
```

##### 四层负载均衡(LVS/Keepalived)

```yaml
# keepalived.conf - 高可用负载均衡配置
! Configuration File for keepalived

global_defs {
   notification_email {
     admin@tailoris.com
   }
   smtp_server 127.0.0.1
   router_id LVS_TAILOR_IS
}

# VIP虚拟IP(对外暴露地址)
vrrp_instance VI_1 {
    state MASTER          # MASTER/BACKUP
    interface eth0        # 网卡名称
    virtual_router_id 51  # VRID(同一集群相同)
    priority 100          # 优先级(MASTER更高)
    advert_int 1          # 心跳间隔(秒)
    
    authentication {
        auth_type PASS
        auth_pass tailoris_2026_secret
    }
    
    virtual_ipaddress {
        192.168.1.100/24  # VIP地址
    }
}

# 四层TCP负载均衡(转发到Nginx)
virtual_server 192.168.1.100 80 {
    delay_loop 6
    lb_algo wrr           # 加权轮询
    lb_kind DR            # 直接路由模式(高性能)
    persistence_timeout 50
    protocol TCP
    
    real_server 192.168.1.10 80 {
        weight 1
        TCP_CHECK {
            connect_timeout 3
            nb_get_retry 3
            delay_before_retry 3
        }
    }
    
    real_server 192.168.1.11 80 {
        weight 1
        TCP_CHECK {
            connect_timeout 3
            nb_get_retry 3
            delay_before_retry 3
        }
    }
}
```

##### 自定义链路追踪注解

```java
// TraceLog.java - 自定义追踪注解
@Target(ElementType.METHOD)
@Retention(RetentionPolicy.RUNTIME)
@Documented
public @interface TraceLog {
    /** 操作名称(显示在SkyWalking UI中) */
    String operationName() default "";
    
    /** 是否记录入参 */
    boolean logParams() default true;
    
    /** 是否记录返回值 */
    boolean logResult() default false;
    
    /** 耗时阈值(ms),超过则告警 */
    long warnThreshold() default 3000;
}

// TraceLogAspect.java - 追踪切面实现
@Aspect
@Component
@Slf4j
public class TraceLogAspect {

    @Autowired
    private Tracer tracer;  // SkyWalking Tracer

    @Around("@annotation(traceLog)")
    public Object aroundTraceLog(ProceedingJoinPoint joinPoint, TraceLog traceLog) throws Throwable {
        String operationName = traceLog.operationName().isEmpty() 
            ? joinPoint.getSignature().toShortString()
            : traceLog.operationName();
        
        // 创建Span
        AbstractSpan span = tracer.createSpan(operationName);
        span.setComponent("TailorIS-Business");
        
        try {
            // 记录入参
            if (traceLog.logParams()) {
                Object[] args = joinPoint.getArgs();
                if (args.length > 0) {
                    span.tag("params", JsonUtils.toJson(args));
                }
            }
            
            long startTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
            Object result = joinPoint.proceed();
            long costTime = System.currentTimeMillis() - startTime;
            
            // 记录返回值
            if (traceLog.logResult()) {
                span.tag("result", JsonUtils.toJson(result));
            }
            
            // 记录耗时
            span.tag("cost_ms", String.valueOf(costTime));
            
            // 超过阈值告警
            if (costTime > traceLog.warnThreshold()) {
                log.warn("⚠️ [慢操作告警] 方法: {}, 耗时: {}ms, 阈值: {}ms",
                    operationName, costTime, traceLog.warnThreshold());
                span.errorOccurred();
                span.log(new RuntimeException("Operation timeout warning"));
            }
            
            span.setTag(SpanTags.STATUS_CODE, "SUCCESS");
            return result;
            
        } catch (Throwable e) {
            span.setErrorLogs(e);
            span.setTag(SpanTags.STATUS_CODE, "ERROR");
            throw e;
        } finally {
            span.finish();  // 结束Span
        }
    }
}

// 使用示例
@Service
public class OrderServiceImpl {

    @TraceLog(operationName = "创建订单", warnThreshold = 2000)
    public OrderDTO createOrder(CreateOrderParam param) {
        // 业务逻辑...
        return order;
    }
    
    @TraceLog(operationName = "同步库存", logParams = false, warnThreshold = 5000)
    public void syncInventory(Long productId, Integer quantity) {
        // 库存同步逻辑...
    }
}
```

## 第五章 多平台兼容性

### 5.1 浏览器兼容性保障

#### 5.1.1 主流浏览器测试矩阵

##### 浏览器兼容性支持范围

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│            Tailor IS 浏览器兼容性测试矩阵                         │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  ┌─────────────┬──────────┬──────────┬──────────┬──────────┐   │
│  │   浏览器     │ 最低版本  │ 推荐版本  │ 市场份额  │ 支持级别  │   │
│  ├─────────────┼──────────┼──────────┼──────────┼──────────┤   │
│  │ Chrome      │ 64+      │ 120+     │ ~65%     │ ✅ 完全   │   │
│  │ Firefox     │ 67+      │ 115+     │ ~3%      │ ✅ 完全   │   │
│  │ Safari      │ 12+(Mac) │ 17+      │ ~18%     │ ✅ 完全   │   │
│  │             │ iOS 12+  │ iOS 17+  │ (移动端)  │          │   │
│  │ Edge        │ 79+      │ 120+     │ ~5%      │ ✅ 完全   │   │
│  │ (Chromium)  │          │          │          │          │   │
│  ├─────────────┼──────────┼──────────┼──────────┼──────────┤   │
│  │ IE 11       │ ❌ 不支持│ -        │ <0.5%    │ ⚠️ 降级   │   │
│  │ UC Browser  │ ⚠️ 部分  │ 最新版   │ ~3%      │ 🔄 适配中 │   │
│  │ QQ Browser  │ ⚠️ 部分  │ 最新版   │ ~2%      │ 🔄 适配中 │   │
│  └─────────────┴──────────┴──────────┴──────────┴──────────┘   │
│                                                                 │
│  兼容性策略:                                                     │
│  • Grade A(完全支持): Chrome/Firefox/Safari/Edge 最新2个版本     │
│  • Grade B(基本支持): 国产浏览器(UC/QQ/360) Chromium内核         │
│  • Grade X(不支持): IE 11及以下,提示用户升级浏览器               │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**参考系统 vs Tailor IS 对比**

| 维度 | 参考系统现状 | Tailor IS 目标方案 |
|------|-------------|-------------------|
| **目标浏览器** | IE 10+/Chrome/Firefox/Safari | Chrome 64+/Firefox 67+/Safari 12+/Edge 79+ |
| **兼容性处理** | 大量Polyfill,代码臃肿 | 现代浏览器优先 + 渐进增强 |
| **CSS前缀** | 手动添加-webkit-/-moz-等 | Autoprefixer自动处理 |
| **构建工具** | Webpack 4.x | Vite + Babel/Preset-env智能降级 |

##### 自动化浏览器测试配置

```javascript
// playwright.config.js - Tailor IS E2E浏览器测试配置
import { defineConfig, devices } from '@playwright/test'

export default defineConfig({
  testDir: './e2e',
  
  // 并行执行测试
  fullyParallel: true,
  
  // 失败时只重试1次
  retries: 1,
  
  // 并发工作线程数
  workers: process.env.CI ? 2 : undefined,
  
  // 测试报告输出
  reporter: [
    ['html', { open: 'never', outputFolder: 'playwright-report' }],
    ['json', { outputFile: 'test-results.json' }]
  ],
  
  use: {
    baseURL: 'http://localhost:3000',
    trace: 'on-first-retry',  // 首次失败时录制trace
    screenshot: 'only-on-failure',  // 仅失败时截图
    video: 'retain-on-failure',  // 失败时保留视频
  },

  projects: [
    // ==================== 桌面浏览器 ====================
    {
      name: 'chromium',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Chrome'] },
    },
    
    {
      name: 'firefox',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Firefox'] },
    },
    
    {
      name: 'webkit',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Safari'] },
    },
    
    // ==================== 移动设备模拟 ====================
    {
      name: 'Mobile Chrome',
      use: { ...devices['Pixel 5'] },
    },
    
    {
      name: 'Mobile Safari',
      use: { ...devices['iPhone 12'] },
    },
    
    // ==================== 平板设备模拟 ====================
    {
      name: 'Tablet Safari',
      use: { ...devices['iPad Pro'] },
    }
  ],

  // 启动开发服务器
  webServer: {
    command: 'npm run dev',
    url: 'http://localhost:3000',
    reuseExistingServer: !process.env.CI,
  },
})
```

#### 5.1.2 Polyfill与Babel配置

##### Vue3兼容性处理方案

```javascript
// vite.config.js - Babel与Polyfill配置
import legacy from '@vitejs/plugin-legacy'

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [
    vue(),
    
    /**
     * @vitejs/plugin-legacy 配置说明:
     * 
     * 工作原理:
     * 1. 构建时生成现代版(Modern)和旧版(Legacy)两套产物
     * 2. 现代浏览器加载ES Module版本(更小更快)
     * 3. 旧浏览器通过<script nomodule>加载IIFE版本(含Polyfill)
     * 4. 通过<script type="module">特性检测自动选择
     */
    legacy({
      // 目标浏览器列表(使用Browserslist标准语法)
      targets: [
        'Chrome >= 64',      // Chrome 64+ (2018年1月)
        'Firefox >= 67',     // Firefox 67+ (2019年5月)
        'Safari >= 12',      // Safari 12+ (2018年9月)
        'Edge >= 79',        // Edge 79+ (Chromium内核,2020年1月)
      ],
      
      // 额外的Polyfill(按需注入)
      additionalLegacyPolyfills: [
        'regenerator-runtime/runtime'  // async/await支持
      ],
      
      // 现代Polyfill(针对新API的Polyfill)
      modernPolyfills: true,
      
      // 渲染Legacy chunks时的选项
      renderLegacyChunks: true,
      
      // 生成Polyfill清单文件(便于排查问题)
      generatePolyfillChunk: true,
    })
  ]
})
```

```javascript
// .browserslistrc - Browserslist配置文件
# Tailor IS 浏览器支持范围

# 生产环境(最终用户)
> 1% in CN           # 中国市场份额超过1%
last 2 versions      # 各浏览器最近2个主版本
not dead             # 排除已停止维护的浏览器
not IE 11            # 明确排除IE 11

# 开发环境(本地开发)
last 1 Chrome version
last 1 Firefox version
last 1 Safari version
```

##### Polyfill按需加载策略

```typescript
// utils/polyfills.ts - 自定义Polyfill管理
/**
 * Tailor IS Polyfill加载策略:
 * 
 * 核心原则:
 * 1. 优先使用原生API(性能最优)
 * 2. 检测到缺失才加载Polyfill(按需加载)
 * 3. 分模块加载(避免一次性加载全部)
 */

// IntersectionObserver懒加载指令依赖
export function ensureIntersectionObserver(): Promise<void> {
  if ('IntersectionObserver' in window) {
    return Promise.resolve()
  }
  
  return import('intersection-observer')
}

// ResizeObserver(响应式组件依赖)
export function ensureResizeObserver(): Promise<void> {
  if ('ResizeObserver' in window) {
    return Promise.resolve()
  }
  
  return import('resize-observer-polyfill')
}

// Clipboard API(复制功能依赖)
export function ensureClipboardAPI(): void {
  if (!navigator.clipboard) {
    // 降级为document.execCommand方案
    console.warn('Clipboard API not supported, fallback to execCommand')
  }
}

// Smooth Scroll平滑滚动
export function ensureSmoothScroll(): void {
  if (!('scrollBehavior' in document.documentElement.style)) {
    import('smoothscroll-polyfill').then(module => {
      module.polyfill()
    })
  }
}

// CSS自定义属性(CSS Variables)检测
export function supportsCssVariables(): boolean {
  return window.CSS && CSS.supports('--a', '0')
}
```

#### 5.1.3 CSS兼容性方案

##### PostCSS与Autoprefixer配置

```javascript
// postcss.config.js - PostCSS处理链配置
module.exports = {
  plugins: [
    // CSS变量降级(为不支持CSS变量的浏览器生成回退值)
    require('postcss-preset-env')({
      stage: 3,  // 使用W3C候选推荐标准的功能
      
      // 启用的功能(按需开启)
      features: {
        'nesting-rules': true,           // CSS嵌套语法
        'custom-media-queries': true,    // 自定义媒体查询
        'custom-properties': true,       // CSS变量
        'color-function': true,          // color()函数
        'gap-properties': true,          // Flex/Grid gap属性
        'not-selectors': true,           // :not()多参数
        'focus-visible': true,           // :focus-visible伪类
        'prefers-color-scheme': true,    // 暗黑模式媒体查询
      },
      
      // 浏览器兼容目标(与Browserslist一致)
      browsers: require('./package.json').browserslist.production
    }),
    
    // 自动添加厂商前缀
    require('autoprefixer')({
      // 覆盖默认配置,精确控制需要的前缀
      overrideBrowserslist: [
        'Chrome >= 64',
        'Firefox >= 67',
        'Safari >= 12',
        'Edge >= 79',
        'iOS >= 12',
        'Android >= 67'
      ],
      
      // 是否移除过时的前缀
      remove: true,
      
      // 是否添加前缀
      add: true,
      
      // 是否支持网格布局内联前缀
      grid: true,  // 为IE生成-grid前缀(虽然我们已放弃IE)
      
      // Flexbox属性是否需要前缀
      flexbox: false  // 现代浏览器已不需要-webkit-box等
    }),
    
    // CSS Modules作用域隔离
    require('postcss-modules')({
      generateScopedName: 'tailoris-[local]--[hash:base64:5]'
    }),
    
    // px转rem(可选,用于移动端适配)
    require('postcss-pxtorem')({
      rootValue: 16,       // 基准字体大小
      unitPrecision: 5,    // 转换精度
      propList: ['*'],     // 需要转换的属性
      selectorBlackList: ['.no-rem'],  // 忽略的选择器
      replace: true,       // 直接替换px值
      mediaQuery: false,   // 媒体查询中的px不转换
      minPixelValue: 2     // 小于2px的不转换
    })
  ]
}
```

##### CSS兼容性工具类库

```scss
// styles/mixins/_compatibility.scss
// Tailor IS CSS兼容性Mixins集合

// ========================================
// Flexbox兼容性Mixin
// ========================================
@mixin flex-display {
  display: flex;
  display: -webkit-flex;  // Safari 9-
  display: -ms-flexbox;   // IE 10(已弃用但保留以防万一)
}

@mixin flex-center {
  @include flex-display;
  justify-content: center;        // -webkit-已不需要(Safari 9+)
  align-items: center;
  -webkit-align-items: center;    // Safari 7-8
  -webkit-justify-content: center;
}

// ========================================
// Grid布局兼容性Mixin
// ========================================
@mixin grid-layout($columns: repeat(3, 1fr), $gap: 16px) {
  display: grid;
  display: -ms-grid;  // IE 10/11(保留但标记废弃)
  grid-template-columns: $columns;
  gap: $gap;
  -webkit-gap: $gap;
  
  // IE 10/11 Grid降级(如果必须支持)
  @supports not (gap: 0) {
    margin: calc(-#{$gap} / 2);
    > * {
      margin: calc(#{$gap} / 2);
    }
  }
}

// ========================================
// 渐变背景兼容性
// ========================================
@mixin linear-gradient($direction: to right, $colors...) {
  background: nth($colors, 1);  // 降级纯色
  
  @if length($colors) >= 2 {
    background: -webkit-linear-gradient(legacy-direction($direction), $colors);
    background: linear-gradient($direction, $colors);
  }
}

@function legacy-direction($dir) {
  // 将标准方向转换为WebKit旧语法
  @if $dir == to right { return left; }
  @else if $dir == to left { return right; }
  @else if $dir == to bottom { return top; }
  @else if $dir == to top { return bottom; }
  @return $dir;
}

// ========================================
// 用户选择禁用(防文本选中)
// ========================================
@mixin user-select($value: none) {
  -webkit-user-select: $value;
  -moz-user-select: $value;
  -ms-user-select: $value;
  user-select: $value;
}

// ========================================
// 触摸操作控制(移动端)
// ========================================
@mixin touch-action($value: manipulation) {
  touch-action: $value;
  -webkit-touch-action: $value;
}

// ========================================
// 滚动条样式兼容(Webkit内核)
// ========================================
@mixin custom-scrollbar($size: 6px, $thumb-color: rgba(0,0,0,0.2)) {
  &::-webkit-scrollbar {
    width: $size;
    height: $size;
  }
  
  &::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb {
    background-color: $thumb-color;
    border-radius: $size / 2;
    
    &:hover {
      background-color: darken($thumb-color, 20%);
    }
  }
  
  &::-webkit-scrollbar-track {
    background-color: transparent;
  }
  
  // Firefox scrollbar styling (Firefox 64+)
  scrollbar-width: thin;
  scrollbar-color: $thumb-color transparent;
}
```

#### 5.1.4 渐进增强与优雅降级策略

##### 特性检测与渐进增强实现

```typescript
// utils/featureDetection.ts - 浏览器特性检测工具集

interface FeatureSupport {
  cssGrid: boolean
  cssFlexbox: boolean
  cssVariables: boolean
  intersectionObserver: boolean
  resizeObserver: boolean
  webp: boolean
  webWorker: boolean
  serviceWorker: boolean
  localStorage: boolean
  sessionStorage: boolean
  es6Modules: boolean
  nativeFetch: boolean
}

/**
 * 全面的浏览器特性检测
 */
export function detectFeatures(): FeatureSupport {
  const features: Partial<FeatureSupport> = {}
  
  // CSS Grid布局检测
  features.cssGrid = CSS.supports('display', 'grid')
  
  // CSS Flexbox检测
  features.cssFlexbox = CSS.supports('display', 'flex')
  
  // CSS变量检测
  features.cssVariables = CSS.supports('--test', '0')
  
  // IntersectionObserver检测
  features.intersectionObserver = 'IntersectionObserver' in window
  
  // ResizeObserver检测
  features.resizeObserver = 'ResizeObserver' in window
  
  // WebP格式支持检测(异步)
  checkWebPSupport().then(supported => {
    features.webp = supported
    // 存储到localStorage供后续使用
    localStorage.setItem('tailoris_webp_support', String(supported))
  })
  
  // Web Worker检测
  features.webWorker = typeof Worker !== 'undefined'
  
  // Service Worker检测
  features.serviceWorker = 'serviceWorker' in navigator
  
  // 存储API检测
  try {
    localStorage.setItem('test', 'test')
    localStorage.removeItem('test')
    features.localStorage = true
  } catch {
    features.localStorage = false
  }
  
  features.sessionStorage = trySessionStorage()
  
  // ES Modules检测
  const script = document.createElement('script')
  script.type = 'module'
  features.es6Modules = !!(script.noModule === undefined || script.noModule === false)
  
  // Fetch API检测
  features.nativeFetch = typeof fetch !== 'undefined'
  
  // 输出检测结果到控制台(仅开发环境)
  if (import.meta.env.DEV) {
    console.table(features)
  }
  
  // 向<body>添加特性class(供CSS条件样式使用)
  updateBodyClasses(features)
  
  return features as FeatureSupport
}

async function checkWebPSupport(): Promise<boolean> {
  // 先检查缓存
  const cached = localStorage.getItem('tailoris_webp_support')
  if (cached !== null) {
    return cached === 'true'
  }
  
  // 创建测试图片进行检测
  return new Promise(resolve => {
    const img = new Image()
    img.onload = () => resolve(img.width > 0 && img.height > 0)
    img.onerror = () => resolve(false)
    img.src = 'data:image/webp;base64,UklGRhoAAABXRUJQVlA4TA0AAAAvAAAAEAcQERGIiP4HAA=='
  })
}

function trySessionStorage(): boolean {
  try {
    sessionStorage.setItem('test', 'test')
    sessionStorage.removeItem('test')
    return true
  } catch {
    return false
  }
}

function updateBodyClasses(features: Partial<FeatureSupport>) {
  const body = document.body
  
  Object.entries(features).forEach(([key, supported]) => {
    if (supported) {
      body.classList.add(`supports-${key}`)
    } else {
      body.classList.add(`no-${key}`)
    }
  })
}
```

##### 优雅降级组件示例

```vue
<!-- ProductGallery.vue - 商品图片画廊(带优雅降级) -->
<template>
  <div class="product-gallery" :class="{ 'no-css-grid': !features.cssGrid }">
    
    <!-- 主图展示区 -->
    <div class="gallery-main" ref="mainImageRef">
      <!-- 现代方案: 使用<picture>元素 + WebP -->
      <picture v-if="features.webp">
        <source 
          :srcset="currentImage.webpUrl" 
          type="image/webp"
        />
        <img
          :src="currentImage.url"
          :alt="product.name"
          class="main-image"
          @load="onImageLoad"
        />
      </picture>
      
      <!-- 降级方案: 传统<img>标签 -->
      <img
        v-else
        :src="currentImage.url"
        :alt="product.name"
        class="main-image"
        @load="onImageLoad"
      />
      
      <!-- 图片放大镜效果(现代浏览器) -->
      <div 
        v-if="features.intersectionObserver"
        class="zoom-lens"
        ref="zoomLensRef"
        v-show="isZooming"
      />
    </div>
    
    <!-- 缩略图列表 -->
    <div class="gallery-thumbs" :class="thumbsLayoutClass">
      <div
        v-for="(image, index) in images"
        :key="image.id"
        class="thumb-item"
        :class="{ active: currentIndex === index }"
        @click="selectImage(index)"
      >
        <img :src="image.thumbnail" :alt="`缩略图${index + 1}`" />
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 旋转木马组件(移动端触摸滑动) -->
    <SwiperCarousel
      v-if="isMobile"
      :images="images"
      @change="selectImage"
    />
    
    <!-- 传统轮播降级(无Swiper时) -->
    <div v-else-if="isMobile" class="fallback-carousel">
      <button @click="prevImage">←</button>
      <img :src="currentImage.url" />
      <button @click="nextImage">→</button>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, computed, onMounted } from 'vue'
import { detectFeatures, FeatureSupport } from '@/utils/featureDetection'

const props = defineProps<{
  product: ProductDTO
  images: ImageDTO[]
}>()

const features = ref<FeatureSupport>({
  cssGrid: false,
  webp: false,
  intersectionObserver: false,
  // ... 其他特性默认false
})

const currentIndex = ref(0)
const isZooming = ref(false)

onMounted(() => {
  // 执行特性检测
  features.value = detectFeatures()
})

const currentImage = computed(() => props.images[currentIndex.value])

// 根据Grid支持情况切换布局
const thumbsLayoutClass = computed(() => {
  return features.value.cssGrid ? 'grid-layout' : 'flex-layout'
})

function selectImage(index: number) {
  currentIndex.value = index
}

function onImageLoad() {
  // 图片加载完成后的逻辑...
}
</script>

<style scoped>
/* 默认: 使用CSS Grid布局 */
.gallery-thumbs.grid-layout {
  display: grid;
  grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fill, minmax(80px, 1fr));
  gap: 8px;
}

/* 降级: 使用Flexbox布局 */
.gallery-thumbs.flex-layout {
  display: flex;
  flex-wrap: wrap;
  gap: 8px;
}

.thumb-item {
  width: 80px;
  height: 80px;
  cursor: pointer;
  border: 2px solid transparent;
  border-radius: 4px;
  overflow: hidden;
  transition: border-color 0.2s;
  
  &.active {
    border-color: #1890ff;
  }
  
  img {
    width: 100%;
    height: 100%;
    object-fit: cover;
  }
}

/* 不支持CSS Grid时的额外样式调整 */
.no-css-grid .gallery-thumbs {
  justify-content: flex-start;
}
</style>
```

### 5.2 移动设备适配

#### 5.2.1 iOS适配要点

##### iOS安全区域与刘海屏处理

```scss
// styles/mixins/_ios.scss
// Tailor IS iOS设备适配Mixins

// ========================================
// Safe Area(安全区域)适配
// iPhone X系列及以后的机型有刘海屏/L动态岛
// ========================================

@mixin safe-area-insets($direction: all) {
  @if $direction == top or $direction == all {
    padding-top: constant(safe-area-inset-top);    // iOS 11.0-11.2
    padding-top: env(safe-area-inset-top);         // iOS 11.2+
  }
  
  @if $direction == bottom or $direction == all {
    padding-bottom: constant(safe-area-inset-bottom);
    padding-bottom: env(safe-area-inset-bottom);
  }
  
  @if $direction == left or $direction == all {
    padding-left: constant(safe-area-inset-left);
    padding-left: env(safe-area-inset-left);
  }
  
  @if $direction == right or $direction == all {
    padding-right: constant(safe-area-inset-right);
    padding-right: env(safe-area-inset-right);
  }
}

// 固定定位底部导航栏(最常见场景)
@mixin fixed-bottom-nav($height: 50px) {
  position: fixed;
  bottom: 0;
  left: 0;
  right: 0;
  height: $height;
  @include safe-area-insets(bottom);
  
  // iOS Safari底部工具栏冲突处理
  @supports (padding: env(safe-area-inset-bottom)) {
    &:after {
      content: '';
      position: absolute;
      top: -$height;
      left: 0;
      right: 0;
      height: $height;
      background: inherit;
    }
  }
}

// 固定顶部导航栏
@mixin fixed-top-nav($height: 44px) {
  position: fixed;
  top: 0;
  left: 0;
  right: 0;
  height: $height;
  @include safe-area-insets(top);
  z-index: 1000;
}
```

```vue
<!-- AppLayout.vue - 移动端布局容器(iOS适配) -->
<template>
  <div class="mobile-app-layout">
    <!-- 顶部导航栏(含状态栏适配) -->
    <header class="app-header" :style="{ paddingTop: statusBarHeight + 'px' }">
      <slot name="header"></slot>
    </header>
    
    <!-- 主内容区域(可滚动) -->
    <main class="app-main" :style="{ paddingTop: headerHeight + 'px' }">
      <slot></slot>
    </main>
    
    <!-- 底部Tab栏(含Home Indicator适配) -->
    <footer class="app-tabbar" :style="{ paddingBottom: safeAreaBottom + 'px' }">
      <slot name="tabbar"></slot>
    </footer>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
import { ref, onMounted, onUnmounted } from 'vue'

// iOS安全区域相关状态
const statusBarHeight = ref(0)  // 状态栏高度
const safeAreaBottom = ref(0)   // 底部安全区域
const headerHeight = ref(44)    // 导航栏基础高度

/**
 * 获取iOS设备安全区域信息
 * 适用于iPhone X/XS/11/12/13/14/15系列(刘海屏/灵动岛)
 */
function getSafeAreaInsets() {
  const div = document.createElement('div')
  div.style.position = 'fixed'
  div.style.left = '0'
  div.style.top = '0'
  div.style.width = '0'
  div.style.height = '0'
  div.style.zIndex = '-1'
  document.body.appendChild(div)
  
  // 获取计算后的样式
  const style = getComputedStyle(div)
  
  const insets = {
    top: parseInt(style.paddingTop) || 0,
    right: parseInt(style.paddingRight) || 0,
    bottom: parseInt(style.paddingBottom) || 0,
    left: parseInt(style.paddingLeft) || 0
  }
  
  document.body.removeChild(div)
  return insets
}

// iOS WebView特殊处理
function detectIOSWebView() {
  const ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase()
  const isIOS = /iphone|ipad|ipod/.test(ua)
  const isWeChat = /micromessenger/.test(ua)
  const isAlipay = /alipayclient/.test(ua)
  
  return {
    isIOS,
    isIOSWebView: isIOS && (isWeChat || isAlipay || !/safari/.test(ua)),
    isWeChat,
    isAlipay
  }
}

onMounted(() => {
  const insets = getSafeAreaInsets()
  statusBarHeight.value = insets.top
  safeAreaBottom.value = insets.bottom
  
  console.log('iOS Safe Area:', insets)
})
</script>

<style scoped>
.mobile-app-layout {
  position: fixed;
  top: 0;
  left: 0;
  right: 0;
  bottom: 0;
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;
  overflow: hidden;
  
  /* iOS Safari橡皮筋效果禁用 */
  overscroll-behavior: none;
  -webkit-overflow-scrolling: touch;
}

.app-header {
  position: relative;
  z-index: 100;
  background: #fff;
  /* iOS状态栏背景色延伸 */
  &:before {
    content: '';
    position: absolute;
    top: 0;
    left: 0;
    right: 0;
    background: inherit;
  }
}

.app-main {
  flex: 1;
  overflow-y: auto;
  overflow-x: hidden;
  /* iOS惯性滚动 */
  -webkit-overflow-scrolling: touch;
  
  /* 隐藏滚动条(可选) */
  &::-webkit-scrollbar {
    display: none;
  }
}

.app-tabbar {
  position: relative;
  z-index: 100;
  background: #fff;
  border-top: 1px solid #eee;
  
  /* iOS底部Home Indicator区域背景色 */
  padding-bottom: constant(safe-area-inset-bottom);
  padding-bottom: env(safe-area-inset-bottom);
}
</style>
```

##### iOS特定问题解决方案

```typescript
// utils/iosFixes.ts - iOS设备常见问题修复

/**
 * iOS常见问题及解决方案:
 * 
 * 1. iOS输入框聚焦页面放大问题
 *    原因: 字体小于16px时iOS会自动放大
 *    解决: input/font-size ≥ 16px 或设置viewport maximum-scale=1
 * 
 * 2. iOS 100vh问题
 *    原因: iOS Safari地址栏影响视口高度
 *    解决: 使用JavaScript动态计算真实视口高度
 * 
 * 3. iOS点击300ms延迟
 *    原因: 双击缩放检测机制
 *    解决: viewport meta设置 user-scalable=no 或使用FastClick
 * 
 * 4. iOS软键盘遮挡输入框
 *    原因: 键盘弹出不会自动滚动到可视区域
 *    解决: scrollIntoView或监听keyboard事件
 */

// 动态获取真实的100vh(解决iOS Safari地址栏问题)
export function getTrueViewportHeight(): number {
  // 使用window.innerHeight(包含/不包含地址栏的真实高度)
  return window.innerHeight
}

// 设置CSS变量--vh(供全局使用)
export function setViewportHeightVariable(): void {
  const setVh = () => {
    const vh = window.innerHeight * 0.01
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--vh', `${vh}px`)
  }
  
  setVh()
  
  // 监听窗口变化(屏幕旋转、键盘弹出收起)
  window.addEventListener('resize', setVh)
  window.addEventListener('orientationchange', () => {
    // 延迟等待方向变化完成
    setTimeout(setVh, 100)
  })
}

// iOS输入框优化
export function fixIOSInputFocus(): void {
  // 方案1: 设置meta标签禁止缩放
  const meta = document.querySelector('meta[name="viewport"]')
  if (meta) {
    meta.setAttribute(
      'content',
      'width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, user-scalable=no, viewport-fit=cover'
    )
  }
  
  // 方案2: 监听input聚焦事件,滚动到可视区域
  document.addEventListener('focusin', (e) => {
    const target = e.target as HTMLElement
    if (
      target.tagName === 'INPUT' ||
      target.tagName === 'TEXTAREA' ||
      target.tagName === 'SELECT'
    ) {
      setTimeout(() => {
        target.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' })
      }, 300)  // 等待键盘弹出动画完成
    }
  })
}

// iOS视频播放优化
export function optimizeIOSVideoPlayback(videoElement: HTMLVideoElement): void {
  // 内联播放(不在新窗口打开)
  videoElement.setAttribute('playsinline', '')
  videoElement.setAttribute('webkit-playsinline', '')
  
  // AirPlay支持
  videoElement.setAttribute('x-webkit-airplay', 'allow')
  
  // 禁用iOS默认的全屏播放行为
  videoElement.setAttribute('controlsList', 'nodownload nofullscreen noremoteplayback')
}
```

```typescript
// utils/androidDetect.ts - Android设备检测与适配

export interface AndroidDeviceInfo {
  manufacturer: string    // 制造商(Huawei/Xiaomi/Oppo/Vivo等)
  model: string           // 型号
  androidVersion: number  // Android版本号
  screenWidth: number     // 屏幕宽度(px)
  screenHeight: number    // 屏幕高度(px)
  pixelRatio: number      // 设备像素比
  isNotchScreen: boolean  // 是否异形屏(挖孔屏/水滴屏)
  notchPosition: 'left' | 'center-right' | 'right' | null  // 刘海位置
}

/**
 * 检测Android设备信息
 */
export function detectAndroidDevice(): AndroidDeviceInfo | null {
  const ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase()
  
  if (!/android/i.test(ua)) {
    return null
  }
  
  // 提取制造商信息
  let manufacturer = 'Unknown'
  if (/huawei|honor/i.test(ua)) manufacturer = 'Huawei'
  else if (/xiaomi|redmi|mi\s/i.test(ua)) manufacturer = 'Xiaomi'
  else if (/oppo/i.test(ua)) manufacturer = 'Oppo'
  else if (/vivo/i.test(ua)) manufacturer = 'Vivo'
  else if (/samsung/i.test(ua)) manufacturer = 'Samsung'
  else if (/oneplus/i.test(ua)) manufacturer = 'OnePlus'
  
  // 提取Android版本
  const versionMatch = ua.match(/android\s(\d+\.?\d*)/)
  const androidVersion = versionMatch ? parseFloat(versionMatch[1]) : 0
  
  // 屏幕信息
  const screenWidth = screen.width
  const screenHeight = screen.height
  const pixelRatio = window.devicePixelRatio || 1
  
  // 异形屏检测(基于屏幕比例推测)
  const aspectRatio = Math.max(screenWidth, screenHeight) / Math.min(screenWidth, screenHeight)
  const isNotchScreen = aspectRatio > 2.0  // 超过20:9大概率是异形屏
  
  // 刘海位置推测(简化判断,实际应通过WebView API获取)
  let notchPosition: AndroidDeviceInfo['notchPosition'] = null
  if (isNotchScreen) {
    // 大部分国产安卓机是居右或居中偏右挖孔
    notchPosition = 'center-right'
  }
  
  return {
    manufacturer,
    model: 'Unknown',
    androidVersion,
    screenWidth,
    screenHeight,
    pixelRatio,
    isNotchScreen,
    notchPosition
  }
}

/**
 * Android WebView内核检测
 * 不同厂商可能使用不同WebView:
 * - Android 5-7: 系统WebView(Chrome M37-M72)
 * - Android 8+: Chrome WebView(可独立更新)
 * - 华为: 可能使用华为自带WebView
 * - 小米: 可能使用小米WebView
 */
export function detectWebViewEngine(): string {
  const ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase()
  
  if (/chrome\/[\d.]+/i.test(ua)) {
    const match = ua.match(/chrome\/([\d.]+)/i)
    return `Chrome WebView ${match?.[1] || 'Unknown'}`
  }
  
  if (/version\/[\d.]+.*safari/i.test(ua)) {
    return 'System WebView'
  }
  
  if (/huaweibrowser/i.test(ua)) {
    return 'Huawei WebView'
  }
  
  if (/miui/i.test(ua)) {
    return 'Xiaomi WebView'
  }
  
  return 'Unknown WebView'
}
```

#### 5.2.3 响应式断点设计

##### Tailor IS断点系统

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│              Tailor IS 响应式断点设计                             │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  断点名称        最小宽度        设备类型        典型设备         │
│  ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────      │
│  xs (超小屏)     0px             手机竖屏      iPhone SE        │
│                                  (320-479px)                   │
│                                                                  │
│  sm (小屏)      480px            手机横屏/大屏  iPhone 12 Pro   │
│                                  (480-767px)   Galaxy S21      │
│                                                                  │
│  md (中等屏)    768px            平板竖屏      iPad             │
│                                  (768-1023px)  iPad Mini       │
│                                                                  │
│  lg (大屏)      1024px           平板横屏/笔记本 iPad Pro        │
│                                  (1024-1279px) MacBook Air      │
│                                                                  │
│  xl (超大屏)    1280px           桌面显示器     iMac 24"        │
│                                  (1280-1535px) Dell U2722D     │
│                                                                  │
│  xxl (超超大屏) 1536px           大屏显示器/电视 4K Display      │
│                                  (1536px+)     iMac 27"         │
│                                                                 │
│  断点使用原则:                                                   │
│  • Mobile First(移动优先): 从小到大编写样式                      │
│  • 内容驱动断点: 根据内容需求而非设备种类                        │
│  • 主要断点之间避免过多中间断点                                 │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

```scss
// styles/_variables.scss
// Tailor IS 设计变量与断点定义

// ========================================
// 响应式断点变量
// ========================================
$breakpoints: (
  'xs': 0,
  'sm': 480px,
  'md': 768px,
  'lg': 1024px,
  'xl': 1280px,
  'xxl': 1536px
);

// ========================================
// 容器最大宽度
// ========================================
$container-max-widths: (
  'xs': 100%,       // 手机: 全宽
  'sm': 100%,       // 小屏: 全宽
  'md': 720px,      // 平板: 720px
  'lg': 960px,      // 笔记本: 960px
  'xl': 1140px,     // 桌面: 1140px
  'xxl': 1320px     // 大屏: 1320px
);

// ========================================
// Mixins: 媒体查询快捷方式
// ========================================

/// 最小宽度断点(@media (min-width: ...))
/// @param {String} $breakpoint - 断点名称(xs/sm/md/lg/xl/xxl)
@mixin respond-above($breakpoint) {
  $value: map-get($breakpoints, $breakpoint);
  
  @if $value {
    @media (min-width: $value) {
      @content;
    }
  } @else {
    @content;
  }
}

/// 最大宽度断点(@media (max-width: ...))
/// @param {String} $breakpoint - 断点名称
@mixin respond-below($breakpoint) {
  $value: map-get($breakpoints, $breakpoint);
  $next-key: map-keys(map-remove($breakpoints, $breakpoint));
  $next-value: map-get($breakpoints, nth($next-key, -1));
  
  @if $next-value {
    @media (max-width: ($next-value - 1px)) {
      @content;
    }
  } @else {
    @content;
  }
}

/// 仅在两个断点之间的样式
/// @param {String} $lower - 下限断点
/// @param {String} $upper - 上限断点
@mixin respond-between($lower, $upper) {
  $min-value: map-get($breakpoints, $lower);
  $max-value: map-get($breakpoints, $upper);
  
  @media (min-width: $min-value) and (max-width: ($max-value - 1px)) {
    @content;
  }
}

// ========================================
// 使用示例
// ========================================

// .container {
//   width: 100%;
//   margin: 0 auto;
//   
//   @each $name, $width in $container-max-widths {
//     @include respond-above($name) {
//       max-width: $width;
//     }
//   }
// }
```

##### TypeScript响应式Hook

```typescript
// hooks/useBreakpoint.ts - Vue3响应式断点Hook
import { ref, onMounted, onUnmounted, computed } from 'vue'

type Breakpoint = 'xs' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'xl' | 'xxl'

const BREAKPOINTS: Record<Breakpoint, number> = {
  xs: 0,
  sm: 480,
  md: 768,
  lg: 1024,
  xl: 1280,
  xxl: 1536
}

export interface UseBreakpointReturn {
  currentBreakpoint: Ref<Breakpoint>
  isMobile: ComputedRef<boolean>      // xs, sm
  isTablet: ComputedRef<boolean>      // md
  isDesktop: ComputedRef<boolean>     // lg, xl, xxl
  screenWidth: Ref<number>
  screenHeight: Ref<number>
}

/**
 * 响应式断点检测Hook
 * 
 * @example
 * ```vue
 * <script setup>
 * const { isMobile, currentBreakpoint } = useBreakpoint()
 * </script>
 * 
 * <template>
 *   <div :class="['layout', currentBreakpoint]">
 *     <Sidebar v-if="!isMobile" />
 *   </div>
 * </template>
 * ```
 */
export function useBreakpoint(): UseBreakpointReturn {
  const screenWidth = ref(window.innerWidth)
  const screenHeight = ref(window.innerHeight)
  
  const currentBreakpoint = computed<Breakpoint>(() => {
    const width = screenWidth.value
    
    if (width >= BREAKPOINTS.xxl) return 'xxl'
    if (width >= BREAKPOINTS.xl) return 'xl'
    if (width >= BREAKPOINTS.lg) return 'lg'
    if (width >= BREAKPOINTS.md) return 'md'
    if (width >= BREAKPOINTS.sm) return 'sm'
    return 'xs'
  })
  
  const isMobile = computed(() => 
    currentBreakpoint.value === 'xs' || currentBreakpoint.value === 'sm'
  )
  
  const isTablet = computed(() => currentBreakpoint.value === 'md')
  
  const isDesktop = computed(() => 
    ['lg', 'xl', 'xxl'].includes(currentBreakpoint.value)
  )
  
  function handleResize() {
    screenWidth.value = window.innerWidth
    screenHeight.value = window.innerHeight
  }
  
  // 使用ResizeObserver替代resize事件(更精确)
  let resizeObserver: ResizeObserver | null = null
  
  onMounted(() => {
    // 优先使用ResizeObserver
    if ('ResizeObserver' in window) {
      resizeObserver = new ResizeObserver(handleResize)
      resizeObserver.observe(document.documentElement)
    } else {
      window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize)
    }
  })
  
  onUnmounted(() => {
    if (resizeObserver) {
      resizeObserver.disconnect()
    } else {
      window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize)
    }
  })
  
  return {
    currentBreakpoint,
    isMobile,
    isTablet,
    isDesktop,
    screenWidth,
    screenHeight
  }
}
```

#### 5.2.4 触摸交互优化

##### 手势事件处理

```typescript
// composables/useTouchGestures.ts - 触摸手势组合式函数
import { ref, onMounted, onUnmounted, type Ref } from 'vue'

interface TouchGestureOptions {
  element: Ref<HTMLElement | undefined>
  swipeThreshold?: number      // 滑动阈值(px),默认50
  swipeVelocity?: number       // 滑动速度阈值(px/ms),默认0.3
  tapThreshold?: number        // 点击阈值(ms),默认300
  longPressDelay?: number      // 长按延迟(ms),默认500
  preventDefault?: boolean     // 是否阻止默认行为
}

interface TouchCallbacks {
  onTap?: (event: TouchEvent) => void
  onDoubleTap?: (event: TouchEvent) => void
  onSwipeLeft?: (event: TouchEvent, distance: number) => void
  onSwipeRight?: (event: TouchEvent, distance: number) => void
  onSwipeUp?: (event: TouchEvent, distance: number) => void
  onSwipeDown?: (event: TouchEvent, distance: number) => void
  onLongPress?: (event: TouchEvent) => void
  onPinchStart?: (scale: number) => void
  onPinchMove?: (scale: number) => void
  onPinchEnd?: (scale: number) => void
}

export function useTouchGestures(options: TouchGestureOptions, callbacks: TouchCallbacks) {
  const {
    element,
    swipeThreshold = 50,
    tapThreshold = 300,
    longPressDelay = 500,
    preventDefault = true
  } = options
  
  let startX = 0
  let startY = 0
  let startTime = 0
  let lastTapTime = 0
  let longPressTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
  let isLongPressTriggered = false
  
  function handleTouchStart(e: TouchEvent) {
    if (preventDefault && e.cancelable) {
      e.preventDefault()
    }
    
    const touch = e.touches[0]
    startX = touch.clientX
    startY = touch.clientY
    startTime = Date.now()
    isLongPressTriggered = false
    
    // 设置长按定时器
    longPressTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      isLongPressTriggered = true
      callbacks.onLongPress?.(e)
    }, longPressDelay)
  }
  
  function handleTouchEnd(e: TouchEvent) {
    if (preventDefault && e.cancelable) {
      e.preventDefault()
    }
    
    // 清除长按定时器
    if (longPressTimer) {
      clearTimeout(longPressTimer)
      longPressTimer = null
    }
    
    // 如果已经触发长按,不再处理点击
    if (isLongPressTriggered) return
    
    const touch = e.changedTouches[0]
    const endX = touch.clientX
    const endY = touch.clientY
    const endTime = Date.now()
    
    const deltaX = endX - startX
    const deltaY = endY - startY
    const deltaTime = endTime - startTime
    const absDeltaX = Math.abs(deltaX)
    const absDeltaY = Math.abs(deltaY)
    
    // 判断手势类型
    if (deltaTime < tapThreshold && absDeltaX < 10 && absDeltaY < 10) {
      // 点击或双击
      const now = Date.now()
      if (now - lastTapTime < 300) {
        callbacks.onDoubleTap?.(e)
        lastTapTime = 0
      } else {
        callbacks.onTap?.(e)
        lastTapTime = now
      }
    } else if (absDeltaX > swipeThreshold || absDeltaY > swipeThreshold) {
      // 滑动手势
      if (absDeltaX > absDeltaY) {
        // 水平滑动
        if (deltaX > 0) {
          callbacks.onSwipeRight?.(e, deltaX)
        } else {
          callbacks.onSwipeLeft?.(e, absDeltaX)
        }
      } else {
        // 垂直滑动
        if (deltaY > 0) {
          callbacks.onSwipeDown?.(e, deltaY)
        } else {
          callbacks.onSwipeUp?.(e, absDeltaY)
        }
      }
    }
  }
  
  onMounted(() => {
    const el = element.value
    if (el) {
      el.addEventListener('touchstart', handleTouchStart, { passive: false })
      el.addEventListener('touchend', handleTouchEnd, { passive: false })
    }
  })
  
  onUnmounted(() => {
    const el = element.value
    if (el) {
      el.removeEventListener('touchstart', handleTouchStart)
      el.removeEventListener('touchend', handleTouchEnd)
    }
    if (longPressTimer) {
      clearTimeout(longPressTimer)
    }
  })
}
```

##### 触摸反馈与优化CSS

```scss
// styles/touch.scss
// Tailor IS 触摸交互优化样式

/* ========================================
   触摸反馈效果
   - 点击高亮(移动端必备)
   - 禁用点击高亮(PC端)
   - 触摸优化
   ======================================== */

// 移动端触摸高亮
.touchable {
  -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(24, 144, 255, 0.3);  // 蓝色半透明
  touch-action: manipulation;  // 优化触摸响应,禁用双击缩放
  
  // 点击时的视觉反馈
  &:active {
    opacity: 0.7;
    transform: scale(0.98);
    transition: transform 0.1s ease, opacity 0.1s ease;
  }
}

// PC端禁用触摸高亮(避免蓝色闪烁)
@media (hover: hover) and (pointer: fine) {
  .touchable {
    -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent;
    
    &:hover {
      opacity: 0.85;
    }
    
    &:active {
      opacity: 1;
      transform: none;
    }
  }
}

/* ========================================
   惯性滚动优化(iOS关键!)
   ======================================== */
.scroll-container {
  overflow-y: auto;
  -webkit-overflow-scrolling: touch;  // iOS弹性滚动
  
  // 隐藏滚动条(保持可滚动)
  &::-webkit-scrollbar {
    display: none;
    width: 0;
    height: 0;
  }
  
  // Firefox隐藏滚动条
  scrollbar-width: none;
}

/* ========================================
   防止iOS下拉刷新冲突
   ======================================== */
.no-pull-to-refresh {
  overscroll-behavior-y: contain;
}

/* ========================================
   可拖拽元素的触摸优化
   ======================================== */
.draggable {
  touch-action: none;  // 完全由JS控制触摸行为
  user-select: none;
  -webkit-user-select: none;
  cursor: grab;
  
  &:active {
    cursor: grabbing;
  }
}

/* ========================================
   Swipeable卡片滑动删除组件
   ======================================== */
.swipeable-item {
  position: relative;
  overflow: hidden;
  touch-action: pan-y;  // 只允许垂直方向的系统手势
  
  .swipeable-content {
    transition: transform 0.3s ease-out;
    will-change: transform;  // GPU加速
  }
  
  .swipeable-actions {
    position: absolute;
    right: 0;
    top: 0;
    bottom: 0;
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    
    .action-btn {
      height: 100%;
      padding: 0 20px;
      color: white;
      font-size: 14px;
      border: none;
      cursor: pointer;
      
      &.danger {
        background: #ff4d4f;
      }
      
      &.warning {
        background: #faad14;
      }
    }
  }
}
```

### 5.3 桌面环境兼容

#### 5.3.1 Windows 10/11兼容性

##### DPI缩放与高分辨率屏适配

```typescript
// utils/dpiAdapter.ts - Windows DPI缩放适配工具

/**
 * Windows DPI缩放问题:
 * 
 * 问题现象:
 * - 125%/150%/175%/200% DPI下界面模糊
 * - Canvas/SVG绘制尺寸不准确
 * - 截图/截图功能尺寸错误
 * - 第三方库(如ECharts)显示异常
 * 
 * 解决方案:
 * 1. 使用devicePixelRatio检测缩放比例
 * 2. Canvas绘制时乘以dpr
 * 3. CSS使用rem/vw单位而非固定px
 * 4. 设置viewport meta标签正确
 */

export interface DPIInfo {
  dpr: number              // 设备像素比(1/1.25/1.5/1.75/2/2.5/3)
  scaleFactor: number      // 缩放百分比(100/125/150/175/200)
  logicalWidth: number     // 逻辑像素宽度
  logicalHeight: number    // 逻辑像素高度
  physicalWidth: number    // 物理像素宽度
  physicalHeight: number   // 物理像素高度
  isHighDPI: boolean       // 是否高DPI屏幕(dpr > 1)
  is4KDisplay: boolean     // 是否4K显示器(≥3840x2160)
}

/**
 * 获取当前设备的DPI信息
 */
export function getDPIInfo(): DPIInfo {
  const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1
  const scaleFactor = Math.round(dpr * 100)
  
  const logicalWidth = screen.width
  const logicalHeight = screen.height
  const physicalWidth = Math.round(screen.width * dpr)
  const physicalHeight = Math.round(screen.height * dpr)
  
  return {
    dpr,
    scaleFactor,
    logicalWidth,
    logicalHeight,
    physicalWidth,
    physicalHeight,
    isHighDPI: dpr > 1,
    is4KDisplay: physicalWidth >= 3840 && physicalHeight >= 2160
  }
}

/**
 * 高DPI Canvas适配
 * 用于Canvas绑制图表、图片编辑等功能
 */
export function adaptCanvasForDPI(canvas: HTMLCanvasElement, width: number, height: number): void {
  const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1
  
  // 设置Canvas的实际物理尺寸(内部缓冲区)
  canvas.width = width * dpr
  canvas.height = height * dpr
  
  // 设置CSS显示尺寸(逻辑尺寸)
  canvas.style.width = `${width}px`
  canvas.style.height = `${height}px`
  
  // 获取绘图上下文并缩放
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d')
  if (ctx) {
    ctx.scale(dpr, dpr)
  }
  
  // 启用图像平滑(高DPI下文字更清晰)
  if (ctx) {
    ctx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true
    ctx.imageSmoothingQuality = 'high'
  }
}

/**
 * 设置全局CSS变量(供样式系统使用)
 */
export function setDPICSSVariables(): void {
  const dpiInfo = getDPIInfo()
  const root = document.documentElement
  
  root.style.setProperty('--dpr', String(dpiInfo.dpr))
  root.style.setProperty('--scale-factor', String(dpiInfo.scaleFactor))
  root.style.setProperty('--physical-width', `${dpiInfo.physicalWidth}px`)
  root.style.setProperty('--physical-height', `${dpiInfo.physicalHeight}px`)
  
  // 根据DPI调整基准字号
  if (dpiInfo.isHighDPI) {
    // 高DPI屏幕可以适当增大字号
    root.style.setProperty('--base-font-size', `${16 * dpiInfo.dpr * 0.85}px`)
  }
}

/**
 * 监听DPI变化(用户更改Windows缩放设置时)
 */
export function watchDPIChange(callback: (dpiInfo: DPIInfo) => void): () => void {
  // 使用matchMedia监听resolution变化
  const query = `(resolution: ${window.devicePixelRatio}dppx)`
  const mediaQuery = window.matchMedia(query)
  
  function handler() {
    callback(getDPIInfo())
    setDPICSSVariables()
  }
  
  mediaQuery.addEventListener('change', handler)
  
  // 返回取消监听的函数
  return () => {
    mediaQuery.removeEventListener('change', handler)
  }
}
```

#### 5.3.2 macOS兼容性

##### Retina显示与触控板支持

```typescript
// utils/macOSAdapter.ts - macOS特定适配

/**
 * macOS特有功能适配:
 * 
 * 1. Retina显示屏(2x/3x/5x像素密度)
 * 2. 触控板手势(双指滚动/三指拖拽/Force Touch)
 * 3. 深色模式(Dark Mode)
 * 4. Mission Control/Spaces虚拟桌面
 * 5. Spotlight搜索集成
 */

// 检测macOS系统
export function isMacOS(): boolean {
  return /macintosh|mac os x|macintel/i.test(navigator.userAgent)
}

// 检测是否Retina显示屏
export function isRetinaDisplay(): boolean {
  if (!isMacOS()) return false
  
  const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1
  // Retina屏幕通常dpr >= 2
  return dpr >= 2
}

// 获取Retina显示等级
export function getRetinaLevel(): 1 | 2 | 3 | 'super-retina' {
  const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1
  
  if (dpr >= 3) return 'super-retina'  // 新款MacBook Pro (3024x1964)
  if (dpr >= 2.5) return 3            // MacBook Pro 2018+
  if (dpr >= 2) return 2              // 标准Retina
  return 1                              // 非Retina
}

// macOS深色模式检测与跟随
export function initDarkModeSync(): void {
  // 检测系统深色模式偏好
  const prefersDark = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)')
  
  const applyDarkMode = (isDark: boolean) => {
    document.documentElement.classList.toggle('dark', isDark)
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', isDark ? 'dark' : 'light')
    
    // 触发Vue响应式更新(如果使用了Pinia/Vuex状态管理)
    window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('theme-change', { detail: { isDark } }))
  }
  
  // 初始应用
  applyDarkMode(prefersDark.matches)
  
  // 监听系统主题变化
  prefersDark.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
    applyDarkMode(e.matches)
  })
}

// macOS触控板手势增强
export function enhanceTrackpadGestures(element: HTMLElement): void {
  if (!isMacOS()) return
  
  // Force Touch压力感应(3D Touch)
  element.addEventListener('webkitmouseforcewillchange', (e) => {
    // 即将触发Force Touch
  }, { passive: true })
  
  element.addEventListener('webkitmouseforcechanged', (e) => {
    const force = (e as any).webkitForce  // 0-1之间的压力值
    
    if (force > 0.8) {
      // 强力按压(类似长按或预览)
      element.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('forcepress', { detail: { force } }))
    }
  }, { passive: true })
  
  // Momentum Scrolling(惯性滚动)已在CSS中通过-webkit-overflow-scrolling启用
}
```

// electron-builder.yml - Electron跨平台打包配置

  output: dist-electron

        - ia32

        - x64

        - arm64

        - x64

  oneClick: false
  perMachine: false
  allowToChangeInstallationDirectory: true
  installerIcon: build/icon.ico
  uninstallerIcon: build/icon.ico
  installerHeaderIcon: build/icon.ico
  createDesktopShortcut: true
  createStartMenuShortcut: true
  shortcutName: Tailor IS

# DMG配置(macOS)

  contents:
    - x: 130
      y: 220
    - x: 410
      y: 220
      type: link
      path: /Applications

# 应用更新配置(使用electron-updater)
publish:
  provider: generic
  url: https://download.tailoris.com/desktop/updates/
```

#### 6.1.1 服装行业UI设计规范

##### Tailor IS设计系统架构

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│              Tailor IS 设计系统(Tailor Design)                   │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │  🎨 品牌色彩系统                                         │   │
│  ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤   │
│  │  主色(Primary):    #1890FF (品牌蓝)                      │   │
│  │  辅助色(Accent):   #FF6B81 (时尚粉/女装强调)             │   │
│  │  成功色(Success):  #52C41A (订单成功绿)                  │   │
│  │  警告色(Warning):   #FAAD14 (库存预警橙)                 │   │
│  │  错误色(Error):    #FF4D4F (价格异常红)                  │   │
│  │  中性色(Neutral):   #8C8C8C ~ #262626 (文字层级)        │   │

│                                                                 │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │

│  │  基础单位(Base Unit): 4px                                │   │
│  │  间距阶梯: 4 / 8 / 12 / 16 / 20 / 24 / 32 / 40 / 48px  │   │
│  │  栅格列数: 24列(Gutter: 16-24px,响应式调整)              │   │
