│  │    • Display: 36px (活动标题/促销Banner)                │   │
│  │    • H1: 30px (页面主标题)                               │   │
│  │    • H2: 24px (区块标题)                                 │   │
│  │    • H3: 20px (卡片标题)                                 │   │
│  │    • Body: 16px (正文内容)                               │   │
│  │    • Caption: 14px (辅助说明)                            │   │
│  │    • Small: 12px (标签/角标)                             │   │
│  │  行高: 1.5 (正文) / 1.2 (标题)                          │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│                                                                 │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │  🖼️ 图标系统                                             │   │
│  ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤   │
│  │  图标库: Element Plus Icons + 自定义行业图标               │   │
│  │  图标尺寸: 12 / 14 / 16 / 20 / 24 / 32 / 48px          │   │
│  │  线条粗细: 1.5px (常规) / 2px (强调)                    │   │
│  │  圆角规则:                                              │   │
│  │    • 小元素(Button/Tag): 4px                             │   │
│  │    • 中元素(Card/Input): 8px                             │   │
│  │    • 大元素(Modal/Drawer): 12px                          │   │
│  │    • 圆形元素(Avatar): 50%                               │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**参考系统 vs Tailor IS 设计对比**

| 设计维度 | 参考系统现状 | Tailor IS 目标方案 |
|---------|-------------|-------------------|
| **UI框架** | Element UI 2.x(传统企业风格) | Element Plus 2.x(现代简洁/Vue3原生) |
| **配色方案** | 蓝色单色调 | 行业特色多色调(蓝+粉+金) |
| **字体** | 默认中文字体 | PingFang SC/Microsoft YaHei优化 |
| **图标** | Element UI图标 | Element Plus Icons + 服装行业定制图标 |
| **动效** | 几乎无过渡动画 | 微交互动效(300ms ease-out) |
| **暗黑模式** | 不支持 | 支持亮色/暗色/自动切换 |

##### CSS设计Token实现

```scss
// styles/_design-tokens.scss
// Tailor IS Design Tokens - 设计变量定义

// ========================================
// 颜色系统(Color Tokens)
// ========================================

// 品牌主色(Primary Blue)
$color-primary: #1890FF;
$color-primary-hover: #40A9FF;
$color-primary-active: #096DD9;
$color-primary-bg: #E6F7FF;

// 时尚强调色(Accent Pink - 用于女装/潮流品类)
$color-accent-pink: #FF6B81;
$color-accent-gold: #FAAD14;     // 高端/奢侈品品类
$color-accent-green: #52C41A;     // 自然/环保品类

// 功能语义色
$color-success: #52C41A;
$color-success-bg: #F6FFED;
$color-warning: #FAAD14;
$color-warning-bg: #FFFBE6;
$error: #FF4D4F;
$error-bg: #FFF2F0;
$info: #1890FF;
$info-bg: #E6F7FF;

// 中性色阶(Neutral Scale)
$color-text-primary: #262626;    // 主文字
$color-text-secondary: #595959;  // 次要文字
$color-text-tertiary: #8C8C8C;   // 辅助文字
$color-text-quaternary: #BFBFBF; // 占位文字/禁用
$color-border: #D9D9D9;
$color-divider: #F0F0F0;
$color-background: #F5F5F5;

// ========================================
// 间距系统(Spacing Tokens)
// ========================================
$spacing-base: 4px;
$space-xs: $spacing-base;         // 4px
$space-sm: $spacing-base * 2;     // 8px
$space-md: $spacing-base * 3;     // 12px
$space-lg: $spacing-base * 4;     // 16px
$space-xl: $spacing-base * 5;     // 20px
$space-xxl: $spacing-base * 6;    // 24px
$space-xxxl: $spacing-base * 8;   // 32px
$space-xxxxl: $spacing-base * 10; // 40px

// ========================================
// 字体系统(TypeScale)
// ========================================
$font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', 
             'PingFang SC', 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'Microsoft YaHei', 
             'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;
$font-family-mono: 'SFMono-Regular', Consolas, 'Liberation Mono', Menlo, monospace;

$font-size-display: 36px;
$font-size-h1: 30px;
$font-size-h2: 24px;
$font-size-h3: 20px;
$font-size-body: 16px;
$font-size-caption: 14px;
$font-size-small: 12px;

$line-height-tight: 1.2;   // 标题行高
$line-height-normal: 1.5;  // 正文行高
$line-height-relaxed: 1.75; // 宽松行高

$font-weight-normal: 400;
$font-weight-medium: 500;
$font-weight-semibold: 600;
$font-weight-bold: 700;

// ========================================
// 圆角系统(Border Radius)
// ========================================
$radius-xs: 2px;
$radius-sm: 4px;    // 小按钮/标签
$radius-md: 8px;    // 卡片/输入框
$radius-lg: 12px;   // 弹窗/抽屉
$radius-xl: 16px;   // 大卡片
$radius-full: 9999px; // 圆形(头像/标签)

// ========================================
// 阴影系统(Box Shadows)
// ========================================
$shadow-sm: 0 1px 2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.03), 
            0 1px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.02), 
            0 2px 4px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.02);
            
$shadow-md: 0 3px 6px -4px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.12), 
            0 6px 16px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08), 
            0 9px 28px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05);
            
$shadow-lg: 0 6px 16px -8px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08), 
            0 9px 28px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05), 
            0 12px 48px 16px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.03);

// ========================================
// 动画系统(Animation/Easing)
// ========================================
$duration-fast: 150ms;
$duration-normal: 300ms;
$duration-slow: 500ms;

$ease-default: cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);      // 标准缓动
$ease-in: cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1);               // 进入缓动
$ease-out: cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1);              // 离开缓动
$ease-in-out: cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);         // 进出缓动
$ease-spring: cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1);    // 弹性效果

// Z-Index层级管理
$z-dropdown: 1000;
$z-sticky: 1020;
$z-fixed: 1030;
$z-modal-backdrop: 1040;
$z-modal: 1050;
$z-popover: 1060;
$z-tooltip: 1070;
```

#### 6.1.2 操作反馈机制

##### 全局反馈组件封装

```typescript
// composables/useFeedback.ts - 统一操作反馈Hook
import { ElMessage, ElNotification, ElMessageBox } from 'element-plus'
import type { MessageOptions } from 'element-plus'

/**
 * Tailor IS 操作反馈规范:
 *
 * 反馈类型与使用场景:
 * 1. Toast消息(ElMessage): 轻量级即时反馈(< 3秒自动消失)
 *    - 操作成功/失败提示
 *    - 表单验证错误
 *    - 数据加载状态
 * 
 * 2. Notification通知(notification): 重要信息提醒
 *    - 订单状态变更
 *    - 系统公告推送
 *    - 库存预警通知
 * 
 * 3. Modal弹窗(Modal): 需要用户确认的操作
 *    - 删除确认
 *    - 敏感操作二次确认
 *    - 重要信息展示
 */

interface FeedbackOptions {
  duration?: number      // 显示时长(ms)
  showProgress?: boolean // 是否显示进度条
  onClose?: () => void   // 关闭回调
}

class FeedbackService {
  
  /**
   * 成功提示
   */
  success(content: string, options?: FeedbackOptions) {
    return message.success({
      content,
      duration: options?.duration ?? 3,
      key: `success-${Date.now()}`,
    })
  }
  
  /**
   * 错误提示
   */
  error(content: string, options?: FeedbackOptions) {
    return message.error({
      content,
      duration: options?.duration ?? 5,  // 错误信息显示更久
      key: `error-${Date.now()}`,
    })
  }
  
  /**
   * 警告提示
   */
  warning(content: string, options?: FeedbackOptions) {
    return message.warning({
      content,
      duration: options?.duration ?? 4,
    })
  }
  
  /**
   * 信息提示
   */
  info(content: string, options?: FeedbackOptions) {
    return message.info({
      content,
      duration: options?.duration ?? 3,
    })
  }
  
  /**
   * 加载中提示(带自定义内容)
   */
  loading(content: string = '加载中...') {
    return message.loading({
      content,
      duration: 0,  // 手动关闭
    })
  }

  // ==================== Notification通知 ====================
  
  /**
   * 订单状态变更通知
   */
  orderNotification(orderInfo: { orderSn: string; status: string; statusText: string }) {
    notification.open({
      message: `订单 ${orderInfo.orderSn} 状态更新`,
      description: `您的订单已变更为「${orderInfo.statusText}」`,
      icon: () => this.getStatusIcon(orderInfo.status),
      placement: 'topRight',
      duration: 10,
    })
  }
  
  /**
   * 库存预警通知
   */
  stockWarningNotification(productName: string, currentStock: number) {
    notification.warning({
      message: '库存预警',
      description: `商品「${productName}」库存不足,当前仅剩${currentStock}件`,
      placement: 'topRight',
      duration: null,  // 手动关闭
    })
  }
  
  private getStatusIcon(status: string) {
    const iconMap: Record<string, string> = {
      PAID: '💰',
      SHIPPED: '🚚',
      DELIVERED: '📦',
      COMPLETED: '✅',
      CANCELLED: '❌',
    }
    return h('span', { style: { fontSize: '24px' } }, iconMap[status] || '📋')
  }

  // ==================== Modal确认框 ====================
  
  /**
   * 删除确认对话框
   */
  async confirmDelete(options: {
    title?: string
    content: string
    dangerText?: string
  }): Promise<boolean> {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      Modal.confirm({
        title: options.title || '确认删除',
        content: options.content,
        okText: '确定删除',
        cancelText: '取消',
        okType: 'danger',
        centered: true,
        onOk: () => resolve(true),
        onCancel: () => resolve(false),
      })
    })
  }
  
  /**
   * 敏感操作二次确认(如批量上下架)
   */
  async confirmSensitiveAction(options: {
    title: string
    description: string
    confirmLabel?: string
    requireInput?: boolean  // 是否需要手动输入确认文字
  }): Promise<boolean> {
    if (options.requireInput) {
      // 需要手动输入确认文字的场景(如删除店铺等高危操作)
      return new Promise((resolve) => {
        Modal.confirm({
          title: options.title,
          content: h('div', [
            h('p', options.description),
            h('p', { style: { color: '#ff4d4f', marginTop: '8px' } }, 
              `请输入「${options.confirmLabel || '确认'}」以继续`),
            h('a-input', { 
              id: 'confirm-input',
              placeholder: `请输入"${options.confirmLabel || '确认'}"`,
              style: { marginTop: '8px' },
              onChange: (e: any) => {
                const value = e.target.value
                const okBtn = document.querySelector('.ant-btn-primary') as HTMLButtonElement
                if (okBtn) {
                  okBtn.disabled = value !== (options.confirmLabel || '确认')
                }
              }
            }),
          ]),
          okText: '确认操作',
          cancelText: '取消',
          okType: 'danger',
          onOk: () => resolve(true),
          onCancel: () => resolve(false),
        })
      })
    }
    
    return this.confirmDelete({ title: options.title, content: options.description })
  }
}

export const feedback = new FeedbackService()
export default feedback
```

```vue
<!-- GlobalLoading.vue - 全局Loading组件 -->
<template>
  <div class="global-loading" :class="{ visible: isVisible }">
    <div class="loading-backdrop" @click="handleBackdropClick" />
    
    <div class="loading-container">
      <!-- 自定义Loading动画 -->
      <div class="loading-spinner">
        <svg viewBox="0 0 50 50" class="spinner-svg">
          <circle
            cx="25"
            cy="25"
            r="20"
            fill="none"
            stroke="#1890FF"
            stroke-width="4"
            stroke-linecap="round"
            class="spinner-circle"
          />
        </svg>
      </div>
      
      <!-- 加载文字 -->
      <p v-if="text" class="loading-text">{{ text }}</p>
      
      <!-- 加载进度(可选) -->
      <div v-if="showProgress && progress !== undefined" class="loading-progress">
        <div class="progress-bar">
          <div 
            class="progress-fill" 
            :style="{ width: `${progress}%` }"
          />
        </div>
        <span class="progress-text">{{ Math.round(progress) }}%</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, computed } from 'vue'

const props = withDefaults(defineProps<{
  visible: boolean
  text?: string
  fullscreen?: boolean
  showProgress?: boolean
  progress?: number
  backdropCloseable?: boolean
}>(), {
  text: '加载中...',
  fullscreen: true,
  showProgress: false,
  backdropCloseable: false
})

const emit = defineEmits<{
  (e: 'update:visible', value: boolean): void
  (e: 'close'): void
}>()

const isVisible = computed(() => props.visible)

function handleBackdropClick() {
  if (props.backdropCloseable) {
    emit('update:visible', false)
    emit('close')
  }
}
</script>

#### 6.1.3 表单体验优化

##### 智能表单校验配置

```typescript
// utils/formValidators.ts - Tailor IS表单校验规则集
import type { FormItemRule } from 'element-plus'

/**
 * 通用校验规则
 */

// 手机号校验(支持中国大陆手机号)
export function validatePhone(rule: RuleObject, value: string): Promise<void> {
  if (!value) {
    return Promise.reject('请输入手机号')
  }
  const phoneReg = /^1[3-9]\d{9}$/
  if (!phoneReg.test(value)) {
    return Promise.reject('请输入正确的11位手机号')
  }
  return Promise.resolve()
}

// 密码强度校验
export function validatePassword(rule: RuleObject, value: string): Promise<void> {
  if (!value) {
    return Promise.reject('请输入密码')
  }
  if (value.length < 8) {
    return Promise.reject('密码长度不能少于8位')
  }
  if (value.length > 20) {
    return Promise.reject('密码长度不能超过20位')
  }
  // 至少包含数字、大写字母、小写字母、特殊符号中的3种
  const patterns = [
    /[0-9]/,
    /[A-Z]/,
    /[a-z]/,
    /[!@#$%^&*()_+\-=\[\]{};':"\\|,.<>\/?]/
  ]
  const matchCount = patterns.filter(p => p.test(value)).length
  if (matchCount < 3) {
    return Promise.reject('密码需包含数字、大小写字母、特殊符号中的至少3种')
  }
  return Promise.resolve()
}

// 商品价格校验(保留2位小数,正数)
export function validatePrice(rule: RuleObject, value: number): Promise<void> {
  if (value === undefined || value === null) {
    return Promise.reject('请输入商品价格')
  }
  if (typeof value !== 'number' || isNaN(value)) {
    return Promise.reject('价格必须是数字')
  }
  if (value <= 0) {
    return Promise.reject('价格必须大于0')
  }
  if (value > 999999.99) {
    return Promise.reject('价格不能超过999,999.99元')
  }
  // 检查小数位数
  const decimalPart = String(value).split('.')[1]
  if (decimalPart && decimalPart.length > 2) {
    return Promise.reject('价格最多保留2位小数')
  }
  return Promise.resolve()
}

// SKU库存校验
export function validateStock(rule: RuleObject, value: number): Promise<void> {
  if (value === undefined || value === null) {
    return Promise.reject('请输入库存数量')
  }
  if (!Number.isInteger(value)) {
    return Promise.reject('库存必须为整数')
  }
  if (value < 0) {
    return Promise.reject('库存不能为负数')
  }
  if (value > 999999) {
    return Promise.reject('库存数量超出限制')
  }
  return Promise.resolve()
}

// 商品名称校验
export function validateProductName(rule: RuleObject, value: string): Promise<void> {
  if (!value || !value.trim()) {
    return Promise.reject('请输入商品名称')
  }
  if (value.trim().length < 2) {
    return Promise.reject('商品名称至少2个字符')
  }
  if (value.trim().length > 100) {
    return Promise.reject('商品名称不能超过100个字符')
  }
  // 检查敏感词(示例)
  const sensitiveWords = ['最', '第一', '国家级', '顶级']
  for (const word of sensitiveWords) {
    if (value.includes(word)) {
      return Promise.reject(`商品名称包含违禁词「${word}」,请修改`)
    }
  }
  return Promise.resolve()
}

// 身份证号校验
export function validateIdCard(rule: RuleObject, value: string): Promise<void> {
  if (!value) {
    return Promise.reject('请输入身份证号')
  }
  const idCardReg = /(^\d{15}$)|(^\d{18}$)|(^\d{17}(\d|X|x)$)/
  if (!idCardReg.test(value)) {
    return Promise.reject('请输入正确的身份证号码')
  }
  return Promise.resolve()
}

/**
 * 异步校验器(用于检查唯一性等场景)
 */
export async function validateUniquePhone(
  rule: RuleObject, 
  value: string
): Promise<void> {
  if (!value) return Promise.resolve()
  
  try {
    const { data } = await api.checkPhoneExists(value)
    if (data.exists) {
      return Promise.reject('该手机号已被注册')
    }
    return Promise.resolve()
  } catch (error) {
    return Promise.reject('校验失败,请稍后重试')
  }
}
```

```vue
<!-- SmartForm.vue - 智能表单组件示例 -->
<template>
  <a-form
    ref="formRef"

          v-model:value="formState.price"
          :min="0.01"
          :max="999999.99"

          :min="0"
          :precision="2"

        />
      </a-form-item>

      <a-table
        :columns="skuColumns"
        :data-source="formState.skuList"
        :pagination="false"
        bordered
        size="middle"
      >
        <template #bodyCell="{ column, record, index }">
          <!-- 价格输入 -->
          <template v-if="column.key === 'price'">
            <a-form-item 
              :name="['skuList', index, 'price']"
              :rules="[{ required: true, validator: validatePrice }]"
              :style="{ marginBottom: 0 }"
            >
              <a-input-number
                v-model:value="record.price"
                :min="0.01"
                :precision="2"
                size="small"
                style="width: 100%"
              />
            </a-form-item>
          </template>

          <!-- 库存输入 -->
          <template v-if="column.key === 'stock'">
            <a-form-item 
              :name="['skuList', index, 'stock']"
              :rules="[{ required: true, validator: validateStock }]"
              :style="{ marginBottom: 0 }"
            >
              <a-input-number
                v-model:value="record.stock"
                :min="0"
                :max="999999"
                size="small"
                style="width: 100%"
              />
            </a-form-item>
          </template>

          <!-- SKU编码 -->
          <template v-if="column.key === 'skuCode'">
            <a-input
              v-model:value="record.skuCode"
              size="small"
              placeholder="SKU编码"
            />
          </template>

          <!-- 操作 -->
          <template v-if="column.key === 'action'">
            <a-button 
              type="link" 
              danger 
              size="small"
              @click="removeSku(index)"
            >
              删除
            </a-button>
          </template>
        </template>
      </a-table>

      <a-button type="dashed" block @click="addSku">
        <PlusOutlined /> 添加SKU规格
      </a-button>
    </a-card>

    <!-- 提交按钮 -->
    <div class="form-actions">
      <a-button size="large" @click="handleReset">重置</a-button>
      <a-button 
        type="primary" 
        size="large" 
        html-type="submit"
        :loading="submitting"
      >
        {{ isEdit ? '保存修改' : '创建商品' }}
      </a-button>
    </div>
  </a-form>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, reactive } from 'vue'
import { ElMessage } from 'element-plus'
import { validatePrice, validateStock, validateProductName } from '@/utils/formValidators'

const formRef = ref()
const submitting = ref(false)

const formState = reactive({
  name: '',
  categoryId: undefined as number[] | undefined,
  price: undefined as number | undefined,
  originalPrice: undefined as number | undefined,
  skuList: [] as SkuItem[]
})

const formRules = {
  name: [{ required: true, validator: validateProductName }],
  categoryId: [{ required: true, message: '请选择商品分类' }],
  price: [{ required: true, validator: validatePrice }]
}

async function handleSubmit() {
  submitting.value = true
  try {
    await api.createProduct(formState)
    message.success('商品创建成功')
  } finally {
    submitting.value = false
  }
}
</script>

#### 6.1.4 无障碍访问支持

##### ARIA属性与键盘导航

```typescript
// utils/a11y.ts - 无障碍访问工具集

/**
 * Web无障碍(WCAG 2.1 AA标准)实施指南:
 * 
 * 1. 键盘导航: 所有可交互元素可通过Tab键访问
 * 2. 屏幕阅读器: ARIA属性正确标注
 * 3. 颜色对比度: 文字与背景对比度≥4.5:1
 * 4. 焦点指示器: 清晰可见的焦点样式
 * 5. 动画控制: 尊重prefers-reduced-motion偏好
 */

/**
 * 设置元素的ARIA属性
 */
export function setAriaAttributes(
  element: HTMLElement, 
  attributes: Record<string, string>
): void {
  Object.entries(attributes).forEach(([key, value]) => {
    element.setAttribute(`aria-${key}`, value)
  })
}

/**
 * 创建键盘可访问的自定义组件焦点陷阱
 */
export function createFocusTrap(container: HTMLElement): { activate: () => void; deactivate: () => void } {
  let previouslyFocused: HTMLElement | null = null
  
  function getFocusableElements(): HTMLElement[] {
    const selector = [
      'a[href]',
      'button:not([disabled])',
      'input:not([disabled])',
      'select:not([disabled])',
      'textarea:not([disabled])',
      '[tabindex]:not([tabindex="-1"])'
    ].join(', ')
    
    return Array.from(container.querySelectorAll(selector))
  }
  
  function handleKeyDown(e: KeyboardEvent) {
    if (e.key !== 'Tab') return
    
    const focusable = getFocusableElements()
    if (focusable.length === 0) return
    
    const firstElement = focusable[0]
    const lastElement = focusable[focusable.length - 1]
    
    if (e.shiftKey) {
      if (document.activeElement === firstElement) {
        e.preventDefault()
        lastElement.focus()
      }
    } else {
      if (document.activeElement === lastElement) {
        e.preventDefault()
        firstElement.focus()
      }
    }
  }
  
  return {
    activate() {
      previouslyFocused = document.activeElement as HTMLElement
      container.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown)
      const firstFocusable = getFocusableElements()[0]
      firstFocusable?.focus()
    },
    deactivate() {
      container.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown)
      previouslyFocused?.focus()
    }
  }
}

/**
 * 检测用户是否偏好减少动画
 */
export function prefersReducedMotion(): boolean {
  return window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches
}

/**
 * 为屏幕阅读器播报实时更新
 */
export function announceToScreenReader(message: string, priority: 'polite' | 'assertive' = 'polite'): void {
  const announcement = document.createElement('div')
  announcement.setAttribute('role', 'status')
  announcement.setAttribute('aria-live', priority)
  announcement.setAttribute('aria-atomic', 'true')
  announcement.className = 'sr-only'
  announcement.textContent = message
  
  document.body.appendChild(announcement)
  
  // 移除旧的通知区域
  setTimeout(() => {
    document.body.removeChild(announcement)
  }, 1000)
}
```

```vue
<!-- AccessibleProductCard.vue - 无障碍商品卡片组件 -->
<template>
  <article 
    class="product-card accessible"
    role="article"
    aria-labelledby="product-name"
    tabindex="0"
    @keydown.enter="handleClick"
    @keydown.space.prevent="handleClick"
  >
    <!-- 商品图片区域 -->
    <div class="card-image-wrapper" role="img" :aria-label="`${product.name}的商品图片`">
      <img
        :src="product.mainImage"
        :alt="product.name"
        loading="lazy"
        @error="onImageError"
      />
      
      <!-- 商品标签(如:新品/热销/折扣) -->
      <div class="card-badges" aria-label="商品标签">
        <span 
          v-for="badge in product.badges" 
          :key="badge.type"
          class="badge"
          :class="[`badge-${badge.type}`]"
          role="status"
        >
          {{ badge.text }}
        </span>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 商品信息区域 -->
    <div class="card-content">
      <!-- 商品名称 -->
      <h3 id="product-name" class="card-title">
        <a 
          :href="`/product/${product.id}`"
          @click.prevent="handleClick"
          :aria-label="`查看${product.name}详情`"
        >
          {{ product.name }}
        </a>
      </h3>
      
      <!-- 商品副标题/描述 -->
      <p v-if="product.subtitle" class="card-subtitle" aria-hidden="true">
        {{ product.subtitle }}
      </p>
      
      <!-- 价格信息(语义化标记) -->
      <div class="card-price" role="group" aria-label="价格信息">
        <span class="current-price" aria-label="售价{{ product.price }}元">
          <span class="currency">¥</span>{{ product.price.toFixed(2) }}
        </span>
        
        <del 
          v-if="product.originalPrice > product.price" 
          class="original-price"
          aria-label="原价{{ product.originalPrice }}元"
        >
          ¥{{ product.originalPrice.toFixed(2) }}
        </del>
        
        <span 
          v-if="discountPercent > 0" 
          class="discount-tag"
          role="status"
          :aria-label="`优惠${discountPercent}折`"
        >
          {{ discountPercent }}折
        </span>
      </div>
      
      <!-- 销量/评价信息 -->
      <div class="card-meta" aria-label="商品统计">
        <span class="sales-count">已售 {{ formatSales(product.salesCount) }}</span>
        <span class="rating" :aria-label="`评分${product.rating}星`">
          <StarFilled v-for="i in 5" :key="i" 
            :class="{ filled: i <= Math.round(product.rating) }"
          />
        </span>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 快捷操作按钮(屏幕阅读器可访问) -->
    <div class="card-actions" aria-label="快捷操作">
      <button
        class="action-btn btn-cart"
        aria-label="加入购物车"
        @click.stop="handleAddCart"
      >
        <ShoppingCartOutlined />
      </button>
      <button
        class="action-btn btn-favorite"
        :aria-label="isFavorite ? '从收藏夹移除' : '添加到收藏'"
        :aria-pressed="isFavorite"
        @click.stop="toggleFavorite"
      >
        <HeartOutlined v-if="!isFavorite" />
        <HeartFilled v-else />
      </button>
      <button
        class="action-btn btn-compare"
        aria-label="加入对比"
        @click.stop="handleCompare"
      >
        <SwapOutlined />
      </button>
    </div>
  </article>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { computed } from 'vue'
import { announceToScreenReader } from '@/utils/a11y'

const props = defineProps<{ product: ProductDTO }>()
const emit = defineEmits(['click', 'add-cart', 'toggle-favorite', 'compare'])

const isFavorite = ref(false)

const discountPercent = computed(() => {
  if (!props.product.originalPrice) return 0
  return Math.round((props.product.price / props.product.originalPrice) * 10)
})

function handleClick() {
  emit('click', props.product.id)
  announceToScreenReader(`正在打开${props.product.name}详情页`)
}

function handleAddCart() {
  emit('add-cart', props.product.id)
  announceToScreenReader(`已将${props.product.name}加入购物车`)
}

function toggleFavorite() {
  isFavorite.value = !isFavorite.value
  emit('toggle-favorite', { productId: props.product.id, favorite: isFavorite.value })
  announceToScreenReader(
    isFavorite.value ? `已收藏${props.product.name}` : `已取消收藏${props.product.name}`
  )
}
</script>

<style scoped>
/* 屏幕阅读器专用样式(视觉隐藏但可被屏幕阅读器读取) */
.sr-only {
  position: absolute;
  width: 1px;
  height: 1px;
  padding: 0;
  margin: -1px;
  overflow: hidden;
  clip: rect(0, 0, 0, 0);
  white-space: nowrap;
  border-width: 0;
}

/* 清晰的焦点指示器(满足WCAG 2.4.7) */
.product-card.accessible:focus-visible {
  outline: 2px solid #1890FF;
  outline-offset: 2px;
  border-radius: 8px;
}

/* 高对比度模式支持 */
@media (forced-colors: active) {
  .product-card {
    border: 1px solid CanvasText;
  }
  
  .btn-cart::after {
    content: ' 加入购物车';
  }
}
</style>

### 6.2 核心业务流程简化

#### 6.2.1 商品浏览流程优化

##### 搜索体验增强方案

```typescript
// services/searchService.ts - 智能搜索服务

/**
 * Tailor IS 搜索功能特性:
 * 
 * 1. 即时搜索建议(输入时实时返回)
 * 2. 搜索历史记录(本地存储)
 * 3. 热门搜索推荐(运营配置)
 * 4. 搜索结果筛选(多维组合)
 * 5. 搜索结果排序(多维度)
 */

interface SearchSuggestion {
  keyword: string
  type: 'keyword' | 'category' | 'brand' | 'product'
  count?: number  // 匹配结果数量
  highlight?: string  // 高亮关键词部分
}

interface SearchHistoryItem {
  keyword: string
  searchTime: number
  resultCount?: number
}

class SearchService {
  private readonly HISTORY_KEY = 'tailoris_search_history'
  private readonly MAX_HISTORY = 20
  
  /**
   * 获取搜索建议(防抖处理)
   */
  async getSuggestions(keyword: string): Promise<SearchSuggestion[]> {
    if (!keyword || keyword.trim().length < 1) {
      return []
    }
    
    // 防抖: 300ms内只请求一次
    return debounce(async () => {
      const { data } = await api.getSearchSuggestions(keyword)
      return data.map(item => ({
        ...item,
        highlight: this.highlightKeyword(item.keyword, keyword)
      }))
    }, 300)()
  }
  
  /**
   * 添加搜索历史
   */
  addHistory(keyword: string, resultCount?: number): void {
    const histories = this.getHistories()
    
    // 移除重复项
    const filtered = histories.filter(h => h.keyword !== keyword)
    
    // 添加到头部
    filtered.unshift({
      keyword: keyword.trim(),
      searchTime: Date.now(),
      resultCount
    })
    
    // 限制数量
    const trimmed = filtered.slice(0, this.MAX_HISTORY)
    
    localStorage.setItem(this.HISTORY_KEY, JSON.stringify(trimmed))
  }
  
  /**
   * 获取搜索历史
   */
  getHistories(): SearchHistoryItem[] {
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(this.HISTORY_KEY)
      return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : []
    } catch {
      return []
    }
  }
  
  /**
   * 清除搜索历史
   */
  clearHistories(): void {
    localStorage.removeItem(this.HISTORY_KEY)
  }
  
  /**
   * 删除单条历史记录
   */
  removeHistory(keyword: string): void {
    const histories = this.getHistories().filter(h => h.keyword !== keyword)
    localStorage.setItem(this.HISTORY_KEY, JSON.stringify(histories))
  }
  
  /**
   * 关键词高亮处理
   */
  private highlightKeyword(text: string, keyword: string): string {
    const escaped = keyword.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&')
    const regex = new RegExp(`(${escaped})`, 'gi')
    return text.replace(regex, '<mark>$1</mark>')
  }
}

export const searchService = new SearchService()
```

```vue
<!-- SmartSearchBar.vue - 智能搜索栏组件 -->
<template>
  <div class="smart-search-bar" :class="{ focused: isFocused }">
    <div class="search-input-wrapper">
      <!-- 搜索图标 -->
      <SearchOutlined class="search-icon" />
      
      <!-- 搜索输入框 -->
      <input
        ref="inputRef"
        v-model="searchKeyword"
        type="search"
        class="search-input"
        :placeholder="placeholder"
        autocomplete="off"
        autocorrect="off"
        spellcheck="false"
        aria-label="搜索商品"
        aria-autocomplete="list"
        aria-controls="search-suggestions"
        aria-expanded="showSuggestions"
        @focus="handleFocus"
        @blur="handleBlur"
        @input="handleInput"
        @keydown.enter="handleSearch"
        @keydown.down="navigateSuggestion('down')"
        @keydown.up="navigateSuggestion('up')"
        @keydown.escape="closeSuggestions"
      />
      
      <!-- 清除按钮 -->
      <button 
        v-if="searchKeyword" 
        class="clear-btn"
        aria-label="清除搜索内容"
        @click="clearSearch"
      >
        <CloseCircleFilled />
      </button>
      
      <!-- 搜索按钮 -->
      <button class="search-btn" @click="handleSearch">
        搜索
      </button>
    </div>
    
    <!-- 搜索建议下拉面板 -->
    <Transition name="slide-down">
      <div 
        v-if="showSuggestions" 
        id="search-suggestions"
        class="suggestions-panel"
        role="listbox"
        :aria-label="`搜索建议,共${suggestions.length}条`}"
      >
        <!-- 搜索历史 -->
        <div v-if="!searchKeyword && searchHistories.length > 0" class="section history-section">
          <div class="section-header">
            <span class="section-title">搜索历史</span>
            <button class="clear-history" @click="clearHistories">清空</button>
          </div>
          <ul role="listbox">
            <li
              v-for="(item, index) in searchHistories.slice(0, 8)"
              :key="item.keyword"
              role="option"
              :aria-selected="activeIndex === index"
              :class="{ active: activeIndex === index }"
              @mousedown.prevent="selectHistory(item.keyword)"
            >
              <ClockCircleOutlined class="history-icon" />
              <span v-html="item.keyword"></span>
              <button 
                class="delete-history" 
                aria-label="删除此条历史"
                @click.stop="removeHistory(item.keyword)"
              >
                <CloseOutlined />
              </button>
            </li>
          </ul>
        </div>
        
        <!-- 热门搜索(无输入时显示) -->
        <div v-if="!searchKeyword && hotKeywords.length > 0" class="section hot-section">
          <div class="section-header">
            <span class="section-title">热门搜索</span>
          </div>
          <div class="hot-keywords">
            <a
              v-for="(kw, index) in hotKeywords"
              :key="index"
              class="hot-tag"
              :class="{ [`rank-${index + 1}`]: index < 3 }"
              @click="selectHotKeyword(kw)"
            >
              {{ kw }}
            </a>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <!-- 搜索建议(有输入时显示) -->
        <div v-if="searchKeyword && suggestions.length > 0" class="section suggest-section">
          <ul role="listbox">
            <li
              v-for="(item, index) in suggestions"
              :key="item.type + item.keyword"
              role="option"
              :aria-selected="activeIndex === index"
              :class="['suggest-item', item.type, { active: activeIndex === index }]"
              @mousedown.prevent="selectSuggestion(item)"
            >
              <component :is="getSuggestionIcon(item.type)" class="item-icon" />
              <span v-html="item.highlight || item.keyword"></span>
              <span v-if="item.count" class="item-count">
                约{{ formatCount(item.count) }}个结果
              </span>
            </li>
          </ul>
          
          <!-- 查看全部结果入口 -->
          <div class="view-all" @click="handleSearch">
            查看「{{ searchKeyword }}」的全部结果
            <RightOutlined />
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <!-- 无结果提示 -->
        <div v-if="searchKeyword && suggestions.length === 0 && !isLoading" class="no-result">
          <p>未找到相关建议</p>
          <p class="tip">试试其他关键词或浏览分类</p>
        </div>
        
        <!-- 加载状态 -->
        <div v-if="isLoading" class="loading-suggestions">
          <a-spin size="small" />
          <span>正在搜索...</span>
        </div>
      </div>
    </Transition>
  </div>
</template>
```

#### 6.2.2 下购支付流程简化

##### 结算流程优化设计

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│              Tailor IS 优化后结算流程                              │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  ┌──────┐    ┌──────┐    ┌──────┐    ┌──────┐    ┌──────┐     │
│  │ 购物车 │ →  │ 确认  │ →  │ 选择  │ →  │ 支付  │ →  │ 完成  │     │
│  │ (编辑) │    │ 订单  │    │ 地址  │    │ 方式  │    │ 页面  │     │
│  └──────┘    └──────┘    └──────┘    └──────┘    └──────┘     │
│     ↑           ↓                                                    │
│     └──── 返回修改 ──┘                                               │
│                                                                 │
│  优化要点:                                                       │
│  ✅ 步骤精简: 从7步减少到5步                                      │
│  ✅ 单页结算: 确认订单+地址+支付在同一页面完成                     │
│  ✅ 智能填充: 自动识别常用地址/支付方式                           │
│  ✅ 实时计算: 优惠券/运费/积分实时联动                            │
│  ✅ 断点续传: 未完成订单可随时恢复继续支付                        │
│                                                                 │
│  参考系统问题:                                                   │
│  ❌ 步骤过多(7步): 购物车→填写地址→选择物流→确认订单→           │
│                   选择优惠券→选择支付→支付确认→完成              │
│  ❌ 页面跳转频繁,每步都需重新加载                                 │
│  ❌ 无法中途返回修改而不丢失数据                                  │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

```typescript
// composables/useCheckout.ts - 结算流程管理Hook
import { ref, reactive, computed } from 'vue'
import { useRouter } from 'vue-router'
import { ElMessage } from 'element-plus'

interface CheckoutState {
  // 选中的商品SKU
  items: CartItem[]
  
  // 收货地址
  selectedAddress: AddressDTO | null
  addressList: AddressDTO[]
  
  // 配送方式
  shippingMethod: string
  shippingFee: number
  
  // 优惠券
  selectedCoupon: CouponDTO | null
  availableCoupons: CouponDTO[]
  
  // 支付方式
  paymentMethod: 'alipay' | 'wechat' | 'unionpay' | 'balance'
  
  // 订单备注
  remark: string
  
  // 积分使用
  usePoints: number
  maxUsablePoints: number
  
  // 发票信息
  invoice: InvoiceInfo | null
}

interface PriceBreakdown {
  goodsTotal: number       // 商品总价
  shippingFee: number       // 运费
  couponDiscount: number    // 优惠券减免
  pointsDiscount: number    // 积分抵扣
  discountTotal: number     // 总优惠金额
  payableAmount: number     // 应付金额
}

export function useCheckout() {
  const router = useRouter()
  
  const state = reactive<CheckoutState>({
    items: [],
    selectedAddress: null,
    addressList: [],
    shippingMethod: 'express',
    shippingFee: 0,
    selectedCoupon: null,
    availableCoupons: [],
    paymentMethod: 'alipay',
    remark: '',
    usePoints: 0,
    maxUsablePoints: 0,
    invoice: null
  })
  
  const isLoading = ref(false)
  const isSubmitting = ref(false)

  // ==================== 价格计算 ====================
  
  const priceBreakdown = computed<PriceBreakdown>(() => {
    const goodsTotal = state.items.reduce(
      (sum, item) => sum + item.price * item.quantity, 
      0
    )
    
    let couponDiscount = 0
    if (state.selectedCoupon) {
      couponDiscount = calculateCouponDiscount(state.selectedCoupon, goodsTotal)
    }
    
    const pointsDiscount = Math.min(
      state.usePoints * 0.01,  // 100积分=1元
      goodsTotal * 0.3        // 积分最多抵扣30%
    )
    
    const discountTotal = couponDiscount + pointsDiscount
    const subtotal = goodsTotal - discountTotal
    const payableAmount = Math.max(subtotal + state.shippingFee, 0.01)
    
    return {
      goodsTotal,
      shippingFee: state.shippingFee,
      couponDiscount,
      pointsDiscount,
      discountTotal,
      payableAmount: Number(payableAmount.toFixed(2))
    }
  })

  // ==================== 流程步骤 ====================
  
  const currentStep = ref<'confirm' | 'payment' | 'result'>('confirm')
  
  /**
   * 下一步: 确认订单 → 支付
   */
  async function goToPayment(): Promise<boolean> {
    // 前置校验
    if (!validateCheckout()) {
      return false
    }
    
    isSubmitting.value = true
    try {
      // 1. 创建订单(预占库存)
      const { data: order } = await api.createOrder({
        items: state.items,
        addressId: state.selectedAddress!.id,
        couponId: state.selectedCoupon?.id,
        shippingMethod: state.shippingMethod,
        usePoints: state.usePoints,
        remark: state.remark,
        invoice: state.invoice
      })
      
      // 2. 跳转到支付步骤
      currentStep.value = 'payment'
      return true
      
    } catch (error) {
      message.error('创建订单失败,请重试')
      return false
    } finally {
      isSubmitting.value = false
    }
  }
  
  /**
   * 执行支付
   */
  async function executePayment(orderId: string): Promise<void> {
    isSubmitting.value = true
    try {
      const { data: payData } = await api.createPayment({
        orderId,
        paymentMethod: state.paymentMethod,
        amount: priceBreakdown.value.payableAmount
      })
      
      // 根据支付方式调起支付
      switch (state.paymentMethod) {
        case 'alipay':
          openAlipay(payData.form)
          break
        case 'wechat':
          callWechatPay(payData.params)
          break
        case 'unionpay':
          openUnionPay(payData.url)
          break
        case 'balance':
          await payWithBalance(orderId)
          break
      }
      
      // 监听支付结果(轮询/WebSocket)
      pollPaymentStatus(orderId)
      
    } catch (error) {
      message.error('发起支付失败')
    } finally {
      isSubmitting.value = false
    }
  }
  
  /**
   * 校验结算信息完整性
   */
  function validateCheckout(): boolean {
    if (state.items.length === 0) {
      message.warning('请先添加商品到购物车')
      return false
    }
    
    if (!state.selectedAddress) {
      message.warning('请选择收货地址')
      return false
    }
    
    if (!state.paymentMethod) {
      message.warning('请选择支付方式')
      return false
    }
    
    return true
  }
  
  // ... 其他方法实现
  
  return {
    state,
    priceBreakdown,
    currentStep,
    isLoading,
    isSubmitting,
    goToPayment,
    executePayment,
    validateCheckout
  }
}
```

#### 6.2.3 订单管理流程清晰化

##### 订单状态可视化

```typescript
// utils/orderStatus.ts - 订单状态机与可视化

/**
 * Tailor IS 订单状态定义
 * 
 * 状态流转图:
 * 
 * PENDING_PAYMENT → PAID → SHIPPED → DELIVERED → COMPLETED
 *       ↕                                    ↕
 *    CANCELLED                         (售后流程)
 *                                          ↕
 *                                   REFUNDING → REFUNDED
 */

export enum OrderStatus {
  PENDING_PAYMENT = 0,    // 待付款
  PAID = 10,              // 已付款
  SHIPPED = 20,           // 已发货
  DELIVERED = 30,         // 已送达
  COMPLETED = 40,         //已完成
  CANCELLED = -1,         // 已取消
  REFUNDING = -2,         // 退款中
  REFUNDED = -3           // 已退款
}

export interface OrderStatusConfig {
  status: OrderStatus
  label: string
  color: string
  bgColor: string
  icon: string
  description: string
  nextActions: OrderAction[]
  timelineText: string
}

export const ORDER_STATUS_MAP: Record<OrderStatus, OrderStatusConfig> = {
  [OrderStatus.PENDING_PAYMENT]: {
    status: OrderStatus.PENDING_PAYMENT,
    label: '待付款',
    color: '#FA8C16',
    bgColor: '#FFF7E6',
    icon: '⏳',
    description: '订单已创建,等待买家付款',
    nextActions: ['PAY', 'CANCEL'],
    timelineText: '等待买家付款'
  },
  [OrderStatus.PAID]: {
    status: OrderStatus.PAID,
    label: '已付款',
    color: '#1890FF',
    bgColor: '#E6F7FF',
    icon: '💰',
    description: '买家已付款,商家准备发货',
    nextActions: ['SHIP', 'REFUND'],
    timelineText: '买家已付款'
  },
  [OrderStatus.SHIPPED]: {
    status: OrderStatus.SHIPPED,
    label: '已发货',
    color: '#722ED1',
    bgColor: '#F9F0FF',
    icon: '🚚',
    description: '商品已发出,正在配送途中',
    nextActions: ['CONFIRM_RECEIVE', 'TRACK', 'REFUND'],
    timelineText: '商家已发货'
  },
  [OrderStatus.DELIVERED]: {
    status: OrderStatus.DELIVERED,
    label: '已送达',
    color: '#13C2C2',
    bgColor: '#E6FFFB',
    icon: '📦',
    description: '包裹已送达,等待确认收货',
    nextActions: ['CONFIRM_RECEIVE', 'REFUND'],
    timelineText: '包裹已送达'
  },
  [OrderStatus.COMPLETED]: {
    status: OrderStatus.COMPLETED,
    label: '已完成',
    color: '#52C41A',
    bgColor: '#F6FFED',
    icon: '✅',
    description: '交易成功完成',
    nextActions: ['REVIEW', 'BUY_AGAIN', 'AFTER_SALE'],
    timelineText: '交易完成'
  },
  [OrderStatus.CANCELLED]: {
    status: OrderStatus.CANCELLED,
    label: '已取消',
    color: '#8C8C8C',
    bgColor: '#FAFAFA',
    icon: '❌',
    description: '订单已取消',
    nextActions: ['DELETE', 'REORDER'],
    timelineText: '订单已取消'
  },
  [OrderStatus.REFUNDING]: {
    status: OrderStatus.REFUNDING,
    label: '退款中',
    color: '#FF4D4F',
    bgColor: '#FFF2F0',
    icon: '↩️',
    description: '退款申请处理中',
    nextActions: ['CANCEL_REFUND', 'CONTACT_SERVICE'],
    timelineText: '退款处理中'
  },
  [OrderStatus.REFUNDED]: {
    status: OrderStatus.REFUNDED,
    label: '已退款',
    color: '#FF4D4F',
    bgColor: '#FFF1F0',
    icon: '💸',
    description: '退款已完成',
    nextActions: ['DELETE', 'REORDER'],
    timelineText: '退款已完成'
  }
}

/**
 * 获取订单状态流转时间线数据
 */
export function getOrderTimeline(order: OrderDTO): TimelineItem[] {
  const timeline: TimelineItem[] = []
  
  // 基础时间线节点
  const baseNodes: Array<{ status: OrderStatus; field: keyof OrderDTO }> = [
    { status: OrderStatus.PENDING_PAYMENT, field: 'createTime' },
    { status: OrderStatus.PAID, field: 'paymentTime' },
    { status: OrderStatus.SHIPPED, field: 'shipTime' },
    { status: OrderStatus.DELIVERED, field: 'deliverTime' },
    { status: OrderStatus.COMPLETED, field: 'completeTime' },
  ]
  
  baseNodes.forEach(node => {
    const time = order[node.field]
    const config = ORDER_STATUS_MAP[node.status]
    
    // 判断该节点是否已完成
    const isCompleted = getStatusOrder(order.status) >= getStatusOrder(node.status)
    
    timeline.push({
      ...config,
      time: time ? formatDate(time) : undefined,
      isCurrent: order.status === node.status,
      isCompleted
    })
  })
  
  // 如果是取消/退款订单,添加特殊节点
  if (order.status === OrderStatus.CANCELLED && order.cancelTime) {
    timeline.push({
      ...ORDER_STATUS_MAP[OrderStatus.CANCELLED],
      time: formatDate(order.cancelTime),
      isCurrent: true,
      isCompleted: true
    })
  }
  
  return timeline
}

function getStatusOrder(status: OrderStatus): number {
  const orderMap: Record<OrderStatus, number> = {
    [OrderStatus.PENDING_PAYMENT]: 0,
    [OrderStatus.PAID]: 1,
    [OrderStatus.SHIPPED]: 2,
    [OrderStatus.DELIVERED]: 3,
    [OrderStatus.COMPLETED]: 4,
    [OrderStatus.CANCELLED]: -1,
    [OrderStatus.REFUNDING]: -2,
    [OrderStatus.REFUNDED]: -3
  }
  return orderMap[status] ?? -99
}
```

#### 6.2.4 新手引导与帮助系统

##### 引导组件实现

```vue
<!-- UserGuideTour.vue - 新手引导漫游组件 -->
<template>
  <div v-if="isVisible" class="guide-overlay">
    <!-- 遮罩层(突出显示目标元素) -->
    <svg class="highlight-mask" :style="{ pointerEvents: isActive ? 'auto' : 'none' }">
      <rect
        v-if="currentStep?.targetRect"
        :x="currentStep.targetRect.left - 8"
        :y="currentStep.targetRect.top - 8"
        :width="currentStep.targetRect.width + 16"
        :height="currentStep.targetRect.height + 16"
        rx="8"
        fill="rgba(0,0,0,0.05)"
        stroke="#1890FF"
        stroke-width="2"
      />
    </svg>
    
    <!-- 引导提示气泡 -->
    <Teleport to="body">
      <Transition name="guide-pop">
        <div 
          v-if="isActive && currentStep"
          class="guide-tooltip"
          :style="tooltipStyle"
          :class="[`position-${currentStep.position}`]"
        >
          <!-- 步骤指示器 -->
          <div class="step-indicator">
            <span class="step-current">{{ currentIndex + 1 }}</span>
            <span class="step-separator">/</span>
            <span class="step-total">{{ totalSteps }}</span>
          </div>
          
          <!-- 引导内容 -->
          <div class="guide-content">
            <!-- 可选: 图标/插图 -->
            <div v-if="currentStep.icon" class="guide-icon">
              <component :is="currentStep.icon" />
            </div>
            
            <h4 class="guide-title">{{ currentStep.title }}</h4>
            <p class="guide-description">{{ currentStep.description }}</p>
            
            <!-- 可选: 交互式演示 -->
            <div v-if="currentStep.interactive" class="guide-demo">
              <slot :name="`demo-${currentIndex}`" />
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <!-- 操作按钮 -->
          <div class="guide-actions">
            <button 
              v-if="canSkip" 
              class="btn-skip" 
              @click="skipGuide"
            >
              跳过引导
            </button>
            
            <div class="actions-right">
              <button 
                v-if="currentIndex > 0" 
                class="btn-prev" 
                @click="prevStep"
              >
                上一步
              </button>
              
              <button 
                v-if="currentIndex < totalSteps - 1" 
                class="btn-next btn-primary" 
                @click="nextStep"
              >
                下一步
              </button>
              
              <button 
                v-else 
                class="btn-next btn-primary" 
                @click="completeGuide"
              >
                开始使用
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <!-- 关闭按钮 -->
          <button class="btn-close" @click="closeGuide" aria-label="关闭引导">
            <CloseOutlined />
          </button>
        </div>
      </Transition>
    </Teleport>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
interface GuideStep {
  target: string  // CSS选择器或ref
  title: string
  description: string
  position: 'top' | 'bottom' | 'left' | 'right'
  icon?: Component
  interactive?: boolean
  beforeEnter?: () => Promise<void>  // 进入前钩子
  afterLeave?: () => void           // 离开后钩子
}

const props = withDefaults(defineProps<{
  steps: GuideStep[]
  storageKey?: string  // 用于记住是否已完成引导
  autoStart?: boolean
  canSkip?: boolean
  maskClickable?: boolean
}>(), {
  storageKey: 'tailoris_guide_completed',
  autoStart: false,
  canSkip: true,
  maskClickable: false
})
</script>
```

// ========================================

#### 6.3.2 断点设计与媒体查询管理

```typescript
// hooks/useResponsive.ts - 响应式状态管理Hook
import { ref, onMounted, onUnmounted, computed, watchEffect } from 'vue'

/**
 * 响应式断点常量(与SCSS变量保持同步)
 */
export const BREAKPOINTS = {
  xs: 0,
  sm: 480,
  md: 768,
  lg: 1024,
  xl: 1280,
  xxl: 1536
} as const

type BreakpointName = keyof typeof BREAKPOINTS

interface ResponsiveState {
  width: number
  height: number
  breakpoint: BreakpointName
  isMobile: boolean      // xs, sm
  isTablet: boolean      // md
  isDesktop: boolean     // lg+
  orientation: 'portrait' | 'landscape'
  isTouchDevice: boolean
  pixelRatio: number
}

export function useResponsive() {
  const state = ref<ResponsiveState>({
    width: 0,
    height: 0,
    breakpoint: 'xs',
    isMobile: false,
    isTablet: false,
    isDesktop: false,
    orientation: 'portrait',
    isTouchDevice: false,
    pixelRatio: 1
  })

  function updateState() {
    const width = window.innerWidth
    const height = window.innerHeight
    
    let breakpoint: BreakpointName = 'xs'
    for (const [name, value] of Object.entries(BREAKPOINTS).reverse()) {
      if (width >= value) {
        breakpoint = name as BreakpointName
        break
      }
    }
    
    state.value = {
      width,
      height,
      breakpoint,
      isMobile: width < BREAKPOINTS.md,
      isTablet: width >= BREAKPOINTS.md && width < BREAKPOINTS.lg,
      isDesktop: width >= BREAKPOINTS.lg,
      orientation: width > height ? 'landscape' : 'portrait',
      isTouchDevice: 'ontouchstart' in window || navigator.maxTouchPoints > 0,
      pixelRatio: window.devicePixelRatio || 1
    }
  }

  // 使用ResizeObserver(比resize事件更精确)
  let observer: ResizeObserver | null = null

  onMounted(() => {
    updateState()
    
    if ('ResizeObserver' in window) {
      observer = new ResizeObserver(updateState)
      observer.observe(document.documentElement)
    } else {
      window.addEventListener('resize', updateState)
      window.addEventListener('orientationchange', updateState)
    }
  })

  onUnmounted(() => {
    if (observer) {
      observer.disconnect()
    } else {
      window.removeEventListener('resize', updateState)
      window.removeEventListener('orientationchange', updateState)
    }
  })

  // 便捷计算属性
  const shouldCollapseSidebar = computed(() => state.value.isMobile)
  const shouldUseDrawerMenu = computed(() => state.value.isTablet)
  const shouldShowTopNav = computed(() => !state.value.isMobile)

  return {
    ...toRefs(state),
    shouldCollapseSidebar,
    shouldUseDrawerMenu,
    shouldShowTopNav
  }
}
```

#### 6.3.3 Element Plus响应式适配

```typescript
// config/elementResponsive.ts - Element Plus响应式配置
import type { ThemeConfig } from 'element-plus'

/**
 * Element Plus 响应式主题配置
 * 根据屏幕尺寸动态调整组件尺寸和间距
 */

export function getResponsiveTheme(breakpoint: BreakpointName): Partial<ThemeConfig> {
  const themes: Record<BreakpointName, Partial<ThemeConfig>> = {
    xs: {
      token: {
        borderRadius: 4,
        controlHeight: 32,
        inputPaddingVertical: 4,
        fontSize: 14,
        sizeStep: 4,        // 间距单位缩小
        sizeUnit: 4,        // 基础单元4px
        sizePopupArrow: 8,
      },
      components: {
        Button: {
          controlHeight: 32,
          paddingInline: 12,
        },
        Card: {
          paddingLG: 12,
          paddingMD: 8,
        },
        Table: {
          headerBg: '#fafafa',
          headerColor: '#262626',
          fontSize: 13,
          padding: 8,
          paddingContent: 8,
        },
        Menu: {
          itemHeight: 40,
          inlineIndent: 12,
          iconSize: 16,
        },
        Modal: {
          bodyPadding: 16,
          headerFontSize: 16,
        }
      }
    },
    sm: {
      token: {
        borderRadius: 6,
        controlHeight: 36,
      }
    },
    md: {
      token: {
        borderRadius: 6,
        controlHeight: 36,
        fontSize: 14,
      },
      components: {
        Table: {
          padding: 12,
          paddingContent: 12,
          fontSize: 14,
        },
        Card: {
          paddingLG: 20,
          paddingMD: 16,
        }
      }
    },
    lg: {
      token: {
        borderRadius: 6,
        controlHeight: 40,
        fontSize: 14,
      },
      components: {
        Button: {
          controlHeight: 40,
          paddingInline: 16,
        },
        Card: {
          paddingLG: 24,
        },
        Table: {
          padding: 16,
          paddingContent: 16,
        }
      }
    },
    xl: {
      token: {
        controlHeight: 40,
      }
    },
    xxl: {
      token: {
        borderRadius: 8,
        controlHeight: 40,
        fontSize: 15,
      }
    }
  }
  
  return themes[breakpoint] || themes.lg
}

/**
 * 响应式Grid配置
 * 根据断点调整Ant Design Grid的列数和间距
 */
export function getResponsiveGridConfig(breakpoint: BreakpointName) {
  const configs = {
    xs: { gutter: [8, 8], columns: 1, span: 24 },
    sm: { gutter: [12, 12], columns: 2, span: 12 },
    md: { gutter: [16, 16], columns: 2, span: 12 },
    lg: { gutter: [20, 20], columns: 3, span: 8 },
    xl: { gutter: [24, 24], columns: 4, span: 6 },
    xxl: { gutter: [24, 24], columns: 4, span: 6 }
  }
  
  return configs[breakpoint]
}
```

  /* 隐藏不需要打印的元素 */
  .no-print,
  nav,
  aside.sidebar,
  .app-header,
  .app-footer,
  .back-to-top,
  .floating-action-btn,
  .ad-banner,
  .cookie-banner {
    display: none !important;
  }

  /* 重置页面布局 */

    background: white !important;
    color: black !important;
    font-size: 12pt;
    line-height: 1.5;
  }

    content: " (" attr(href) ")";

    color: #666;

    content: "";
  }

  }

    page-break-inside: avoid;
  }

##### 暗黑模式完整实现

```typescript
// composables/useDarkMode.ts - 暗黑模式管理Hook

/**
 * Tailor IS 暗黑模式策略:
 * 
 * 1. 用户手动切换(优先级最高)
 * 2. 跟随系统偏好(prefers-color-scheme)
 * 3. 时间段自动切换(可选: 日间亮色/夜间暗色)
 * 
 * 存储位置: localStorage('tailoris_theme_mode')
 * CSS变量: 通过[data-theme="dark"]属性切换
 */

type ThemeMode = 'light' | 'dark' | 'auto'

export function useDarkMode() {
  const mode = ref<ThemeMode>((localStorage.getItem('tailoris_theme_mode') as ThemeMode) || 'auto')
  const isDark = ref(false)

  // 系统暗色偏好检测
  const systemPrefersDark = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)')
  
  /**
   * 应用主题
   */
  function applyTheme(dark: boolean) {
    isDark.value = dark
    
    const root = document.documentElement
    
    // 设置HTML属性(CSS变量通过此属性切换)
    root.setAttribute('data-theme', dark ? 'dark' : 'light')
    root.classList.toggle('dark', dark)
    
    // 更新meta theme-color(移动端浏览器地址栏颜色)
    let metaThemeColor = document.querySelector('meta[name="theme-color"]')
    if (!metaThemeColor) {
      metaThemeColor = document.createElement('meta')
      metaThemeColor.name = 'theme-color'
      document.head.appendChild(metaThemeColor)
    }
    metaThemeColor.setAttribute('content', dark ? '#141414' : '#ffffff')
    
    // 触发全局事件(供其他组件监听)
    window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('theme-change', { detail: { isDark: dark } }))
    
    // 同步Element Plus主题(如果使用)
    if (window.__ELEMENT_PLUS_CONFIG__) {
      window.__ELEMENT_PLUS_CONFIG__.update({
        algorithm: dark ? theme.darkAlgorithm : theme.defaultAlgorithm
      })
    }
  }
  
  /**
   * 解析当前应该使用的主题
   */
  function resolveTheme(): boolean {
    if (mode.value === 'light') return false
    if (mode.value === 'dark') return true
    // auto模式: 跟随系统
    return systemPrefersDark.matches
  }
  
  /**
   * 切换主题
   */
  function toggleTheme() {
    mode.value = isDark.value ? 'light' : 'dark'
    localStorage.setItem('tailoris_theme_mode', mode.value)
    applyTheme(resolveTheme())
  }
  
  /**
   * 设置特定主题
   */
  function setTheme(newMode: ThemeMode) {
    mode.value = newMode
    localStorage.setItem('tailoris_theme_mode', newMode)
    applyTheme(resolveTheme())
  }

  // 初始化
  onMounted(() => {
    // 应用初始主题
    applyTheme(resolveTheme())
    
    // 监听系统主题变化
    systemPrefersDark.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
      if (mode.value === 'auto') {
        applyTheme(e.matches)
      }
    })
  })

  return {
    mode: readonly(mode),
    isDark: readonly(isDark),
    toggleTheme,
    setTheme
  }
}
```

```scss
// styles/themes/_dark.scss
// Tailor IS 暗黑模式CSS变量覆盖

/* 暗黑模式激活条件 */
[data-theme="dark"],
.dark {
  // ========================================
  // 背景色系(深色背景)
  // ========================================
  --color-background: #141414;
  --color-background-elevated: #1f1f1f;
  --color-background-overlay: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.65);
  
  // ========================================
  // 文字色系(浅色文字)
  // ========================================
  --color-text-primary: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.92);
  --color-text-secondary: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.68);
  --color-text-tertiary: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.45);
  --color-text-quaternary: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.22);
  
  // ========================================
  // 边框与分割线
  // ========================================
  --color-border: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.12);
  --color-border-secondary: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.08);
  --color-divider: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.06);
  
  // ========================================
  // 品牌色调整(降低饱和度/提高亮度)
  // ========================================
  --color-primary: #177ddc;        // 亮度微降
  --color-primary-hover: #3c9ae8;
  --color-primary-active: #0e5dab;
  --color-primary-bg: rgba(22, 125, 220, 0.15);
  
  // ========================================
  // 功能色调整
  // ========================================
  --color-success: #49aa19;
  --color-success-bg: rgba(73, 170, 25, 0.15);
  --color-warning: #d48806;
  --color-warning-bg: rgba(212, 136, 6, 0.15);
  --color-error: #d32029;
  --color-error-bg: rgba(211, 32, 41, 0.15);
  --color-info: #177ddc;
  --color-info-bg: rgba(22, 125, 220, 0.15);
  
  // ========================================
  // 阴影(暗黑模式下阴影更深)
  // ========================================
  --shadow-sm: 0 1px 2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3),
               0 1px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
               
  --shadow-md: 0 3px 6px -4px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.48),
               0 6px 16px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.32),
               0 9px 28px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2);
               
  --shadow-lg: 0 6px 16px -8px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.32),
               0 9px 28px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2),
               0 12px 48px 16px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.12);
  
  // ========================================
  // 卡片/容器背景
  // ========================================
  --card-background: #1f1f1f;
  --card-background-hover: #262626;
  --input-background: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.04);
  --input-background-hover: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.08);
  
  // ========================================
  // 滚动条(暗色风格)
  // ========================================
  &::-webkit-scrollbar {
    width: 8px;
    height: 8px;
  }
  
  &::-webkit-scrollbar-track {
    background: transparent;
  }
  
  &::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb {
    background: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.15);
    border-radius: 4px;
    
    &:hover {
      background: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.25);
    }
  }
}

/* 减少动画偏好(尊重用户设置) */
@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {
  *,
  *::before,
  *::after {
    animation-duration: 0.01ms !important;
    animation-iteration-count: 1 !important;
    transition-duration: 0.01ms !important;
  }
}

/* 高对比度模式支持 */
@media (forced-colors: active) {
  [data-theme="dark"] {
    --color-border: CanvasText;
    --color-text-primary: Canvas;
    --color-background: Canvas;
  }
}
```

##### 用户体验提升Checklist

```markdown
## 第六章 用户体验提升 - 实施Checklist

### 6.1 界面交互设计优化
- [ ] **设计系统建立**
  - [ ] 设计Token变量定义完成(颜色/间距/字体/圆角/阴影)
  - [ ] Tailor IS设计规范文档输出
  - [ ] 组件库样式统一(基于Design Token)
  
- [ ] **操作反馈机制**
  - [ ] 统一Toast/Notification/Modal反馈服务
  - [ ] Loading状态组件(全屏/局部/骨架屏)
  - [ ] 操作成功/失败/警告反馈标准化
  
- [ ] **表单体验**
  - [ ] 实时校验规则库建立(手机/密码/价格/SKU等)
  - [ ] 智能表单组件(自动填充/联想输入)
  - [ ] 错误提示友好化(具体原因+修复建议)
  
- [ ] **无障碍支持**
  - [ ] ARIA属性正确标注(角色/标签/状态)
  - [ ] 键盘导航全链路可达(Tab顺序合理)
  - [ ] 屏幕阅读器兼容测试(NVDA/JAWS/VoiceOver)
  - [ ] WCAG 2.1 AA标准合规审计

### 6.2 核心业务流程简化
- [ ] **商品浏览优化**
  - [ ] 智能搜索(即时建议/历史/热搜)
  - [ ] 多维筛选(分类/品牌/价格/属性)
  - [ ] 商品对比功能(参数对比/图片对比)
  
- [ ] **结算支付流程**
  - [ ] 步骤精简至5步以内
  - [ ] 单页结算(地址+支付同一页)
  - [ ] 多种支付方式(支付宝/微信/银联/余额)
  - [ ] 未完成订单恢复机制
  
- [ ] **订单管理清晰化**
  - [ ] 订单状态可视化(时间线/状态机)
  - [ ] 操作引导明确(每个状态可执行的操作)
  - [ ] 物流追踪集成(地图/轨迹)
  
- [ ] **新手引导系统**
  - [ ] 核心功能引导漫游(首次登录触发)
  - [ ] Tooltip帮助提示(关键操作点)
  - [ ] FAQ常见问题中心
  - [ ] 在线客服入口(悬浮/侧边栏)

### 6.3 响应式布局实现
- [ ] **布局系统**
  - [ ] Mobile First CSS Grid/Flexbox布局
  - [ ] 6档断点(xs/sm/md/lg/xl/xxl)全覆盖
  - [ ] useResponsive Hook集成使用
  
- [ ] **组件响应式**
  - [ ] Element Plus响应式主题配置
  - [ ] 导航菜单自适应(汉堡菜单/侧边抽屉)
  - [ ] 表格/列表移动端适配(卡片视图)
  
- [ ] **特殊模式支持**
  - [ ] 暗黑模式(手动/跟随系统/定时)
  - [ ] 打印样式优化(订单/发票/商品详情)
  - [ ] 高对比度模式兼容
  - [ ] 减少动画偏好支持
