# 第七章 测试体系保障

> **基于Spec需求10**: 建立覆盖单元测试、集成测试、E2E测试、性能测试、安全测试及UAT的完整测试体系,确保系统质量达到生产级标准。

## 7.1 单元测试规范

### 7.1.1 测试框架选型

| 组件 | 技术选型 | 版本 | 说明 |
|------|---------|------|------|
| **测试框架** | JUnit 5 | 5.10.x | 现代Java测试标准,支持嵌套测试/参数化 |
| **Mock框架** | Mockito | 5.x + MockitoExtension | 外部依赖Mock,隔离测试边界 |
| **断言库** | AssertJ | 3.25.x | 流式断言API,可读性强 |
| **覆盖率** | JaCoCo | 0.8.11 | 覆盖率收集与HTML报告生成 |
| **测试容器** | TestContainers | 1.19.x | 集成测试真实依赖启动 |

### 7.1.2 Maven依赖配置

```xml
<!-- pom.xml - 测试相关依赖 -->
<dependencies>
    <!-- JUnit 5 核心依赖 -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.junit.jupiter</groupId>
        <artifactId>junit-jupiter</artifactId>
        <scope>test</scope>
    </dependency>

    <!-- Mockito (JUnit 5扩展) -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.mockito</groupId>
        <artifactId>mockito-junit-jupiter</artifactId>
        <version>5.8.0</version>
        <scope>test</scope>
    </dependency>

    <!-- AssertJ 流式断言 -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.assertj</groupId>
        <artifactId>assertj-core</artifactId>
        <version>3.25.2</version>
        <scope>test</scope>
    </dependency>

    <!-- Spring Boot Test -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.springframework.boot</groupId>
        <artifactId>spring-boot-starter-test</artifactId>
        <scope>test</scope>
    </dependency>

    <!-- TestContainers (集成测试) -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.testcontainers</groupId>
        <artifactId>testcontainers</artifactId>
        <version>1.19.3</version>
        <scope>test</scope>
    </dependency>
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.testcontainers</groupId>
        <artifactId>junit-jupiter</artifactId>
        <version>1.19.3</version>
        <scope>test</scope>
    </dependency>
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.testcontainers</groupId>
        <artifactId>mysql</artifactId>
        <version>1.19.3</version>
        <scope>test</scope>
    </dependency>

    <!-- JsonPath (JSON断言) -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>com.jayway.jsonpath</groupId>
        <artifactId>json-path</artifactId>
        <scope>test</scope>
    </dependency>

    <!-- Awaitility (异步测试) -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.awaitility</groupId>
        <artifactId>awaitility</artifactId>
        <version>4.2.0</version>
        <scope>test</scope>
    </dependency>
</dependencies>

<!-- JaCoCo 覆盖率插件 -->
<plugin>
    <groupId>org.jacoco</groupId>
    <artifactId>jacoco-maven-plugin</artifactId>
    <version>0.8.11</version>
    <executions>
        <execution>
            <goals><goal>prepare-agent</goal></goals>
        </execution>
        <execution>
            <id>report</id>
            <phase>test</phase>
            <goals><goal>report</goal></goals>
        </execution>
        <execution>
            <id>check</id>
            <goals><goal>check</goal></goals>
            <configuration>
                <rules>
                    <rule>
                        <element>BUNDLE</element>
                        <limits>
                            <limit>
                                <counter>LINE</counter>
                                <value>COVEREDRATIO</value>
                                <minimum>0.90</minimum>
                            </limit>
                            <limit>
                                <counter>BRANCH</counter>
                                <value>COVEREDRATIO</value>
                                <minimum>0.85</minimum>
                            </limit>
                            <limit>
                                <counter>METHOD</counter>
                                <value>COVEREDRATIO</value>
                                <minimum>0.90</minimum>
                            </limit>
                            <limit>
                                <counter>CLASS</counter>
                                <value>COVEREDRATIO</value>
                                <minimum>0.95</minimum>
                            </limit>
                        </limits>
                    </rule>
                </rules>
            </configuration>
        </execution>
    </executions>
</plugin>
```

### 7.1.3 覆盖率目标 (Spec需求10.1)

| 指标类型 | 目标值 | 门禁规则 | 说明 |
|---------|--------|---------|------|
| **行覆盖率(Line)** | **≥90%** | 构建阻断 | 核心业务代码必须达标 |
| **分支覆盖率(Branch)** | **≥85%** | 构建告警 | if/else/switch全覆盖 |
| **方法覆盖率(Method)** | **≥90%** | 构建告警 | 公开API全部覆盖 |
| **类覆盖率(Class)** | **≥95%** | 构建告警 | 避免空壳测试类 |

### 7.1.4 测试命名规范

```
{TestedClass}Test.java          -- 测试类命名
{methodName}_{scenario}_{expectedResult}  -- 测试方法命名
```

**命名示例**:

| 方法名 | 场景 | 预期结果 | 完整测试方法名 |
|--------|------|---------|---------------|
| createProduct | 正常数据 | 返回成功 | `createProduct_withValidData_returnsSuccess` |
| createProduct | 价格为负 | 抛出异常 | `createProduct_withNegativePrice_throwsException` |
| findById | 存在的ID | 返回产品 | `findById_withExistingId_returnsProduct` |
| findById | 不存在的ID | 返回空 | `findById_withNonExistentId_returnsEmpty` |
| updateStock | 并发扣减 | 数据一致 | `updateStock_withConcurrentDeduction_maintainsConsistency` |

### 7.1.5 测试分类策略

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                   测试金字塔                          │
│                                                     │
│                    ▲                                 │
│                   ╱ ╲     E2E测试 (~5%)              │
│                  ╱   ╲   Playwright / Selenium       │
│                 ╱─────╲  全流程验证                    │
│                ╱       ╲                              │
│               ╱─────────╲  集成测试 (~15%)            │
│              ╱           ╲ TestContainers             │
│             ╱─────────────╲ 模块交互验证               │
│            ╱               ╲                           │
│           ╱─────────────────╲ 单元测试 (~80%)          │
│          ╱                   ╲ JUnit + Mockito         │
│         ────────────────────── 函数/方法级验证          │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**测试分类详情**:

| 分类 | 占比 | 执行频率 | 执行时间 | 负责人 |
|------|------|---------|---------|--------|
| **正常路径测试(Happy Path)** | 50% | 每次提交 | 秒级 | 开发者 |
| **边界条件测试(Boundary)** | 25% | 每次提交 | 秒级 | 开发者 |
| **异常场景测试(Exception)** | 20% | 每次提交 | 秒级 | 开发者 |
| **并发安全测试(Concurrency)** | 5% | 每日构建 | 分钟级 | 测试团队 |

### 7.1.6 Mock策略

**原则**: 所有外部依赖必须Mock,确保单元测试的隔离性和执行速度。

| 依赖类型 | Mock方式 | 工具 | 示例 |
|---------|----------|------|------|
| **数据库(MyBatis-Plus Mapper)** | @MockBean | Mockito | `@MockBean private ProductMapper productMapper;` |
| **消息队列(RabbitMQ)** | @MockBean | Mockito | `@MockBean private RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate;` |
| **Redis缓存** | @MockBean | Mockito | `@MockBean private RedisTemplate<String, Object> redisTemplate;` |
| **HTTP调用(RestTemplate/Feign)** | MockRestServiceServer | Spring | `mockServer.expect(requestTo(...))` |
| **文件存储(MinIO)** | @MockBean | Mockito | `@MockBean private MinioClient minioClient;` |
| **时间依赖(LocalDateTime)** | @MockitoStatic | Mockito | `try (var mocked = mockStatic(LocalDateTime.class))` |

### 7.1.7 Service层单元测试完整示例

```java
package com.tailoris.product.service;

import com.tailoris.common.exception.BusinessException;
import com.tailoris.product.dto.ProductCreateRequest;
import com.tailoris.product.dto.ProductVO;
import com.tailoris.product.entity.Product;
import com.tailoris.product.entity.ProductCategory;
import com.tailoris.product.mapper.ProductMapper;
import com.tailoris.product.mapper.ProductCategoryMapper;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.*;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtendWith;
import org.mockito.*;
import org.mockito.junit.jupiter.MockitoExtension;
import org.springframework.data.domain.Page;
import org.springframework.data.domain.PageRequest;

import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.util.*;

import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.*;
import static org.mockito.ArgumentMatchers.*;
import static org.mockito.Mockito.*;

@ExtendWith(MockitoExtension.class)
@DisplayName("ProductService - 商品服务单元测试")
class ProductServiceTest {

    @Mock
    private ProductMapper productMapper;

    @Mock
    private ProductCategoryMapper categoryMapper;

    @Mock
    private ProductCacheService cacheService;

    @InjectMocks
    private ProductServiceImpl productService;

    private ProductCreateRequest validRequest;
    private Product existingProduct;

    @BeforeEach
    void setUp() {
        validRequest = ProductCreateRequest.builder()
                .name("经典修身西装")
                .categoryId(100L)
                .price(new BigDecimal("1299.00"))
                .originalPrice(new BigDecimal("1999.00"))
                .stock(500)
                .description("高端商务正装系列")
                .build();

        existingProduct = Product.builder()
                .id(1L)
                .name("经典修身西装")
                .categoryId(100L)
                .price(new BigDecimal("1299.00"))
                .stock(500)
                .status(1)
                .createTime(LocalDateTime.now())
                .updateTime(LocalDateTime.now())
                .build();
    }

    // ==================== 正常路径测试 ====================

    @Nested
    @DisplayName("createProduct - 创建商品")
    class CreateProduct {

        @Test
        @DisplayName("✅ 有效数据创建商品成功")
        void createProduct_withValidData_returnsSuccess() {
            given(categoryMapper.selectById(100L))
                    .willReturn(new ProductCategory().setId(100L).setName("男装"));
            given(productMapper.insert(any(Product.class)))
                    .willReturn(1);

            ProductVO result = productService.createProduct(validRequest);

            assertThat(result).isNotNull();
            assertThat(result.getName()).isEqualTo("经典修身西装");
            assertThat(result.getPrice()).isEqualByComparingTo("1299.00");

            then(productMapper).should().insert(any(Product.class));
            then(cacheService).should().evictCategoryProducts(100L);
        }

        @Test
        @DisplayName("✅ 自动设置默认字段")
        void createProduct_autoSetsDefaultFields() {
            given(categoryMapper.selectById(anyLong())).willReturn(new ProductCategory());
            given(productMapper.insert(any(Product.class))).willReturn(1);

            productService.createProduct(validRequest);

            ArgumentCaptor<Product> captor = ArgumentCaptor.forClass(Product.class);
            then(productMapper).should().insert(captor.capture());

            Product saved = captor.getValue();
            assertThat(saved.getStatus()).isEqualTo(0); // 默认下架状态
            assertThat(saved.getSalesCount()).isEqualTo(0);
            assertThat(saved.getCreateTime()).isNotNull();
            assertThat(saved.getUpdateTime()).isNotNull();
        }
    }

    // ==================== 边界条件测试 ====================

    @Nested
    @DisplayName("边界条件测试")
    class BoundaryTests {

        @Test
        @DisplayName("📏 价格为0时创建失败")
        void createProduct_withZeroPrice_throwsException() {
            validRequest.setPrice(BigDecimal.ZERO);

            assertThatThrownBy(() -> productService.createProduct(validRequest))
                    .isInstanceOf(BusinessException.class)
                    .hasMessageContaining("价格必须大于0");
        }

        @Test
        @DisplayName("📏 库存为负数时创建失败")
        void createProduct_withNegativeStock_throwsException() {
            validRequest.setStock(-1);

            assertThatThrownBy(() -> productService.createProduct(validRequest))
                    .isInstanceOf(BusinessException.class)
                    .hasMessageContaining("库存不能为负数");
        }

        @Test
        @DisplayName("📏 商品名称超长(200字符)时截断处理")
        void createProduct_withLongName_truncatesName() {
            String longName = "a".repeat(300);
            validRequest.setName(longName);

            given(categoryMapper.selectById(anyLong())).willReturn(new ProductCategory());
            given(productMapper.insert(any(Product.class))).willReturn(1);

            ProductVO result = productService.createProduct(validRequest);

            assertThat(result.getName()).hasSize(200);
        }

        @Test
        @DisplayName("📏 分页查询第一页边界")
        void findPage_firstPageBoundary_correctResult() {
            Page<Product> mockPage = Page.empty();
            given(productMapper.selectPage(any(), any()))
                    .willReturn(mockPage);

            var result = productService.findPage(
                    ProductQuery.builder().build(),
                    PageRequest.of(0, 10));

            assertThat(result.getContent()).isEmpty();
            then(productMapper).should().selectPage(any(), any());
        }
    }

    // ==================== 异常场景测试 ====================

    @Nested
    @DisplayName("异常场景测试")
    class ExceptionTests {

        @Test
        @DisplayName("❌ 分类不存在时抛出异常")
        void createProduct_categoryNotFound_throwsException() {
            given(categoryMapper.selectById(999L)).willReturn(null);

            validRequest.setCategoryId(999L);

            assertThatThrownBy(() -> productService.createProduct(validRequest))
                    .isInstanceOf(BusinessException.class)
                    .hasMessageContaining("分类不存在");
        }

        @Test
        @DisplayName("❌ 数据库插入失败时抛出异常")
        void createProduct_dbInsertFailure_throwsException() {
            given(categoryMapper.selectById(anyLong())).willReturn(new ProductCategory());
            given(productMapper.insert(any(Product.class)))
                    .willReturn(0); // 插入0行表示失败

            assertThatThrownBy(() -> productService.createProduct(validRequest))
                    .isInstanceOf(BusinessException.class)
                    .hasMessageContaining("商品创建失败");
        }

        @Test
        @DisplayName("❌ 商品不存在时查询返回空")
        void findById_nonExistentId_returnsEmpty() {
            given(productMapper.selectById(999L)).willReturn(null);

            Optional<ProductVO> result = productService.findById(999L);

            assertThat(result).isEmpty();
        }
    }

    // ==================== 并发安全测试 ====================

    @Nested
    @DisplayName("并发安全测试")
    class ConcurrencyTests {

        @Test
        @DisplayName("🔄 并发扣减库存保持一致性")
        void deductStock_concurrentDeduction_maintainsConsistency() {
            int initialStock = 100;
            int concurrentRequests = 10;
            int deductAmount = 5;

            AtomicInteger remainingStock = new AtomicInteger(initialStock);

            ExecutorService executor = Executors.newFixedThreadPool(concurrentRequests);
            CountDownLatch latch = new CountDownLatch(concurrentRequests);
            AtomicInteger successCount = new AtomicInteger(0);
            List<Throwable> errors = new CopyOnWriteArrayList<>();

            given(productMapper.selectById(1L))
                    .willAnswer(invocation -> {
                        Product p = new Product();
                        p.setId(1L);
                        p.setStock(remainingStock.get());
                        return p;
                    });

            given(productMapper.updateById(any(Product.class)))
                    .willAnswer(invocation -> {
                        Product p = invocation.getArgument(0);
                        boolean success = remainingStock.compareAndSet(
                                p.getStock() + deductAmount,
                                p.getStock()
                        );
                        return success ? 1 : 0;
                    });

            for (int i = 0; i < concurrentRequests; i++) {
                executor.submit(() -> {
                    try {
                        latch.countDown();
                        latch.await();
                        productService.deductStock(1L, deductAmount);
                        successCount.incrementAndGet();
                    } catch (BusinessException e) {
                        // 库存不足是预期行为
                    } catch (Throwable t) {
                        errors.add(t);
                    }
                });
            }

            executor.shutdown();
            assertThat(executor.awaitTermination(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS)).isTrue();

            assertThat(errors).isEmpty();
            assertThat(successCount.get() + (initialStock - remainingStock.get()))
                    .isEqualTo(initialStock);
            assertThat(remainingStock.get()).isGreaterThanOrEqualTo(0);
        }
    }
}
```

### 7.1.8 Controller层单元测试示例

```java
package com.tailoris.product.controller;

import com.tailoris.common.result.Result;
import com.tailoris.product.dto.ProductCreateRequest;
import com.tailoris.product.dto.ProductVO;
import com.tailoris.product.service.ProductService;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.*;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.boot.test.autoconfigure.web.servlet.WebMvcTest;
import org.springframework.boot.test.mock.mockito.MockBean;
import org.springframework.http.MediaType;
import org.springframework.test.web.servlet.MockMvc;

import java.math.BigDecimal;

import static org.mockito.BDDMockito.*;
import static org.springframework.test.web.servlet.request.MockMvcRequestBuilders.*;
import static org.springframework.test.web.servlet.result.MockMvcResultMatchers.*;

@WebMvcTest(ProductController.class)
@DisplayName("ProductController - 商品控制器单元测试")
class ProductControllerTest {

    @Autowired
    private MockMvc mockMvc;

    @MockBean
    private ProductService productService;

    @Test
    @DisplayName("POST /api/v1/products - 创建商品成功返回201")
    void createProduct_success_returns201() throws Exception {
        ProductCreateRequest request = new ProductCreateRequest();
        request.setName("测试商品");
        request.setPrice(new BigDecimal("99.00"));

        ProductVO expectedVO = new ProductVO();
        expectedVO.setId(1L);
        expectedVO.setName("测试商品");

        given(productService.createProduct(any(ProductCreateRequest.class)))
                .willReturn(expectedVO);

        String jsonBody = """
                {
                    "name": "测试商品",
                    "price": 99.00,
                    "categoryId": 1,
                    "stock": 100
                }
                """;

        mockMvc.perform(post("/api/v1/products")
                        .contentType(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
                        .content(jsonBody))
                .andExpect(status().isOk())
                .andExpect(jsonPath("$.code").value(200))
                .andExpect(jsonPath("$.data.name").value("测试商品"))
                .andExpect(jsonPath("$.data.id").value(1));
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("GET /api/v1/products/{id} - 商品存在返回200")
    void getProduct_exists_returns200() throws Exception {
        ProductVO vo = new ProductVO();
        vo.setId(1L);
        vo.setName("存在的商品");

        given(productService.findById(1L)).willReturn(java.util.Optional.of(vo));

        mockMvc.perform(get("/api/v1/products/1"))
                .andExpect(status().isOk())
                .andExpect(jsonPath("$.data.name").value("存在的商品"));
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("GET /api/v1/products/{id} - 商品不存在返回404")
    void getProduct_notExists_returns404() throws Exception {
        given(productService.findById(999L)).willReturn(java.util.Optional.empty());

        mockMvc.perform(get("/api/v1/products/999"))
                .andExpect(status().isNotFound());
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("参数校验失败返回400")
    void createProduct_invalidInput_returns400() throws Exception {
        String invalidJson = """
                {
                    "name": "",
                    "price": -10
                }
                """;

        mockMvc.perform(post("/api/v1/products")
                        .contentType(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
                        .content(invalidJson))
                .andExpect(status().isBadRequest());
    }
}
```

---

## 7.2 集成测试

### 7.2.1 集成测试架构

```
┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                  集成测试环境 (TestContainers)           │
│                                                        │
│  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  ┌───────┐ │
│  │ MySQL    │  │ RabbitMQ │  │  Redis   │  │ MinIO │ │
│  │ :3306    │  │ :5672    │  │ :6379    │  │ :9000 │ │
│  └────┬─────┘  └────┬─────┘  └────┬─────┘  └───┬───┘ │
│       │              │             │             │     │
│  ┌────▼──────────────▼─────────────▼─────────────▼───┐ │
│  │            Spring Boot Application                 │ │
│  │  ┌─────────┐ ┌─────────┐ ┌─────────┐ ┌────────┐  │ │
│  │  │Product  │ │ Order   │ │ Payment │ │ User   │  │ │
│  │  │Service  │ │ Service │ │ Service │ │Service │  │ │
│  │  └─────────┘ └─────────┘ └─────────┘ └────────┘  │ │
│  └───────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                        │
│  ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│  │              JUnit 5 Test Runner                   │ │
│  │  @SpringBootTest + @Testcontainers                 │ │
│  └───────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 7.2.2 TestContainers基础配置

```java
package com.tailoris.config;

import org.springframework.boot.test.context.TestConfiguration;
import org.springframework.boot.testcontainers.service.connection.ServiceConnection;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
import org.springframework.test.context.DynamicPropertyRegistry;
import org.testcontainers.containers.GenericContainer;
import org.testcontainers.containers.MySQLContainer;
import org.testcontainers.containers.RabbitMQContainer;
import org.testcontainers.utility.DockerImageName;

@TestConfiguration
public class TestContainersConfig {

    @Bean
    @ServiceConnection
    public MySQLContainer<?> mysqlContainer() {
        return new MySQLContainer<>("mysql:8.0")
                .withDatabaseName("tailor_is_test")
                .withUsername("test_user")
                .withPassword("test_pass")
                .withInitScript("db/init-test.sql")
                .withReuse(true);
    }

    @Bean
    @ServiceConnection
    public RabbitMQContainer rabbitmqContainer() {
        return new RabbitMQContainer("rabbitmq:3.12-management")
                .withReuse(true);
    }

    @Bean
    public GenericContainer<?> redisContainer() {
        return new GenericContainer<>(DockerImageName.parse("redis:7-alpine"))
                .withExposedPorts(6379)
                .withReuse(true);
    }

    @Bean
    public GenericContainer<?> minioContainer() {
        return new GenericContainer<>(DockerImageName.parse("minio/minio:latest"))
                .withExposedPorts(9000, 9001)
                .withCommand("server /data --console-address ':9001'")
                .withEnv("MINIO_ROOT_USER", "minioadmin")
                .withEnv("MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD", "minioadmin")
                .withReuse(true);
    }
}
```

### 7.2.3 应用测试配置

```yaml
# src/test/resources/application-test.yml
spring:
  datasource:
    url: jdbc:tc:mysql:8.0:///tailor_is_test?TC_INITSCRIPT=db/init-test.sql
    username: test_user
    password: test_pass
    driver-class-name: org.testcontainers.jdbc.ContainerDatabaseDriver

  data:
    redis:
      host: localhost
      port: 6379

  rabbitmq:
    host: localhost
    port: 5672
    username: guest
    password: guest

  sql:
    init:
      mode: always

mybatis-plus:
  configuration:
    log-impl: org.apache.ibatis.logging.stdout.StdOutImpl

logging:
  level:
    com.tailoris: DEBUG
    org.springframework.transaction: DEBUG
```

### 7.2.4 OrderService集成测试完整示例

```java
package com.tailoris.order.service;

import com.tailoris.order.dto.OrderCreateRequest;
import com.tailoris.order.dto.OrderVO;
import com.tailoris.order.entity.Order;
import com.tailoris.order.entity.OrderItem;
import com.tailoris.order.enums.OrderStatus;
import com.tailoris.order.mapper.OrderMapper;
import com.tailoris.order.mapper.OrderItemMapper;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.*;
import org.springframework.amqp.rabbit.core.RabbitTemplate;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.boot.test.context.SpringBootTest;
import org.springframework.data.redis.core.StringRedisTemplate;
import org.springframework.test.context.ActiveProfiles;
import org.springframework.test.context.DynamicPropertyRegistry;
import org.springframework.test.context.DynamicPropertySource;
import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;
import org.testcontainers.containers.MySQLContainer;
import org.testcontainers.containers.RabbitMQContainer;
import org.testcontainers.junit.jupiter.Container;
import org.testcontainers.junit.jupiter.Testcontainers;

import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;

import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.*;
import static org.awaitility.Awaitility.*;
import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.*;

@SpringBootTest
@Testcontainers
@ActiveProfiles("test")
@Transactional
@DisplayName("OrderService - 订单服务集成测试")
class OrderServiceIntegrationTest {

    @Container
    static final MySQLContainer<?> mysql = new MySQLContainer<>("mysql:8.0")
            .withDatabaseName("tailor_order_test")
            .withInitScript("db/order-init.sql");

    @Container
    static final RabbitMQContainer rabbitMQ = new RabbitMQContainer("rabbitmq:3.12-management");

    @DynamicPropertySource
    static void configureProperties(DynamicPropertyRegistry registry) {
        registry.add("spring.datasource.url", mysql::getJdbcUrl);
        registry.add("spring.datasource.username", mysql::getUsername);
        registry.add("spring.datasource.password", mysql::getPassword);
        registry.add("spring.rabbitmq.host", rabbitMQ::getHost);
        registry.add("spring.rabbitmq.port", rabbitMQ::getAmqpPort);
    }

    @Autowired
    private OrderService orderService;

    @Autowired
    private OrderMapper orderMapper;

    @Autowired
    private OrderItemMapper orderItemMapper;

    @Autowired
    private RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate;

    @Autowired
    private StringRedisTemplate redisTemplate;

    // ==================== 订单创建集成测试 ====================

    @Test
    @DisplayName("✅ 完整订单创建流程 - DB+缓存+消息队列联动")
    void createOrder_fullFlow_dbAndCacheAndMQ() {
        OrderCreateRequest request = OrderCreateRequest.builder()
                .userId(1001L)
                .merchantId(2001L)
                .remark("尽快发货")
                .items(List.of(
                        new OrderItemRequest(1L, 2, new BigDecimal("1299.00")),
                        new OrderItemRequest(2L, 1, new BigDecimal("599.00"))
                ))
                .build();

        OrderVO order = orderService.createOrder(request);

        assertThat(order).isNotNull();
        assertThat(order.getOrderNo()).startsWith("TI");
        assertThat(order.getStatus()).isEqualTo(OrderStatus.PENDING_PAYMENT);
        assertThat(order.getTotalAmount())
                .isEqualByComparingTo("3197.00"); // 1299*2 + 599

        verifyDatabasePersistence(order.getId());
        verifyCacheConsistency(order.getOrderNo());
        verifyMessagePublished(order.getOrderNo());
    }

    private void verifyDatabasePersistence(Long orderId) {
        Order dbOrder = orderMapper.selectById(orderId);
        assertThat(dbOrder).isNotNull();
        assertThat(dbOrder.getStatus()).isEqualTo(OrderStatus.PENDING_PAYMENT);

        List<OrderItem> items = orderItemMapper.selectList(
                new QueryWrapper<OrderItem>().eq("order_id", orderId));
        assertThat(items).hasSize(2);
    }

    private void verifyCacheConsistency(String orderNo) {
        String cached = redisTemplate.opsForValue()
                .get("order:" + orderNo);
        assertThat(cached).isNotNull();
        assertThat(cached).contains(orderNo);
    }

    private void verifyMessagePublished(String orderNo) {
        await().atMost(5, TimeUnit.seconds)
                .untilAsserted(() -> {
                    String message = (String) rabbitTemplate
                            .receiveAndConvert("order.created.queue");
                    assertThat(message).contains(orderNo);
                });
    }

    // ==================== 订单状态流转测试 ====================

    @Test
    @DisplayName("✅ 订单状态机完整流转: 待支付→已支付→已发货→已完成")
    void orderStatusTransition_fullLifecycle() {
        OrderVO order = createSampleOrder();

        orderService.payOrder(order.getId(), "PAY_20260530001");
        Order afterPay = orderMapper.selectById(order.getId());
        assertThat(afterPay.getStatus()).isEqualTo(OrderStatus.PAID);

        orderService.shipOrder(order.getId(), "SF1234567890");
        Order afterShip = orderMapper.selectById(order.getId());
        assertThat(afterShip.getStatus()).isEqualTo(OrderStatus.SHIPPED);
        assertThat(afterShip.getLogisticsCompany()).isEqualTo("顺丰速运");
        assertThat(afterShip.getLogisticsNo()).isEqualTo("SF1234567890");

        orderService.completeOrder(order.getId());
        Order afterComplete = orderMapper.selectById(order.getId());
        assertThat(afterComplete.getStatus()).isEqualTo(OrderStatus.COMPLETED);
    }

    @Test
    @DisplayName("❌ 非法状态转换抛出异常")
    void invalidStatusTransition_throwsException() {
        OrderVO order = createSampleOrder();

        assertThatThrownBy(() -> orderService.shipOrder(order.getId(), "SF001"))
                .isInstanceOf(IllegalStateException.class)
                .hasMessageContaining("当前状态不允许发货操作");
    }

    // ==================== 并发订单测试 ====================

    @Test
    @DisplayName("🔄 高并发下单库存扣减一致性")
    void concurrentOrderCreation_stockConsistency() {
        int threadCount = 20;
        int quantityPerOrder = 2;
        Long productId = 100L;
        int initialStock = 100;

        ExecutorService executor = Executors.newFixedThreadPool(threadCount);
        CountDownLatch startLatch = new CountDownLatch(1);
        CountDownLatch doneLatch = new CountDownLatch(threadCount);
        AtomicInteger successCount = new AtomicInteger(0);

        for (int i = 0; i < threadCount; i++) {
            final Long userId = 1000L + i;
            executor.submit(() -> {
                try {
                    startLatch.await();
                    OrderCreateRequest req = OrderCreateRequest.builder()
                            .userId(userId)
                            .merchantId(2001L)
                            .items(List.of(
                                    new OrderItemRequest(productId, quantityPerOrder,
                                            new BigDecimal("100.00"))
                            ))
                            .build();
                    orderService.createOrder(req);
                    successCount.incrementAndGet();
                } catch (Exception e) {
                    // 库存不足为预期行为
                } finally {
                    doneLatch.countDown();
                }
            });
        }

        startLatch.countDown();
        assertThat(doneLatch.await(30, TimeUnit.SECONDS)).isTrue();
        executor.shutdown();

        int totalDeducted = successCount.get() * quantityPerOrder;
        int remainingStock = queryProductStock(productId);

        assertThat(totalDeducted + remainingStock)
                .as("库存扣减总量应等于初始库存")
                .isEqualTo(initialStock);
    }

    private int queryProductStock(Long productId) {
        return Integer.parseInt(
                Objects.requireNonNull(redisTemplate.opsForValue()
                        .get("product:stock:" + productId)));
    }

    private OrderVO createSampleOrder() {
        return orderService.createOrder(OrderCreateRequest.builder()
                .userId(1001L)
                .merchantId(2001L)
                .items(List.of(new OrderItemRequest(1L, 1, new BigDecimal("99.00"))))
                .build());
    }

    @AfterEach
    void cleanup() {
        redisTemplate.getConnectionFactory()
                .getConnection()
                .flushAll();
    }
}
```

### 7.2.5 集成测试Checklist

- [ ] **环境隔离**: 每个测试类独立容器实例,互不干扰
- [ ] **数据清理**: @Transactional自动回滚或@AfterEach手动清理
- [ ] **异步验证**: Awaitility等待MQ消息/缓存更新完成
- [ ] **并发安全**: 多线程模拟真实并发场景
- [ ] **性能基线**: 单个集成测试用例执行时间<5秒
- [ ] **端口冲突**: 使用随机端口避免CI环境冲突

---

## 7.3 系统测试(E2E)

### 7.3.1 E2E测试框架选型

| 维度 | Playwright | Cypress | Selenium |
|------|-----------|---------|----------|
| **浏览器支持** | Chromium/Firefox/WebKit | Chrome(Family) | 全浏览器 |
| **执行速度** | ⚡⚡⚡ 最快 | ⚡⚡ 快 | ⚡ 一般 |
| **自动等待** | ✅ 智能 | ✅ 智能 | ❌ 手动 |
| **并行执行** | ✅ 原生支持 | ✅ 支持 | ⚠️ 需Grid |
| **网络拦截** | ✅ 强大 | ✅ 支持 | ⚠️ 有限 |
| **移动端模拟** | ✅ 原生 | ⚠️ 有限 | ⚠️ Appium |
| **推荐度** | ★★★★★ | ★★★★☆ | ★★★☆☆ |

**结论**: 采用 **Playwright** 作为E2E测试框架。

### 7.3.2 项目初始化与配置

```bash
# 初始化Playwright项目
npm init playwright@latest

# 安装依赖
npm install -D @playwright/test
npx playwright install chromium firefox webkit
```

```typescript
// playwright.config.ts - Tailor IS E2E测试配置
import { defineConfig, devices } from '@playwright/test';

export default defineConfig({
  testDir: './e2e',
  fullyParallel: true,
  forbidOnly: !!process.env.CI,
  retries: process.env.CI ? 2 : 0,
  workers: process.env.CI ? 4 : undefined,
  reporter: [
    ['html', { open: 'never', outputFolder: 'playwright-report' }],
    ['junit', { outputFile: 'results/junit.xml' }],
  ],
  use: {
    baseURL: process.env.E2E_BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:8080',
    trace: 'on-first-retry',
    screenshot: 'only-on-failure',
    video: 'retain-on-failure',
  },
  projects: [
    {
      name: 'chromium',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Chrome'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'firefox',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Firefox'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'webkit',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Safari'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'mobile-chromium',
      use: { ...devices['Pixel 5'] },
    },
  ],
  webServer: {
    command: 'npm run dev',
    port: 3000,
    reuseExistingServer: !process.env.CI,
  },
});
```

### 7.3.3 测试数据工厂模式

```typescript
// e2e/helpers/TestDataFactory.ts - 测试数据工厂
import { faker } from '@faker-js/faker/locale/zh_CN';

export class UserDataFactory {
  static createValidUser(overrides?: Partial<UserData>): UserData {
    return {
      phone: faker.phone.number('138########'),
      password: 'Test@2026!',
      nickname: faker.person.firstName(),
      avatar: faker.image.avatar(),
      ...overrides,
    };
  }

  static createMerchantUser(): MerchantData {
    return {
      ...this.createValidUser(),
      merchantName: faker.company.name() + '服饰旗舰店',
      contactPerson: faker.person.fullName(),
      businessLicense: faker.string.uuid() + '.jpg',
      category: ['男装', '女装', '童装'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)],
    };
  }
}

export class ProductDataFactory {
  static createProduct(overrides?: Partial<ProductData>): ProductData {
    return {
      name: `${faker.commerce.productAdjective()}${faker.commerce.productMaterial()}${faker.commerce.product()}`,
      price: parseFloat(faker.commerce.price({ min: 99, max: 9999 })),
      originalPrice: parseFloat(faker.commerce.price({ min: 199, max: 19999 })),
      stock: faker.number.int({ min: 10, max: 999 }),
      description: faker.commerce.productDescription(),
      categoryId: faker.number.int({ min: 1, max: 50 }),
      images: Array.from({ length: 3 }, () => faker.image.url()),
      skuAttributes: {
        color: ['黑色', '白色', '藏青色'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)],
        size: ['S', 'M', 'L', 'XL', 'XXL'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)],
      },
      ...overrides,
    };
  }

  static createBulkProducts(count: number): ProductData[] {
    return Array.from({ length: count }, () => this.createProduct());
  }
}

export class OrderDataFactory {
  static createOrder(userId: number, products: ProductData[]): OrderInput {
    const items = products.map(p => ({
      productId: faker.number.int(),
      quantity: faker.number.int({ min: 1, max: 5 }),
      price: p.price,
      skuId: faker.string.uuid(),
    }));

    return {
      userId,
      items,
      address: {
        receiver: faker.person.fullName(),
        phone: faker.phone.number('138########'),
        province: faker.location.state(),
        city: faker.location.city(),
        district: faker.location.county(),
        detail: faker.location.streetAddress(),
        isDefault: true,
      },
      remark: faker.lorem.sentence(),
    };
  }
}
```

### 7.3.4 用户端全流程E2E测试

```typescript
// e2e/specs/user-full-flow.spec.ts - 用户全流程E2E测试
import { test, expect, Page } from '@playwright/test';
import { UserDataFactory, ProductDataFactory, OrderDataFactory } from '../helpers/TestDataFactory';

test.describe('用户端全流程 - 注册→登录→浏览→下单→支付', () => {

  let userPage: Page;
  const user = UserDataFactory.createValidUser();

  test.beforeAll(async ({ browser }) => {
    userPage = await browser.newPage();
  });

  test('步骤1: 用户注册 - 手机号+验证码', async () => {
    await userPage.goto('/register');

    await userPage.getByPlaceholder(/请输入手机号/).fill(user.phone);
    await userPage.getByRole('button', { name: /获取验证码/ }).click();

    await expect(userPage.locator('.countdown')).toContainText('60');

    const code = '123456';
    await userPage.fill('input[placeholder="验证码"]', code);
    await userPage.getByPlaceholder(/设置密码/).fill(user.password);
    await userPage.getByPlaceholder(/确认密码/).fill(user.password);
    await userPage.getByRole('checkbox').check({ force: true });
    await userPage.getByRole('button', { name: /注册/ }).click();

    await expect(userPage).toHaveURL(/\/register\/success/);
    await expect(userPage.locator('.success-message'))
        .toContainText('注册成功');
  });

  test('步骤2: 用户登录 - 密码登录', async () => {
    await userPage.goto('/login');

    await userPage.getByPlaceholder(/手机号/).fill(user.phone);
    await userPage.getByPlaceholder(/密码/).fill(user.password);
    await userPage.getByRole('button', { name: /登录/ }).click();

    await userPage.waitForLoadState('networkidle');
    await expect(userPage).toHaveURL(/\//);
    await expect(userPage.locator('.user-nickname'))
        .toContainText(user.nickname || user.phone.slice(0, 3));
  });

  test('步骤3: 浏览商品 - 搜索→筛选→查看详情', async () => {
    await userPage.goto('/products');

    await userPage.getByPlaceholder(/搜索商品/).fill('西装');
    await userPage.press('.search-input', 'Enter');
    await userPage.waitForSelector('.product-list');

    const firstProduct = userPage.locator('.product-card').first();
    await expect(firstProduct).toBeVisible();

    await firstProduct.click();
    await userPage.waitForLoadState('networkidle');

    await expect(userPage.locator('.product-detail-title')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(userPage.locator('.product-price')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(userPage.locator('.sku-selector')).toBeVisible();

    await userPage.locator('[data-color="黑色"]').click();
    await userPage.locator('[data-size="L"]').click();
    await expect(userPage.locator('.selected-sku-info')).toBeVisible();
  });

  test('步骤4: 加入购物车→结算→提交订单', async () => {
    await userPage.goto('/cart');

    const cartItems = userPage.locator('.cart-item');
    const count = await cartItems.count();
    expect(count).toBeGreaterThan(0);

    await userPage.getByRole('button', { name: /去结算/ }).click();
    await userPage.waitForLoadState('networkidle');

    await expect(userPage).toHaveURL(/\/checkout/);

    await expect(userPage.locator('.address-selector')).toBeVisible();
    await userPage.locator('.address-option').first().click();

    await userPage.getByRole('button', { name: /提交订单/ }).click();

    await userPage.waitForResponse('**/api/orders/**');
    await expect(userPage.locator('.order-success'))
        .toBeVisible({ timeout: 10000 });
  });

  test('步骤5: 支付流程 - 选择支付方式→模拟支付', async () => {
    const orderNo = await userPage.locator('.order-no').textContent();

    await userPage.getByRole('button', { name: /去支付/ }).click();
    await userPage.waitForLoadState('networkidle');

    await userPage.locator('.payment-method[data-type="alipay"]').click();
    await userPage.getByRole('button', { name: /确认支付/ }).click();

    await userPage.waitForResponse('**/api/payments/**', { timeout: 15000 });
    await expect(userPage.locator('.payment-success'))
        .toBeVisible({ timeout: 15000 });
  });

  test('步骤6: 订单管理 - 查看→确认收货→评价', async () => {
    await userPage.goto('/user/orders');

    const paidOrder = userPage.locator('.order-card[data-status="paid"]').first();
    await expect(paidOrder).toBeVisible({ timeout: 10000 });

    await paidOrder.locator('.btn-confirm-receive').click();
    await userPage.getByRole('button', { name: /确定/ }).click();

    await expect(userPage.locator('.toast-message'))
        .toContainText('确认收货成功');

    await userPage.goto('/user/orders?tab=completed');
    const completedOrder = userPage.locator('.order-card').first();
    await completedOrder.locator('.btn-review').click();

    await userPage.fill('.review-textarea', '质量很好,尺码标准,物流很快!');
    await userPage.locator('.star-rating .star[data-value="5"]').click();
    await userPage.getByRole('button', { name: /提交评价/ }).click();

    await expect(userPage.locator('.review-success-toast')).toBeVisible();
  });
});
```

### 7.3.5 商家端全流程E2E测试

```typescript
// e2e/specs/merchant-full-flow.spec.ts - 商家全流程E2E测试
import { test, expect } from '@playwright/test';
import { UserDataFactory, ProductDataFactory } from '../helpers/TestDataFactory';

test.describe('商家端全流程 - 入驻→上架→接单→提现', () => {
  const merchant = UserDataFactory.createMerchantUser();

  test.beforeEach(async ({ page }) => {
    await page.goto('/merchant/login');
    await page.fill('input[name="phone"]', merchant.phone);
    await page.fill('input[name="password"]', merchant.password);
    await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
    await page.waitForURL('/merchant/dashboard');
  });

  test('商家入驻资料填写与审核', async ({ page }) => {
    await page.goto('/merchant/onboarding');

    await page.fill('#merchantName', merchant.merchantName);
    await page.fill('#contactPerson', merchant.contactPerson);
    await page.selectOption('#category', merchant.category);

    const fileInput = page.locator('input[type="file"]');
    await fileInput.setInputFiles('./test-fixtures/license.jpg');

    await page.click('button[type="submit"]');

    await expect(page.locator('.submit-success'))
        .toContainText('入驻申请已提交');
  });

  test('商品上架 - 多SKU管理', async ({ page }) => {
    await page.goto('/merchant/products/create');

    const product = ProductDataFactory.createProduct({
      name: '2026春夏新款韩版修身小西装外套',
    });

    await page.fill('#productName', product.name);
    await page.fill('#price', String(product.price));
    await page.fill('#stock', String(product.stock));

    await page.selectOption('#category', String(product.categoryId));
    await page.fill('#description', product.description);

    for (const image of product.images) {
      const uploadInput = page.locator('.image-upload input[type="file"]');
      await uploadInput.setInputFiles(image);
    }

    await page.click('.add-sku-btn');

    const colors = ['黑色', '白色', '藏青色'];
    const sizes = ['S', 'M', 'L', 'XL'];

    for (const color of colors) {
      await page.click(`.color-option:text("${color}")`);
    }
    for (const size of sizes) {
      await page.click(`.size-option:text("${size}")`);
    }

    await page.click('button[type="submit"]:has-text("发布商品")');

    await expect(page.locator('.publish-success'))
        .toBeVisible({ timeout: 10000 });
  });

  test('订单处理 - 接单→发货→打印面单', async ({ page }) => {
    await page.goto('/merchant/orders?status=pending');

    const pendingOrders = page.locator('.order-row[data-status="pending"]');
    const orderCount = await pendingOrders.count();
    expect(orderCount).toBeGreaterThan(0);

    await pendingOrders.first().locator('.btn-accept').click();
    await page.click('.confirm-dialog button:has-text("确认接单")');

    await expect(page.locator('.accept-toast'))
        .toContainText('接单成功');

    await page.goto('/merchant/orders?status=accepted');
    const acceptedOrder = page.locator('.order-row').first();

    await acceptedOrder.locator('.btn-ship').click();
    await page.fill('#logisticsCompany', '顺丰速运');
    await page.fill('#logisticsNo', `SF${Date.now()}`);
    await page.click('.submit-ship-btn');

    await expect(page.locator('.ship-success'))
        .toContainText('发货成功');

    await acceptedOrder.locator('.btn-print-waybill').click();
    const printPopup = page.locator('.print-preview-modal');
    await expect(printPopup).toBeVisible();
    await expect(printPopup.locator('.waybill-content')).toBeVisible();
  });

  test('收益提现 - 申请→审核→到账', async ({ page }) => {
    await page.goto('/merchant/finance/withdraw');

    const balance = await page.locator('.available-balance').textContent();
    expect(parseFloat(balance?.replace(/[^\d.]/g, '') || '0')).toBeGreaterThan(0);

    await page.fill('#withdrawAmount', '100.00');
    await page.selectOption('#withdrawMethod', 'bank');
    await page.fill('#bankAccount', '6222021234567890123');
    await page.fill('#bankName', '工商银行');

    await page.click('button:has-text("申请提现")');

    await expect(page.locator('.withdraw-success'))
        .toContainText('提现申请已提交');
  });
});
```

import { test } from '@playwright/test';

test.describe.configure({ mode: 'parallel' as const });

test('并行测试用例1: 浏览商品列表', async ({ page }) => {
  await page.goto('/products');
  await expect(page.locator('.product-list')).toBeVisible();

test('并行测试用例2: 搜索功能验证', async ({ page }) => {

  await page.fill('.search-box', '连衣裙');
  await page.press('.search-box', 'Enter');

  await page.click('.category-nav >> text=男装');

});

---

## 7.4 性能测试

### 7.4.1 性能测试工具对比

| 工具 | 类型 | 语言 | 适用场景 | 学习成本 |
|------|------|------|---------|---------|
| **JMeter** | GUI+CLI | Java | 协议级压测,全面协议支持 | 中等 |
| **Gatling** | 代码驱动 | Scala | 高并发场景,DSL友好 | 中等 |
| **k6** | 代码驱动 | Go(JS) | 云原生,轻量高效 | 低 |
| **Locust** | 代码驱动 | Python | 分布式压测灵活 | 低 |

**推荐方案**: **k6** 用于日常性能基准测试,**JMeter** 用于正式性能验收。

### 7.4.2 性能指标要求 (Spec需求10.4)

| 指标 | 目标值 | 告警阈值 | P0/P1判定 |
|------|--------|---------|-----------|
| **平均响应时间(Avg RT)** | ≤200ms | >300ms | P1 |
| **P99响应时间** | ≤500ms | >800ms | P0 |
| **QPS(每秒查询数)** | ≥10,000 | <5,000 | P1 |
| **错误率(Error Rate)** | <0.1% | >1% | P0 |
| **TPS(每秒事务数)** | ≥3,000 | <1,000 | P1 |
| **CPU利用率** | <70% | >85% | P2 |
| **内存利用率** | <75% | >90% | P2 |
| **GC暂停时间** | <100ms | >500ms | P1 |

### 7.4.3 k6性能测试脚本示例

```javascript
// performance/k6-load-test.js - k6负载测试脚本
import http from 'k6/http';
import { check, sleep } from 'k6';
import { Rate, Trend, Counter } from 'k6/metrics';

// 自定义指标
const errorRate = new Rate('errors');
const responseTime = new Trend('response_time');
const requestCounter = new Counter('requests_total');

// 测试配置
export const options = {
  stages: [
    { duration: '2m', target: 100 },    // 预热: 逐步加到100用户
    { duration: '5m', target: 500 },    // 负载: 500并发用户
    { duration: '3m', target: 1000 },   // 加压: 1000并发
    { duration: '2m', target: 500 },    // 恢复: 降到500
    { duration: '1m', target: 0 },      // 冷却: 逐步停止
  ],
  thresholds: {
    http_req_duration: ['p(95)<300', 'p(99)<500'], // P95<300ms, P99<500ms
    errors: ['rate<0.001'],                         // 错误率<0.1%
  },
};

// 测试数据
const BASE_URL = __ENV.BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:8080';
const TEST_USERS = JSON.parse(open('./performance/test-users.json'));

export default function () {
  const user = TEST_USERS[__VU % TEST_USERS.length];

  // 步骤1: 用户登录
  const loginRes = http.post(`${BASE_URL}/api/v1/auth/login`, JSON.stringify({
    phone: user.phone,
    password: user.password,
  }), {
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    tags: { name: 'login' },
  });

  check(loginRes, {
    '登录状态200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    '响应体包含token': (r) => JSON.parse(r.body).data?.token !== undefined,
  });

  errorRate.add(loginRes.status !== 200);
  responseTime.add(loginRes.timings.duration);
  requestCounter.add(1);

  const token = JSON.parse(loginRes.body).data.token;
  const authHeaders = {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}`,
  };

  // 步骤2: 浏览商品列表(最频繁操作)
  const listRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/v1/products?page=1&size=20&sort=sales_desc`, {
    headers: authHeaders,
    tags: { name: 'product_list' },
  });

  check(listRes, {
    '商品列表200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    '列表数据非空': (r) => JSON.parse(r.body).data?.records?.length > 0,
  });

  errorRate.add(listRes.status !== 200);
  responseTime.add(listRes.timings.duration);
  requestCounter.add(1);

  // 步骤3: 商品详情(30%概率)
  if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
    const products = JSON.parse(listRes.body).data.records;
    if (products.length > 0) {
      const productId = products[Math.floor(Math.random() * products.length)].id;
      const detailRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/v1/products/${productId}`, {
        headers: authHeaders,
        tags: { name: 'product_detail' },
      });

      check(detailRes, { '商品详情200': (r) => r.status === 200 });
      errorRate.add(detailRes.status !== 200);
    }
  }

  // 步骤4: 搜索商品(20%概率)
  if (Math.random() < 0.2) {
    const keywords = ['西装', '连衣裙', '衬衫', 'T恤', '牛仔裤'];
    const keyword = keywords[Math.floor(Math.random() * keywords.length)];
    const searchRes = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/api/v1/products/search?keyword=${encodeURIComponent(keyword)}`, {
      headers: authHeaders,
      tags: { name: 'product_search' },
    });

    check(searchRes, { '搜索接口200': (r) => r.status === 200 });
    errorRate.add(searchRes.status !== 200);
  }

  sleep(Math.random() * 2 + 1); // 模拟用户思考时间1-3秒
}
```

### 7.4.5 性能测试执行流程

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                  性能测试执行流程                          │
│                                                         │
│  ┌──────────┐   ┌──────────┐   ┌──────────┐            │
│  │ 1.基准测试 │ → │ 2.负载测试 │ → │ 3.压力测试 │            │
│  │ 单用户RT  │   │ 逐步加压  │   │ 超出极限  │            │
│  │ QPS基线  │   │ 找拐点   │   │ 找崩溃点  │            │
│  └──────────┘   └──────────┘   └──────────┘            │
│       ↓              ↓              ↓                  │
│  ┌──────────┐   ┌──────────┐   ┌──────────┐            │
│  │ 4.稳定性  │ → │ 5.分析报告 │ → │ 6.优化迭代 │            │
│  │ 长时间运行 │   │ 瓶颈定位  │   │ 复测验证  │            │
│  │ 内存泄漏  │   │ 调优建议  │   │ 达标闭环  │            │
│  └──────────┘   └──────────┘   └──────────┘            │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 7.4.6 性能测试Checklist

- [ ] **基准测试**: 单用户各接口响应时间记录
- [ ] **负载测试**: 100/500/1000/5000并发逐级加压
- [ ] **压力测试**: 找到系统最大承载能力
- [ ] **稳定性测试**: 7×24小时持续运行无内存泄漏
- [ ] **资源监控**: CPU/内存/磁盘IO/网络IO全程监控
- [ ] **报告输出**: HTML报告含趋势图和瓶颈分析

---

## 7.5 安全测试

### 7.5.1 OWASP Top 10检测清单

| # | 漏洞类型 | 检测工具 | 检测方法 | 严重级别 |
|---|---------|---------|---------|---------|
| A01 | **访问控制失效** | Burp Suite | 越权测试(IDOR) | Critical |
| A02 | **加密机制失败** | SSL Labs | TLS配置检测 | High |
| A03 | **注入攻击** | sqlmap/XSStrike | SQL/XSS/命令注入 | Critical |
| A04 | **不安全设计** | 手工审查 | 业务逻辑漏洞 | High |
| A05 | **安全配置错误** | Nmap/Nikto | 配置扫描 | Medium |
| A06 | **易受攻击组件** | Dependency-Check/Snyk | 依赖漏洞扫描 | High |
| A07 | **身份认证失效** | Hydra | 弱口令爆破 | Critical |
| A08 | **软件和数据完整性失败** | 手工审查 | 供应链安全 | Medium |
| A09 | **安全日志不足** | ELK审计 | 日志完整性检查 | Low |
| A10 | **服务端请求伪造(SSRF)** | SSRFMap | SSRF检测 | High |

### 7.5.2 SQL注入测试(sqlmap)

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# security/sql-injection-test.sh - SQL注入自动化测试脚本

TARGET_BASE="http://localhost:8080/api/v1"
AUTH_TOKEN=$(curl -s -X POST "${TARGET_BASE}/auth/login" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"phone":"13800138000","password":"Test@2026!"}' \
  | jq -r '.data.token')

echo "=========================================="
echo "  Tailor IS SQL注入安全测试"
echo "  测试时间: $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"
echo "=========================================="

# 待测试的参数化接口列表
declare -a ENDPOINTS=(
  "/products?id=1"
  "/products/search?keyword=test"
  "/orders?id=1"
  "/users/profile?userId=1"
  "/categories?id=1"
)

for endpoint in "${ENDPOINTS[@]}"; do
  echo ""
  echo "[TEST] 测试接口: ${endpoint}"

  sqlmap -u "${TARGET_BASE}${endpoint}" \
    --headers="Authorization: Bearer ${AUTH_TOKEN}" \
    --level=3 \
    --risk=2 \
    --batch \
    --random-agent \
    --technique=BEUSTQ \
    --output-dir="./security/results/sqlmap_$(date +%Y%m%d)" \
    --tamper=space2comment,between \
    2>&1 | tee -a ./security/results/sqlmap_scan.log
done

echo ""
echo "=========================================="
echo "  SQL注入测试完成!"
echo "  详细报告: ./security/results/"
echo "=========================================="
```

### 7.5.3 XSS跨站脚本测试(XSStrike)

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# security/xss-test.sh - XSS自动化测试脚本

TARGET="http://localhost:8080"

echo "=========================================="
echo "  Tailor IS XSS安全测试"
echo "=========================================="

xsser -u "${TARGET}/products/search?keyword=XSS_PAYLOAD" \
  --payloads="<script>alert(1)</script>'\"><img src=x onerror=alert(1)>" \
  -c 50 \
  --Cw \
  --Ak \
  --auto \
  --threads 5 \
  --output "./security/results/xss_report_$(date +%Y%m%d).html"

echo "XSS测试报告已生成"
```

### 7.5.4 CSRF越权测试(Burp Suite)

```python
# security/csrf_test.py - CSRF越权测试脚本
import requests
import json

BASE_URL = "http://localhost:8080/api/v1"

def test_csrf_protection():
    """CSRF防护测试"""
    session = requests.Session()

    login_res = session.post(f"{BASE_URL}/auth/login", json={
        "phone": "13800138000",
        "password": "Test@2026!"
    })
    token = login_res.json()["data"]["token"]

    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}"}

    # 测试1: 无CSRF Token的写操作应被拒绝
    dangerous_operations = [
        ("POST", f"{BASE_URL}/products", {"name": "test"}),
        ("PUT", f"{BASE_URL}/users/profile", {"nickname": "hacked"}),
        ("DELETE", f"{BASE_URL}/cart/items/1", {}),
    ]

    print("=" * 50)
    print("CSRF保护测试结果:")
    print("=" * 50)

    for method, url, data in dangerous_operations:
        res = session.request(method, url, headers=headers, json=data)
        status = "✅ PASS" if res.status_code == 403 else "⚠️ NEED_CHECK"
        print(f"{method} {url}: [{res.status_code}] {status}")

def test_idor_vulnerability():
    """越权访问测试(IDOR)"""
    session = requests.Session()

    # User A登录
    session.post(f"{BASE_URL}/auth/login", json={
        "phone": "13800138000",
        "password": "Test@2026!"
    })
    token_a = session.json()["data"]["token"]

    # 尝试访问User B的订单
    b_order_id = 99999
    res = requests.get(f"{BASE_URL}/orders/{b_order_id}",
                       headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {token_a}"})

    print("\n" + "=" * 50)
    print("IDOR越权测试结果:")
    print("=" * 50)
    status = "✅ PASS(已拒绝)" if res.status_code == 403 or res.status_code == 404 else "❌ FAIL(存在越权)"
    print(f"User A访问User B订单: [{res.status_code}] {status}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_csrf_protection()
    test_idor_vulnerability()
```

### 7.5.5 依赖漏洞扫描

```xml
<!-- pom.xml - OWASP Dependency-Check插件配置 -->
<plugin>
    <groupId>org.owasp</groupId>
    <artifactId>dependency-check-maven</artifactId>
    <version>9.0.7</version>
    <configuration>
        <format>HTML,XML,JSON,JUNIT</format>
        <suppressionFile>${project.basedir}/owasp-suppressions.xml</suppressionFile>
        <failBuildOnCVSS>7</failBuildOnCVSS>
        <analysisTarget>${project.build.outputDirectory}</analysisTarget>
    </configuration>
    <executions>
        <execution>
            <goals><goal>check</goal></goals>
        </execution>
    </executions>
</plugin>
```

```yaml
# .github/workflows/security-scan.yml - Snyk安全扫描
name: Security Scan

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  schedule:
    - cron: '0 2 * * 1'  # 每周一凌晨2点

jobs:
  snyk-scan:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Run Snyk to check for vulnerabilities
        uses: snyk/actions/maven@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
        with:
          args: --severity-threshold=high

      - name: Upload Snyk results
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: snyk-report
          path: snyk-results.json

  dependency-check:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: OWASP Dependency Check
        uses: dependency-check/Dependency-Check_Action@main
        with:
          project: 'Tailor-IS'
          path: '.'
          format: 'HTML'
          out: 'reports'

      - name: Upload Dependency Check Report
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: dependency-check-report
          path: reports/*
```

### 7.5.6 安全扫描频率与门禁

| 扫描类型 | 频率 | 触发条件 | 门禁规则 | 责任人 |
|---------|------|---------|---------|--------|
| **SCA依赖扫描** | 每次PR | 代码提交 | 无Critical/High漏洞 | CI自动 |
| **SAST静态分析** | 每次PR | 代码提交 | SonarQube安全规则集通过 | CI自动 |
| **DAST动态扫描** | 每日 | 定时任务 | OWASP ZAP无High以上漏洞 | 安全团队 |
| **容器镜像扫描** | 每次构建 | Docker构建 | Trivy无CRITICAL漏洞 | CI自动 |
| **渗透测试** | 每季度 | 发布前 | 无Critical/High漏洞 | 第三方安全公司 |
| **合规审计** | 每年 | 年度评审 | 符合等级保护要求 | 合规团队 |

## 7.6 用户验收测试(UAT)

### 7.6.1 UAT环境准备

```yaml
# docker-compose.uat.yml - UAT环境一键部署
version: '3.8'

services:
  mysql-uat:
    image: mysql:8.0
    environment:
      MYSQL_DATABASE: tailor_is_uat
      MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD: ${UAT_DB_PASSWORD}
      MYSQL_CHARACTER_SET_SERVER: utf8mb4
      MYSQL_COLLATION_SERVER: utf8mb4_unicode_ci
    ports:
      - "3307:3306"
    volumes:
      - uat_mysql_data:/var/lib/mysql
      - ./uat-db/init:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d
    deploy:
      resources:
        limits:
          memory: 2G
          cpus: '1.0'

  redis-uat:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6380:6379"
    command: redis-server --requirepass ${UAT_REDIS_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - uat_redis_data:/data

  rabbitmq-uat:
    image: rabbitmq:3.12-management
    ports:
      - "5673:5672"
      - "15673:15672"
    environment:
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER: ${UAT_MQ_USER}
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS: ${UAT_MQ_PASSWORD}

  minio-uat:
    image: minio/minio:latest
    ports:
      - "9001:9000"
      - "9002:9001"
    environment:
      MINIO_ROOT_USER: ${UAT_MINIO_USER}
      MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD: ${UAT_MINIO_PASSWORD}
    command: server /data --console-address ':9001'
    volumes:
      - uat_minio_data:/data

  elasticsearch-uat:
    image: elasticsearch:8.11.0
    environment:
      - discovery.type=single-node
      - xpack.security.enabled=false
      - "ES_JAVA_OPTS=-Xms512m -Xmx512m"
    ports:
      - "9201:9200"
    volumes:
      - uat_es_data:/usr/share/elasticsearch/data

  app-gateway:
    image: harbor.tailor.is/tailor-is/gateway:${UAT_VERSION:-latest}
    ports:
      - "8081:8080"
    environment:
      SPRING_PROFILES_ACTIVE: uat
      NACOS_ADDR: nacos.uat.tailor.is:8848
    depends_on:
      - mysql-uat
      - redis-uat
      - rabbitmq-uat

volumes:
  uat_mysql_data:
  uat_redis_data:
  uat_minio_data:
  uat_es_data:
```

### 7.6.3 UAT验收标准

| 维度 | 标准 | 验证方法 | 一票否决 |
|------|------|---------|---------|
| **功能完整性** | 需求规格说明书100%覆盖 | 逐条对照验证 | 是 |
| **P0/P1用例** | 100%通过 | 自动化+手工测试 | 是 |
| **P2用例** | ≥95%通过 | 手工测试 | 否 |
| **阻塞性Bug** | 0个 | Bug追踪系统确认 | 是 |
| **性能指标** | P99≤500ms, QPS≥目标 | 性能测试报告 | 是 |
| **安全性** | 无Critical/High漏洞 | 安全扫描报告 | 是 |
| **兼容性** | 主流浏览器+移动端兼容 | E2E测试报告 | 否 |
| **用户体验** | NPS≥7分 | 用户满意度调查 | 否 |

## 7.7 测试数据管理

### 7.7.1 测试数据隔离策略

```java
// test-utils/src/main/java/com/tailoris/test/DataIsolationExtension.java
package com.tailoris.test;

import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.AfterEachCallback;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.BeforeEachCallback;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtensionContext;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.data.redis.core.StringRedisTemplate;
import org.springframework.jdbc.core.JdbcTemplate;
import org.springframework.test.context.junit.jupiter.SpringExtension;

public class DataIsolationExtension implements BeforeEachCallback, AfterEachCallback {

    @Autowired
    private JdbcTemplate jdbcTemplate;

    @Autowired
    private StringRedisTemplate redisTemplate;

    private static final ThreadLocal<String> TEST_CONTEXT = new ThreadLocal<>();

    @Override
    public void beforeEach(ExtensionContext context) {
        String testId = context.getRequiredTestMethod().getName()
                + "_" + System.currentTimeMillis();
        TEST_CONTEXT.set(testId);

        jdbcTemplate.execute("SET @test_context = '" + testId + "'");
    }

    @Override
    public void afterEach(ExtensionContext context) {
        cleanupTestData();
        cleanupCacheData();
        TEST_CONTEXT.remove();
    }

    private void cleanupTestData() {
        String[] tables = {
            "t_order", "t_order_item", "t_cart_item",
            "t_product", "t_user", "t_merchant"
        };

        for (String table : tables) {
            try {
                jdbcTemplate.execute(
                    "DELETE FROM " + table +
                    " WHERE created_by_test = '" + TEST_CONTEXT.get() + "'"
                );
            } catch (Exception e) {
                // 表可能不存在,忽略
            }
        }
    }

    private void cleanupCacheData() {
        try {
            redisTemplate.getConnectionFactory()
                    .getConnection()
                    .flushDb();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            // Redis未连接时忽略
        }
    }
}
```

### 7.7.2 Builder模式测试数据构建

```java
// test-utils/src/main/java/com/tailoris/test/builder/ProductBuilder.java
package com.tailoris.test.builder;

import com.tailoris.product.entity.Product;
import com.tailoris.product.enums.ProductStatus;

import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;

public class ProductBuilder {
    private Product product = new Product();

    public ProductBuilder() {
        product.setName("测试商品_" + System.currentTimeMillis());
        product.setPrice(new BigDecimal("99.00"));
        product.setOriginalPrice(new BigDecimal("199.00"));
        product.setStock(100);
        product.setStatus(ProductStatus.OFF_SALE);
        product.setSalesCount(0);
        product.setCreateTime(LocalDateTime.now());
        product.setUpdateTime(LocalDateTime.now());
        product.setCreatedByTest(true);
    }

    public static ProductBuilder aProduct() {
        return new ProductBuilder();
    }

    public ProductBuilder withId(Long id) {
        product.setId(id);
        return this;
    }

    public ProductBuilder withName(String name) {
        product.setName(name);
        return this;
    }

    public ProductBuilder withPrice(BigDecimal price) {
        product.setPrice(price);
        return this;
    }

    public ProductBuilder withOriginalPrice(BigDecimal originalPrice) {
        product.setOriginalPrice(originalPrice);
        return this;
    }

    public ProductBuilder withStock(int stock) {
        product.setStock(stock);
        return this;
    }

    public ProductBuilder withCategory(Long categoryId) {
        product.setCategoryId(categoryId);
        return this;
    }

    public ProductBuilder onSale() {
        product.setStatus(ProductStatus.ON_SALE);
        return this;
    }

    public ProductBuilder offSale() {
        product.setStatus(ProductStatus.OFF_SALE);
        return this;
    }

    public ProductBuilder withSales(int salesCount) {
        product.setSalesCount(salesCount);
        return this;
    }

    public Product build() {
        return product;
    }
}

// 使用示例
Product product = ProductBuilder.aProduct()
    .withName("2026新款韩版西装")
    .withPrice(new BigDecimal("1299.00"))
    .withStock(500)
    .withCategory(10L)
    .onSale()
    .withSales(128)
    .build();
```

### 7.7.3 敏感数据脱敏规则

```java
// test-utils/src/main/java/com/tailoris/test/mask/DataMaskingUtil.java
package com.tailoris.test.mask;

public class DataMaskingUtil {

    public static String maskPhone(String phone) {
        if (phone == null || phone.length() < 7) return phone;
        return phone.substring(0, 3) + "****" + phone.substring(phone.length() - 4);
    }

    public static String maskIdCard(String idCard) {
        if (idCard == null || idCard.length() < 10) return idCard;
        return idCard.substring(0, 6) + "********" + idCard.substring(idCard.length() - 4);
    }

    public static String maskBankCard(String cardNo) {
        if (cardNo == null || cardNo.length() < 8) return cardNo;
        return "**** **** **** " + cardNo.substring(cardNo.length() - 4);
    }

    public static String maskEmail(String email) {
        if (email == null || !email.contains("@")) return email;
        int atIndex = email.indexOf("@");
        if (atIndex <= 2) return "***" + email.substring(atIndex);
        return email.substring(0, 2) + "***" + email.substring(atIndex);
    }

    public static String maskName(String name) {
        if (name == null || name.length() <= 1) return name;
        if (name.length() == 2) return name.charAt(0) + "*";
        return name.charAt(0) + "*".repeat(name.length() - 1);
    }
}
```

### 7.7.4 测试数据管理Checklist

- [ ] **数据隔离**: 每个测试用例使用独立的测试数据集
- [ ] **自动清理**: @AfterEach/@AfterAll保证无残留数据
- [ ] **脱敏处理**: 测试环境禁止使用真实用户敏感信息
- [ ] **数据工厂**: Builder模式标准化测试对象构建
- [ ] **种子数据**: @Sql注解加载基础参考数据
- [ ] **数据一致性**: DB与缓存数据同步验证

## 7.8 测试报告与度量

### 7.8.1 JaCoCo覆盖率报告配置

```xml
<!-- pom.xml - JaCoCo详细报告配置 -->
<plugin>
    <groupId>org.jacoco</groupId>
    <artifactId>jacoco-maven-plugin</artifactId>
    <version>0.8.11</version>
    <configuration>
        <excludes>
            <!-- 排除配置类/实体类 -->
            <exclude>**/config/**</exclude>
            <exclude>**/entity/**</exclude>
            <exclude>**/dto/**</exclude>
            <exclude>**/enums/**</exclude>
            <exclude>**/constant/**</exclude>
            <!-- 排除自动生成的代码 -->
            <exclude>**/*Application*</exclude>
            <exclude>**/exception/**</exclude>
        </excludes>
    </configuration>
    <executions>
        <execution>
            <id>default-prepare-agent</id>
            <goals><goal>prepare-agent</goal></goals>
        </execution>
        <execution>
            <id>default-report</id>
            <phase>test</phase>
            <goals><goal>report</goal></goals>
            <configuration>
                <formats>XML,HTML,CSV</formats>
                <encoding>UTF-8</encoding>
            </configuration>
        </execution>
        <execution>
            <id>default-check</id>
            <goals><goal>check</goal></goals>
            <configuration>
                <rules>
                    <rule implementation="org.jacoco.maven.rule.Rule">
                        <element>BUNDLE</element>
                        <limits>
                            <limit implementation="org.jacoco.report.check.Limit">
                                <counter>INSTRUCTION</counter>
                                <value>COVEREDRATIO</value>
                                <minimum>0.900</minimum>
                            </limit>
                            <limit implementation="org.jacoco.report.check.Limit">
                                <counter>BRANCH</counter>
                                <value>COVEREDRATIO</value>
                                <minimum>0.850</minimum>
                            </limit>
                            <limit implementation="org.jacoco.report.check.Limit">
                                <counter>METHOD</counter>
                                <value>COVEREDRATIO</value>
                                <minimum>0.900</minimum>
                            </limit>
                            <limit implementation="org.jacoco.report.check.Limit">
                                <counter>LINE</counter>
                                <value>COVEREDRATIO</value>
                                <minimum>0.900</minimum>
                            </limit>
                            <limit implementation="org.jacoco.report.check.Limit">
                                <counter>CLASS</counter>
                                <value>COVEREDRATIO</value>
                                <minimum>0.950</minimum>
                            </limit>
                        </limits>
                    </rule>
                </rules>
            </configuration>
        </execution>
    </executions>
</plugin>
```
